[#psalms]
== The Psalms

*Psalms | Ψαλμοί | תהלים*

[#psalms-book-1%breakable]
=== BOOK I

[#psa001%breakable]
=== Psalm 1

[.outline.text-center]
_The happiness of the godly, 1-3. The unhappiness of the ungodly, 4-6._

1 Blessed is the man who does not walk in the counsel of the ungodly, [.linebr]#/# +
nor stands in the way of sinners, [.linebr]#/# +
nor sits in the seat of scoffers.

2 But his delight is in the law of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and on his law he meditates day and night.

3 And he shall be like a tree planted by the rivers of water [.linebr]#/# +
that brings forth its fruit in season, [.linebr]#/# +
and its leaf shall not wither. [.linebr]#/# +
And whatever he does shall prosper.

4 The ungodly are not so, [.linebr]#/# +
but are like the chaff which the wind drives away.

5 Therefore, the ungodly shall not stand in the judgment, [.linebr]#/# +
nor sinners in the congregation of the righteous.

6 For the LORD knows the way of the righteous. [.linebr]#/# +
But the way of the ungodly shall perish.

[#psa002%breakable]
=== Psalm 2

[.outline.text-center]
_The kingdom of Christ, 1-9. Kings are exhorted to accept it, 10-12._

[[psa002-001]]1 Why do the heathen rage [.linebr]#/# +
and the people plot a vain thing?

[[psa002-002]]2 The kings of the earth set themselves, [.linebr]#/# +
and the rulers take counsel together [.linebr]#/# +
against the LORD and against his anointed, saying,

3 "Let us break their bonds apart [.linebr]#/# +
and cast away their cords from us."

4 He who sits in the heavens shall laugh. [.linebr]#/# +
The Lord shall have them in derision.

5 Then he shall speak to them in his wrath [.linebr]#/# +
and trouble them in his sore displeasure.

6 "Yet I have set my king [.linebr]#/# +
upon my holy hill of Zion.

[[psa002-007]]7 I will declare the decree. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD has said to me, 'You are my Son. [.linebr]#/# +
This day I have begotten you.

[[psa002-008]]8 Ask of me, and I will give you the heathen for your inheritance [.linebr]#/# +
and the uttermost parts of the earth for your possession.

[[psa002-009]]9 You shall break them with a rod of iron. [.linebr]#/# +
You shall dash them in pieces like a potter's vessel.'"

10 Now therefore, be wise, O kings. [.linebr]#/# +
Be instructed, you judges of the earth.

11 Serve the LORD with fear [.linebr]#/# +
and rejoice with trembling.

12 Kiss the Son, lest he be angry, and you perish from the way, [.linebr]#/# +
for his wrath may soon be kindled. [.linebr]#/# +
Blessed are all those who put their trust in him.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.1]*: Quoted in xref:#act004-025[Acts 4:25]. *[v.2]*: Quoted in xref:#act004-026[Acts 4:26]. *[v.7]*: Quoted in xref:#act013-033[Acts 13:33]; xref:#heb001-005[Hebrews 1:5], xref:#heb005-005[5:5]. *[v.8]*: Quoted in xref:#rev002-026[Revelation 2:26]. *[v.9]*: Quoted in xref:#rev002-027[Revelation 2:27], xref:#rev012-005[12:5], xref:#rev019-015[19:15].

[#psa003%breakable]
=== Psalm 3

[.outline.text-center]
_The security of God's protection, 1-8._

1 [_A Psalm of David: when he fled from Absalom his son._]

LORD, how those who trouble me are multiplied! [.linebr]#/# +
Many are those who rise up against me.

2 There are many who say of my soul, [.linebr]#/# +
"There is no help for him in God." [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

3 But you, O LORD, are a shield for me, [.linebr]#/# +
my glory and the lifter up of my head.

4 I cried to the LORD with my voice, [.linebr]#/# +
and he heard me from his holy hill. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

5 I laid myself down and slept. [.linebr]#/# +
I awoke, for the LORD sustained me.

6 I will not be afraid of tens of thousands of people [.linebr]#/# +
who have set themselves against me on all sides.

7 Arise, O LORD. Save me, O my God. [.linebr]#/# +
For you have smitten all my enemies upon the cheek bone. [.linebr]#/# +
You have broken the teeth of the ungodly.

8 Salvation belongs to the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Your blessing is upon your people. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

[#psa004%breakable]
=== Psalm 4

[.outline.text-center]
_David prays for audience, 1. He reproves and exhorts his enemies, 2-5. Man's happiness is in God's favor, 6-8._

1 [_To the Chief Musician on Neginoth. A Psalm of David._]

Hear me when I call, O God of my righteousness. [.linebr]#/# +
You have enlarged me when I was in distress. [.linebr]#/# +
Have mercy upon me and hear my prayer.

2 O sons of men, how long will you turn my glory into shame? [.linebr]#/# +
How long will you love vanity and seek after falsehood? [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

3 But know that the LORD has set apart him who is godly for himself. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD will hear when I call to him.

[[psa004-004]]4 Stand in awe and do not sin. [.linebr]#/# +
Speak with your own heart upon your bed and be still. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

5 Offer the sacrifices of righteousness [.linebr]#/# +
and put your trust in the LORD.

6 There are many who say, "Who will show us any good?" [.linebr]#/# +
LORD, lift upon us the light of your countenance.

7 You have put gladness in my heart, [.linebr]#/# +
more than in the time when their grain and their wine increased.

8 I will both lay myself down in peace and sleep, [.linebr]#/# +
for you only, LORD, make me dwell in safety.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.4]*: Quoted in xref:#eph004-026[Ephesians 4:26].

[#psa005%breakable]
=== Psalm 5

[.outline.text-center]
_David prays and professes his diligence in prayer, 1-3. God does not favor the wicked, 4-6. David, professing his faith, prays to God to guide him, 7-9; to destroy his enemies, 10; and to preserve the godly, 11, 12._

1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Nehiloth. A Psalm of David._]

Give ear to my words, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Consider my meditation.

2 Listen to the voice of my cry, my King and my God. [.linebr]#/# +
For to you I will pray.

3 My voice you shall hear in the morning, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
In the morning I will direct my prayer to you and will look up.

4 For you are not a God who has pleasure in wickedness, [.linebr]#/# +
neither shall evil dwell with you.

5 The foolish shall not stand in your sight. [.linebr]#/# +
You hate all workers of iniquity.

6 You shall destroy those who speak falsehood. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD will abhor the bloody and deceitful man.

7 But as for me, I will come into your house [.linebr]#/# +
in the multitude of your mercy, [.linebr]#/# +
and in your fear I will worship [.linebr]#/# +
toward your holy temple.

8 Lead me, O LORD, in your righteousness because of my enemies. [.linebr]#/# +
Make your way straight before my face.

[[psa005-009]]9 For there is no faithfulness in their mouth. [.linebr]#/# +
Their inward part is wickedness. [.linebr]#/# +
Their throat is an open sepulcher. [.linebr]#/# +
They flatter with their tongue.

10 Destroy them, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them fall by their own counsels. [.linebr]#/# +
Cast them out in the multitude of their transgressions. [.linebr]#/# +
For they have rebelled against you.

11 But let all those who put their trust in you rejoice. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them always shout for joy because you defend them. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them also who love your name be joyful in you.

12 For you, LORD, will bless the righteous. [.linebr]#/# +
With favor you will compass him as with a shield.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.9]*: Quoted in xref:#rom003-013[Romans 3:13].

[#psa006%breakable]
=== Psalm 6

[.outline.text-center]
_David's complaint in his sickness, 1-7. He triumphs over his enemies, 8-10._

1 [_To the Chief Musician on Neginoth upon Sheminith. A Psalm of David._]

O LORD, do not rebuke me in your anger, [.linebr]#/# +
neither chasten me in your hot displeasure.

2 Have mercy upon me, O LORD, for I am weak. [.linebr]#/# +
O LORD, heal me, for my bones are agitated.

[[psa006-003]]3 My soul is also greatly disquieted. [.linebr]#/# +
But you, O LORD, how long?

4 Return, O LORD, deliver my soul. [.linebr]#/# +
Oh save me for your mercy's sake.

5 For in death there is no remembrance of you. [.linebr]#/# +
In the grave, who will give you thanks?

6 I am weary with my groaning. [.linebr]#/# +
All the night I make my bed to swim. [.linebr]#/# +
I water my couch with my tears.

7 My eye is consumed because of grief. [.linebr]#/# +
It grows old because of all my enemies.

[[psa006-008]]8 Depart from me, all you workers of iniquity, [.linebr]#/# +
for the LORD has heard the voice of my weeping.

9 The LORD has heard my supplication. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD will receive my prayer.

10 Let all my enemies be ashamed and greatly disquieted. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them return and be suddenly ashamed.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.3]*: Quoted in xref:#jhn012-027[John 12:27] *[v.8]*: Quoted in xref:#mth007-023[Matthew 7:23]; xref:#luk013-027[Luke 13:27].

[#psa007%breakable]
=== Psalm 7

[.outline.text-center]
_David prays against the malice of his enemies, professing his innocence, 1-9. By faith he sees his defense and the destruction of his enemies, 10-17._

[[psa007-001]]1 [_Shiggaion of David: which he sang to the LORD concerning the words of Cush the Benjaminite._]

O LORD my God, I put my trust in you. [.linebr]#/# +
Save me from all those who persecute me, and deliver me,

2 Lest he tear my soul like a lion, [.linebr]#/# +
rending it in pieces, while there is no one to deliver.

3 O LORD my God, if I have done this, [.linebr]#/# +
if there is iniquity in my hands,

4 If I have rewarded evil to him who was at peace with me [.linebr]#/# +
(I have even delivered him who without cause is my enemy),

5 Let the enemy persecute my soul and take it. [.linebr]#/# +
Let him even tread down my life upon the earth [.linebr]#/# +
and lay my honor in the dust. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

6 Arise, O LORD, in your anger, [.linebr]#/# +
lift up yourself because of the rage of my enemies, [.linebr]#/# +
and awake for me to the judgment that you have commanded.

7 And the congregation of the people shall encompass you. [.linebr]#/# +
For their sakes therefore return on high.

8 The LORD shall judge the people. [.linebr]#/# +
Judge me, O LORD, according to my righteousness [.linebr]#/# +
and according to my integrity that is in me.

9 Oh let the wickedness of the wicked come to an end, [.linebr]#/# +
but establish the just, [.linebr]#/# +
for the righteous God tries the hearts and minds.

10 My defense is from God, [.linebr]#/# +
who saves the upright in heart.

11 God judges the righteous, [.linebr]#/# +
and God is angry with the wicked every day.

12 If he does not turn, he will whet his sword. [.linebr]#/# +
He has bent his bow and made it ready.

13 He has also prepared for him the instruments of death. [.linebr]#/# +
He ordains his arrows against the persecutors.

14 Behold, he travails with iniquity, [.linebr]#/# +
has conceived mischief, and brought forth falsehood.

15 He made a pit, dug it, [.linebr]#/# +
and has fallen into the ditch which he made.

16 His mischief shall return upon his own head, [.linebr]#/# +
and his violent dealing shall come down upon the crown of his own head.

17 I will praise the LORD according to his righteousness [.linebr]#/# +
and sing praise to the name of the LORD most high.

[#psa008%breakable]
=== Psalm 8

[.outline.text-center]
_God's glory is magnified by his works and by his love to man, 1-9._

1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Gittith. A Psalm of David._]

O Yahweh our Lord, [.linebr]#/# +
how excellent your name is in all the earth! [.linebr]#/# +
You have set your glory above the heavens.

[[psa008-002]]2 Out of the mouth of babies and infants you have ordained strength [.linebr]#/# +
because of your enemies, [.linebr]#/# +
so that you might still the enemy and the avenger.

3 When I consider your heavens, the work of your fingers, [.linebr]#/# +
the moon and the stars, which you have ordained,

[[psa008-004]]4 What is man that you are mindful of him, [.linebr]#/# +
and the son of man that you visit him?

[[psa008-005]]5 For you have made him a little lower than the angels [.linebr]#/# +
and have crowned him with glory and honor.

[[psa008-006]]6 You have made him to have dominion over the works of your hands. [.linebr]#/# +
You have put all things under his feet:

7 All sheep and oxen [.linebr]#/# +
and even the beasts of the field,

8 The birds of the air, the fish of the sea, [.linebr]#/# +
and whatever passes through the paths of the seas.

9 O Yahweh our Lord, [.linebr]#/# +
how excellent your name is in all the earth!

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.2]*: Quoted in xref:#mth021-016[Matthew 21:16]. *[v.4]*: Quoted in xref:#heb002-006[Hebrews 2:6]. *[v.5]*: Quoted in xref:#heb002-007[Hebrews 2:7]. *[v.6]*: Quoted in xref:#fco015-027[1st Corinthians 15:27]; xref:#heb002-007[Hebrews 2:7-8].

[#psa009%breakable]
=== Psalm 9

[.outline.text-center]
_David praises God for executing judgment, 1-10. He incites others to praise him, 11, 12. He prays that he may have cause to praise him, 13-20._

1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Muthlabben. A Psalm of David._]

I will praise you, O LORD, with my whole heart. [.linebr]#/# +
I will show forth all your wonderful works.

2 I will be glad and rejoice in you. [.linebr]#/# +
I will sing praise to your name, O most High.

3 When my enemies are turned back, [.linebr]#/# +
they shall fall and perish at your presence.

4 For you have maintained my right and my cause. [.linebr]#/# +
You sat on the throne judging right.

5 You have rebuked the heathen, [.linebr]#/# +
you have destroyed the wicked, [.linebr]#/# +
you have blotted out their name forever and ever.

6 O enemy, destructions have come to a perpetual end, [.linebr]#/# +
and you have destroyed cities. [.linebr]#/# +
Their memorial has perished with them.

7 But the LORD shall endure forever. [.linebr]#/# +
He has prepared his throne for judgment.

8 And he shall judge the world in righteousness. [.linebr]#/# +
He shall minister judgment to the people in uprightness.

9 The LORD will also be a refuge for the oppressed, [.linebr]#/# +
a refuge in times of trouble.

10 And those who know your name will put their trust in you, [.linebr]#/# +
for you, LORD, have not forsaken those who seek you.

11 Sing praises to the LORD who dwells in Zion. [.linebr]#/# +
Declare among the people his doings.

12 For he who avenges blood remembers them. [.linebr]#/# +
He does not forget the cry of the humble.

13 Have mercy upon me, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Consider my trouble which I suffer from those who hate me, [.linebr]#/# +
and lift me up from the gates of death

14 So that I may show forth all your praise [.linebr]#/# +
in the gates of the daughter of Zion. [.linebr]#/# +
I will rejoice in your salvation.

15 The heathen are sunk down in the pit that they made. [.linebr]#/# +
In the net which they hid, their own foot is taken.

16 The LORD is known by the judgment which he executes. [.linebr]#/# +
The wicked is snared in the work of his own hands. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Higgaion. Selah._ +]+

17 The wicked shall be turned into hell— [.linebr]#/# +
all the nations who forget God.

18 For the needy shall not always be forgotten. [.linebr]#/# +
The expectation of the poor shall not perish forever.

19 Arise, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not let man prevail. [.linebr]#/# +
Let the heathen be judged in your sight.

20 Put them in fear, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
so that the nations may know themselves to be only men. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

[#psa010%breakable]
=== Psalm 10

[.outline.text-center]
_David accuses the wicked, 1-11. He prays for remedy, 12-15. He professes his confidence, 16-18._

1 Why do you stand afar off, O LORD? [.linebr]#/# +
Why do you hide yourself in times of trouble?

2 The wicked in his pride persecutes the poor. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them be taken in the devices that they have conceived.

3 For the wicked boasts about his heart's desire [.linebr]#/# +
and blesses the covetous, whom the LORD abhors.

4 The wicked, through the pride of his countenance, [.linebr]#/# +
will not seek after God. [.linebr]#/# +
God is not in all his thoughts.

5 His ways are always grievous. [.linebr]#/# +
Your judgments are far above out of his sight. [.linebr]#/# +
As for all his enemies, he puffs at them.

6 He has said in his heart, "I shall not be moved, [.linebr]#/# +
for I shall never be in adversity."

[[psa010-007]]7 His mouth is full of cursing and deceit and fraud. [.linebr]#/# +
Under his tongue is mischief and vanity.

8 He sits in the lurking places of the villages. [.linebr]#/# +
In the secret places he murders the innocent. [.linebr]#/# +
His eyes are secretly set against the poor.

9 He lies in wait secretly like a lion in his den. [.linebr]#/# +
He lies in wait to catch the poor. [.linebr]#/# +
He catches the poor when he draws him into his net.

10 He crouches and humbles himself [.linebr]#/# +
so that the poor may fall by his strong ones.

11 He has said in his heart, "God has forgotten. [.linebr]#/# +
He hides his face. He will never see it."

12 Arise, O LORD. O God, lift up your hand. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not forget the humble.

13 Why does the wicked despise God? [.linebr]#/# +
He has said in his heart, "You will not require it."

14 You have seen it, [.linebr]#/# +
for you behold mischief and spite to requite it with your hand. [.linebr]#/# +
The poor commits himself to you. [.linebr]#/# +
You are the helper of the fatherless.

15 Break the arm of the wicked and the evil man. [.linebr]#/# +
Seek out his wickedness until you find none.

16 The LORD is King forever and ever. [.linebr]#/# +
The heathen have perished out of his land.

17 LORD, you have heard the desire of the humble. [.linebr]#/# +
You will prepare their heart. [.linebr]#/# +
You will cause your ear to hear,

18 Doing justice for the fatherless and the oppressed [.linebr]#/# +
so that the man of the earth may no longer oppress.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.7]*: Quoted in xref:#rom003-014[Romans 3:14].

[#psa011%breakable]
=== Psalm 11

[.outline.text-center]
_David encourages himself in God against his enemies, 1-3. The providence and justice of God, 4-7._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

I put my trust in the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
How can you say to my soul, [.linebr]#/# +
"Flee like a bird to your mountain"?

2 For behold, the wicked bend their bow. [.linebr]#/# +
They make ready their arrow upon the string [.linebr]#/# +
so that they may secretly shoot at the upright in heart.

3 If the foundations are destroyed, [.linebr]#/# +
what can the righteous do?

4 The LORD is in his holy temple. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD'S throne is in heaven. [.linebr]#/# +
His eyes behold. His eyelids try the children of men.

5 The LORD tries the righteous, [.linebr]#/# +
but the wicked and him who loves violence his soul hates.

6 Upon the wicked he shall rain snares, [.linebr]#/# +
fire and brimstone, and a horrible tempest. [.linebr]#/# +
This shall be the portion of their cup.

7 For Yahweh is righteous. [.linebr]#/# +
He loves righteousness. [.linebr]#/# +
His countenance beholds the upright.

[#psa012%breakable]
=== Psalm 12

[.outline.text-center]
_David, destitute of human comfort, craves help from God, 1, 2. He comforts himself with God's promises and judgments on the wicked, 3-8._

1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Sheminith. A Psalm of David._]

Help, LORD, for the godly man ceases, [.linebr]#/# +
for the faithful fail from among the children of men.

2 They each speak vanity with his neighbor. [.linebr]#/# +
With flattering lips and with a double heart they speak.

3 The LORD shall cut off all flattering lips [.linebr]#/# +
and the tongue that speaks proud things,

4 Who have said, "With our tongue we will prevail. [.linebr]#/# +
Our lips are our own. Who is lord over us?"

5 "For the oppression of the poor, for the sighing of the needy, [.linebr]#/# +
now I will arise," says the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
"I will set him in safety from him who puffs at him."

6 The words of the LORD are pure words, [.linebr]#/# +
like silver tried in a furnace of earth, [.linebr]#/# +
purified seven times.

7 You shall keep them, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
you shall preserve them from this generation forever.

8 The wicked walk on every side [.linebr]#/# +
when the vilest men are exalted.

[#psa013%breakable]
=== Psalm 13

[.outline.text-center]
_David bemoans delay, 1, 2. He prays for preventing grace, 3, 4. He boasts of divine mercy, 5, 6._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

How long will you forget me, O LORD? Forever? [.linebr]#/# +
How long will you hide your face from me?

2 How long shall I take counsel in my soul, [.linebr]#/# +
having sorrow in my heart daily? [.linebr]#/# +
How long shall my enemy be exalted over me?

3 Consider and hear me, O LORD my God. [.linebr]#/# +
Lighten my eyes, lest I sleep the sleep of death,

4 Lest my enemy say, "I have prevailed against him." [.linebr]#/# +
And those who trouble me rejoice when I am moved.

5 But I have trusted in your mercy. [.linebr]#/# +
My heart shall rejoice in your salvation.

6 I will sing to the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
because he has dealt bountifully with me.

[#psa014%breakable]
=== Psalm 14

[.outline.text-center]
_David describes a natural man, 1-3. He convinces the wicked by the light of their conscience, 4-6. He glories in the salvation of God, 7._

[[psa014-001]]1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

The fool has said in his heart, "There is no God." [.linebr]#/# +
They are corrupt. They have done abominable works. [.linebr]#/# +
There is no one who does good.

2 The LORD looked down from heaven upon the children of men [.linebr]#/# +
to see if there were any who understood and sought God.

3 They have all gone aside. [.linebr]#/# +
They have all together become filthy. [.linebr]#/# +
There is no one who does good, not even one.

4 Have all the workers of iniquity no knowledge, [.linebr]#/# +
who eat up my people like they eat bread [.linebr]#/# +
and do not call upon the LORD?

5 There they were in great fear, [.linebr]#/# +
for God is in the generation of the righteous.

6 You have shamed the counsel of the poor [.linebr]#/# +
because the LORD is his refuge.

7 Oh that the salvation of Israel would come out of Zion! [.linebr]#/# +
When the LORD brings back the captivity of his people, [.linebr]#/# +
Jacob shall rejoice and Israel shall be glad.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.1]*: Reference, xref:#rom003-010[Romans 3:10].

[#psa015%breakable]
=== Psalm 15

[.outline.text-center]
_David describes a citizen of Zion, 1-5._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

LORD, who shall abide in your tabernacle? [.linebr]#/# +
Who shall dwell on your holy hill?

2 He who walks uprightly, works righteousness, [.linebr]#/# +
and speaks the truth in his heart;

3 He who does not backbite with his tongue, [.linebr]#/# +
nor does evil to his neighbor, [.linebr]#/# +
nor takes up a reproach against his neighbor;

4 In whose eyes a vile person is despised, [.linebr]#/# +
but he honors those who fear the LORD; [.linebr]#/# +
he who swears to his own hurt and does not change;

5 He who does not put out his money to usury, [.linebr]#/# +
nor takes reward against the innocent. [.linebr]#/# +
He who does these things shall never be moved.

[#psa016%breakable]
=== Psalm 16

[.outline.text-center]
_David, in distrust of merits and hatred of idolatry, flees to God for preservation, 1-4. He shows the hope of his calling, of the resurrection, and life everlasting, 5-11._

1 [_Michtam of David._]

Preserve me, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
for I put my trust in you.

2 O my soul, you have said to the LORD, "You are my Lord. [.linebr]#/# +
My goodness does not extend to you."

3 But to the saints who are in the earth, [.linebr]#/# +
and to the excellent, [.linebr]#/# +
all my delight is in them.

4 Their sorrows shall be multiplied [.linebr]#/# +
who hasten after another god. [.linebr]#/# +
Their drink-offerings of blood I will not offer, [.linebr]#/# +
nor take their names into my lips.

5 The LORD is the portion of my inheritance and of my cup. [.linebr]#/# +
You maintain my lot.

6 The lines have fallen to me in pleasant places. [.linebr]#/# +
Indeed, I have a beautiful heritage.

7 I will bless the LORD who has given me counsel. [.linebr]#/# +
My heart also instructs me in the night season.

[[psa016-008]]8 I have set the LORD always before me. [.linebr]#/# +
Because he is at my right hand, I shall not be moved.

[[psa016-009]]9 Therefore, my heart is glad and my glory rejoices. [.linebr]#/# +
My flesh shall also rest in hope.

[[psa016-010]]10 For you will not leave my soul in hell, [.linebr]#/# +
neither will you allow your Holy One to see corruption.

[[psa016-011]]11 You will show me the path of life. [.linebr]#/# +
In your presence is fullness of joy. [.linebr]#/# +
At your right hand are pleasures forevermore.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.8]*: Quoted in xref:#act002-025[Acts 2:25]. *[v.9]*: Quoted in xref:#act002-026[Acts 2:26]. *[v.10]*: Quoted in xref:#act002-027[Acts 2:27], xref:#act013-035[13:35]. *[v.11]*: Quoted in xref:#act002-028[Acts 2:28].

[#psa017%breakable]
=== Psalm 17

[.outline.text-center]
_David, in confidence of his integrity, craves defense from God against his enemies, 1-9. He shows their pride, craft, and eagerness, 10-12. He prays against them in confidence of his hope, 13-15._

1 [_A Prayer of David._]

Hear the right, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Attend to my cry. [.linebr]#/# +
Give ear to my prayer, [.linebr]#/# +
which does not go out of feigned lips.

2 Let my sentence come forth from your presence. [.linebr]#/# +
Let your eyes behold the things that are equal.

3 You have proved my heart. [.linebr]#/# +
You have visited me in the night. [.linebr]#/# +
You have tried me and shall find nothing. [.linebr]#/# +
I have purposed that my mouth shall not transgress.

4 Concerning the works of men, [.linebr]#/# +
by the word of your lips [.linebr]#/# +
I have kept myself from the paths of the destroyer.

5 Uphold my goings in your paths [.linebr]#/# +
so that my footsteps do not slip.

6 I have called upon you, for you will hear me, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
Incline your ear to me and hear my speech.

7 Show your wonderful loving-kindness, [.linebr]#/# +
O you who save by your right hand [.linebr]#/# +
those who put their trust in you [.linebr]#/# +
from those who rise up against them.

8 Keep me as the apple of your eye. [.linebr]#/# +
Hide me under the shadow of your wings

9 From the wicked who oppress me, [.linebr]#/# +
from my deadly enemies who encompass me.

10 They are enclosed in their own fat. [.linebr]#/# +
They speak proudly with their mouth.

11 They have now compassed us in our steps. [.linebr]#/# +
They have set their eyes bowing down to the earth,

12 Like a lion that is greedy of his prey, [.linebr]#/# +
like a young lion lurking in secret places.

13 Arise, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Disappoint him. Cast him down. [.linebr]#/# +
Deliver my soul from the wicked by your sword,

14 From men who are your hand, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
from men of the world who have their portion in this life [.linebr]#/# +
and whose belly you fill with your hidden treasure. [.linebr]#/# +
They are full of children [.linebr]#/# +
and leave the rest of their substance to their babies.

15 As for me, I shall behold your face in righteousness. [.linebr]#/# +
I shall be satisfied with your likeness when I awake.

[#psa018%breakable]
=== Psalm 18

[.outline.text-center]
_David praises God for his manifold and marvelous blessings, 1-50._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David the Servant of the LORD: who spoke the words of this song to the LORD in the day that the LORD delivered him from the hand of all his enemies and from the hand of Saul. He said,_]

I will love you, O LORD, my strength.

2 The LORD is my rock, my fortress, and my deliverer, [.linebr]#/# +
my God, my strength in whom I will trust, [.linebr]#/# +
my buckler, the horn of my salvation, and my high tower.

3 I will call upon the LORD who is worthy to be praised. [.linebr]#/# +
So I shall be saved from my enemies.

4 The sorrows of death compassed me, [.linebr]#/# +
and the floods of ungodly men made me afraid.

5 The sorrows of hell encompassed me. [.linebr]#/# +
The snares of death seized me.

6 In my distress I called upon the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
and cried to my God. [.linebr]#/# +
He heard my voice out of his temple, [.linebr]#/# +
and my cry came before him, even into his ears.

7 Then the earth shook and trembled, [.linebr]#/# +
and also the foundations of the hills moved [.linebr]#/# +
and were shaken, because he was angry.

8 There went up a smoke out of his nostrils, [.linebr]#/# +
and fire out of his mouth devoured. [.linebr]#/# +
Coals were kindled by it.

9 He also bowed the heavens and came down, [.linebr]#/# +
and darkness was under his feet.

10 And he rode upon a cherub and flew. [.linebr]#/# +
He even flew upon the wings of the wind.

11 He made darkness his secret place, his pavilion around him, [.linebr]#/# +
dark waters and thick clouds of the skies.

12 At the brightness that was before him his thick clouds passed [.linebr]#/# +
with hail stones and coals of fire.

13 The LORD also thundered in the heavens, [.linebr]#/# +
and the Highest gave his voice [.linebr]#/# +
with hail stones and coals of fire.

14 He even sent out his arrows and scattered them, [.linebr]#/# +
and he shot out lightnings and completely defeated them.

15 Then the channels of waters were seen [.linebr]#/# +
and the foundations of the world were uncovered [.linebr]#/# +
at your rebuke, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
at the blast of the breath of your nostrils.

16 He sent from above, he took me, [.linebr]#/# +
he drew me out of many waters.

17 He delivered me from my strong enemy [.linebr]#/# +
and from those who hated me, for they were too strong for me.

18 They attacked me in the day of my calamity, [.linebr]#/# +
but the LORD was my stay.

19 He also brought me forth in a large place. [.linebr]#/# +
He delivered me because he delighted in me.

20 The LORD rewarded me [.linebr]#/# +
according to my righteousness. [.linebr]#/# +
According to the cleanness of my hands [.linebr]#/# +
he has recompensed me.

21 For I have kept the ways of the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
and have not wickedly departed from my God.

22 For all his judgments were before me, [.linebr]#/# +
and I did not put away his statutes from me.

23 I was also upright before him [.linebr]#/# +
and I kept myself from my iniquity.

24 Therefore, the LORD has recompensed me [.linebr]#/# +
according to my righteousness, [.linebr]#/# +
according to the cleanness of my hands in his sight.

25 With the merciful you will show yourself merciful. [.linebr]#/# +
With an upright man you will show yourself upright.

26 With the pure you will show yourself pure. [.linebr]#/# +
With the perverse you will contend.

27 For you will save the afflicted people, [.linebr]#/# +
but will bring down high looks.

28 For you will light my candle. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD my God will enlighten my darkness.

29 For by you I have run through a troop. [.linebr]#/# +
And by my God I have leaped over a wall.

30 As for God, his way is perfect. [.linebr]#/# +
The word of the LORD is tried. [.linebr]#/# +
He is a buckler to all those who trust in him.

31 For who is God except the LORD? [.linebr]#/# +
Or who is a rock except our God?

32 It is God who girds me with strength [.linebr]#/# +
and makes my way perfect.

33 He makes my feet like those of a doe [.linebr]#/# +
and sets me upon my high places.

34 He teaches my hands to war [.linebr]#/# +
so that a bow of steel is broken by my arms.

35 You have also given me the shield of your salvation. [.linebr]#/# +
Your right hand has held me up, [.linebr]#/# +
and your gentleness has made me great.

36 You have enlarged my steps under me, [.linebr]#/# +
and my feet have not slipped.

37 I have pursued my enemies and overtaken them, [.linebr]#/# +
neither did I turn back until they were consumed.

38 I have wounded them so that they were not able to rise. [.linebr]#/# +
They have fallen under my feet.

39 For you have girded me with strength to battle. [.linebr]#/# +
You have subdued under me those who rose up against me.

40 You have also given me the necks of my enemies [.linebr]#/# +
so that I might destroy those who hate me.

41 They cried, but there was no one to save them, [.linebr]#/# +
even to the LORD, but he did not answer them.

42 Then I beat them as small as the dust before the wind. [.linebr]#/# +
I cast them out like the dirt in the streets.

43 You have delivered me from the strivings of the people [.linebr]#/# +
and you have made me the head of the heathen. [.linebr]#/# +
A people whom I have not known shall serve me.

44 As soon as they hear of me, they shall obey me. [.linebr]#/# +
The strangers shall submit themselves to me.

45 The strangers shall fade away [.linebr]#/# +
and be afraid from their strongholds.

46 The LORD lives. Blessed be my rock. [.linebr]#/# +
Let the God of my salvation be exalted.

47 It is God who avenges me [.linebr]#/# +
and subdues the people under me.

48 He delivers me from my enemies. [.linebr]#/# +
You even lift me up above those who rise up against me. [.linebr]#/# +
You have delivered me from the violent man.

[[psa018-049]]49 Therefore, I will give thanks to you, O LORD, among the heathen [.linebr]#/# +
and sing praises to your name.

50 He gives great deliverance to his king [.linebr]#/# +
and shows mercy to his anointed, [.linebr]#/# +
to David, and to his offspring forever.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.49]*: Quoted in xref:#rom015-009[Romans 15:9].

[#psa019%breakable]
=== Psalm 19

[.outline.text-center]
_The creatures show God's glory, 1-6. The excellency of the divine law, 7-12. David prays for grace, 12-14._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

The heavens declare the glory of God, [.linebr]#/# +
and the firmament shows the work of his hands.

2 Day to day utters speech, [.linebr]#/# +
and night to night shows knowledge.

3 There is no speech nor language [.linebr]#/# +
where their voice is not heard.

[[psa019-004]]4 Their line has gone out through all the earth, [.linebr]#/# +
and their words to the end of the world. [.linebr]#/# +
In them he has set a tabernacle for the sun.

5 It is like a bridegroom coming out of his chamber. [.linebr]#/# +
It rejoices like a strong man running a race.

6 Its going forth is from the end of the heaven, [.linebr]#/# +
and its circuit to the ends of it, [.linebr]#/# +
and there is nothing hid from its heat.

7 The law of the LORD is perfect, [.linebr]#/# +
converting the soul. [.linebr]#/# +
The testimony of the LORD is sure, [.linebr]#/# +
making the simple wise.

8 The statutes of the LORD are right, [.linebr]#/# +
rejoicing the heart. [.linebr]#/# +
The commandment of the LORD is pure, [.linebr]#/# +
enlightening the eyes.

[[psa019-009]]9 The fear of the LORD is clean, [.linebr]#/# +
enduring forever. [.linebr]#/# +
The judgments of the LORD are true, [.linebr]#/# +
being altogether righteous.

10 They are to be more desired than gold, [.linebr]#/# +
even much fine gold, [.linebr]#/# +
and also sweeter than honey [.linebr]#/# +
and the honey-comb.

11 Moreover, by them your servant is warned, [.linebr]#/# +
and in keeping them there is great reward.

12 Who can understand his errors? [.linebr]#/# +
Cleanse me from secret faults.

13 Keep back your servant also from presumptuous sins. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not let them have dominion over me. [.linebr]#/# +
Then I shall be upright [.linebr]#/# +
and be innocent from the great transgression.

14 Let the words of my mouth [.linebr]#/# +
and the meditation of my heart [.linebr]#/# +
be acceptable in your sight, [.linebr]#/# +
O LORD, my strength and my redeemer.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.4]*: Quoted in xref:#rom010-018[Romans 10:18]. *[v.9]*: Quoted in xref:#rev019-002[Revelation 19:2].

[#psa020%breakable]
=== Psalm 20

[.outline.text-center]
_The church blesses the king in his exploits, 1-6; and expresses her confidence in God's aid, 7-9._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

May the LORD hear you in the day of trouble. [.linebr]#/# +
May the name of the God of Jacob defend you,

2 Send you help from the sanctuary, [.linebr]#/# +
strengthen you out of Zion,

3 Remember all your offerings, [.linebr]#/# +
and accept your burnt-sacrifice. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

4 May he grant you according to your own heart [.linebr]#/# +
and fulfill all your counsel.

5 We will rejoice in your salvation, [.linebr]#/# +
and in the name of our God we will set up our banners. [.linebr]#/# +
May the LORD fulfill all your petitions.

6 Now I know that the LORD saves his anointed. [.linebr]#/# +
He will hear him from his holy heaven [.linebr]#/# +
with the saving strength of his right hand.

7 Some trust in chariots and some in horses, [.linebr]#/# +
but we will remember the name of the LORD our God.

8 They are brought down and fallen, [.linebr]#/# +
but we are raised and stand upright.

9 Save, LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Let the king hear us when we call.

[#psa021%breakable]
=== Psalm 21

[.outline.text-center]
_A thanksgiving for victory, 1-6; with confidence of further success, 7-13._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

The king shall rejoice in your strength, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
And in your salvation how greatly he shall rejoice!

2 You have given him his heart's desire [.linebr]#/# +
and have not withheld the request of his lips. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

3 For you have met him with the blessings of goodness. [.linebr]#/# +
You have set a crown of pure gold on his head.

4 He asked life of you, and you gave it to him, [.linebr]#/# +
even length of days forever and ever.

5 His glory is great in your salvation. [.linebr]#/# +
Honor and majesty you have laid upon him.

6 For you have made him most blessed forever. [.linebr]#/# +
You have made him exceedingly glad with your countenance.

7 For the king trusts in the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and through the mercy of the most High he shall not be moved.

8 Your hand shall find out all your enemies. [.linebr]#/# +
Your right hand shall find out those who hate you.

9 You shall put them into a fiery oven in the time of your anger. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD shall swallow them up in his wrath, [.linebr]#/# +
and the fire shall devour them.

10 You shall destroy their fruit from the earth [.linebr]#/# +
and their offspring from among the children of men.

11 For they intended evil against you. [.linebr]#/# +
They conceived a mischievous device which they are not able to perform.

12 Therefore, you shall make them turn their back [.linebr]#/# +
when you make ready your arrows upon your strings against their face.

13 Be exalted, LORD, in your own strength, [.linebr]#/# +
and we will sing and praise your power.

[#psa022%breakable]
=== Psalm 22

[.outline.text-center]
_David complains in great discouragement, 1-8. He prays in great distress, 9-22. He praises God, 23-31._

[[psa022-001]]1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Aijeleth Shahar. A Psalm of David._]

My God, my God, why have you forsaken me? [.linebr]#/# +
Why are you so far from helping me [.linebr]#/# +
and from the words of my roaring?

2 O my God, I cry in the day-time, but you do not hear, [.linebr]#/# +
and in the night season, and I am not silent.

3 But you are holy, [.linebr]#/# +
O you who inhabit the praises of Israel.

4 Our fathers trusted in you. [.linebr]#/# +
They trusted, and you delivered them.

5 They cried to you and were delivered. [.linebr]#/# +
They trusted in you and were not confounded.

6 But I am a worm and no man, [.linebr]#/# +
a reproach of men and despised by the people.

7 All those who see me deride me. [.linebr]#/# +
They shoot out the lip and shake the head, saying,

[[psa022-008]]8 "He trusted in the LORD that he would deliver him. [.linebr]#/# +
Let him deliver him, seeing he delighted in him."

9 But you are he who brought me forth into life. [.linebr]#/# +
You made me hope when I was upon my mother's breasts.

10 I was cast upon you from my birth. [.linebr]#/# +
You are my God from the time I was born.

11 Do not be far from me, for trouble is near. [.linebr]#/# +
For there is no one to help.

12 Many bulls have surrounded me. [.linebr]#/# +
Strong bulls of Bashan have compassed me.

13 They gaped upon me with their mouths [.linebr]#/# +
like a ravening and a roaring lion.

14 I am poured out like water, [.linebr]#/# +
and all my bones are out of joint. [.linebr]#/# +
My heart is like wax. [.linebr]#/# +
It is melted in the midst of my body.

15 My strength is dried up like a potsherd, [.linebr]#/# +
and my tongue cleaves to my jaws. [.linebr]#/# +
And you have brought me into the dust of death.

16 For dogs have compassed me. [.linebr]#/# +
The assembly of the wicked have enclosed me. [.linebr]#/# +
They pierced my hands and my feet.

17 I may number all my bones. [.linebr]#/# +
They look and stare upon me.

[[psa022-018]]18 They part my garments among them [.linebr]#/# +
and cast lots upon my vesture.

19 But do not be far from me, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
O my strength, hasten to help me.

20 Deliver my soul from the sword, [.linebr]#/# +
my darling from the power of the dog.

21 Save me from the lion's mouth, [.linebr]#/# +
for you have heard me from the horns of the wild oxen.

[[psa022-022]]22 I will declare your name to my brothers. [.linebr]#/# +
In the midst of the congregation I will praise you.

23 You who fear the LORD, praise him. [.linebr]#/# +
All you offspring of Jacob, glorify him. [.linebr]#/# +
And fear him, all you offspring of Israel.

24 For he has not despised nor abhorred [.linebr]#/# +
the affliction of the afflicted, [.linebr]#/# +
neither has he hid his face from him. [.linebr]#/# +
But when he cried to him, he heard.

25 My praise shall be of you in the great congregation. [.linebr]#/# +
I will pay my vows before those who fear him.

26 The meek shall eat and be satisfied. [.linebr]#/# +
They shall praise the LORD who seek him. [.linebr]#/# +
Your heart shall live forever.

27 All the ends of the world shall remember and turn to the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and all the kindreds of the nations shall worship before you.

28 For the kingdom is the LORD'S, [.linebr]#/# +
and he is the governor among the nations.

29 All those who are fat upon earth shall eat and worship. [.linebr]#/# +
All those who go down to the dust shall bow before him. [.linebr]#/# +
And no one can keep his own soul alive.

30 Posterity shall serve him. [.linebr]#/# +
It shall be accounted to the Lord for a generation.

31 They shall come and declare his righteousness [.linebr]#/# +
to a people who shall be born, [.linebr]#/# +
that he has done this.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.1]*: Quoted in xref:#mth027-046[Matthew 27:46]; xref:#mrk015-034[Mark 15:34]. *[v.8]*: Quoted in xref:#mth027-043[Matthew 27:43]. *[v.18]*: Quoted in xref:#mth027-035[Matthew 27:35]; xref:#jhn019-024[John 19:24]. *[v.22]*: Quoted in xref:#heb002-012[Hebrews 2:12].

[#psa023%breakable]
=== Psalm 23

[.outline.text-center]
_David's confidence in God's grace, 1-6._

1 [_A Psalm of David._] The LORD is my shepherd. [.linebr]#/# +
I shall lack nothing.

2 He makes me to lie down in green pastures. [.linebr]#/# +
He leads me beside the still waters.

3 He restores my soul. [.linebr]#/# +
He leads me in the paths of righteousness [.linebr]#/# +
for his name's sake.

4 Even though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death, [.linebr]#/# +
I will fear no evil, [.linebr]#/# +
for you are with me. [.linebr]#/# +
Your rod and your staff, they comfort me.

5 You prepare a table before me [.linebr]#/# +
in the presence of my enemies. [.linebr]#/# +
You anoint my head with oil. [.linebr]#/# +
My cup runs over.

6 Surely goodness and mercy shall follow me [.linebr]#/# +
all the days of my life. [.linebr]#/# +
And I will dwell in the house of the LORD forever.

[#psa024%breakable]
=== Psalm 24

[.outline.text-center]
_God's lordship in the world, 1, 2. The citizens of his spiritual kingdom, 3-6. An exhortation to receive him, 7-10._

[[psa024-001]]1 [_A Psalm of David._]

The earth is the LORD'S, and the fullness thereof, [.linebr]#/# +
the world, and those who dwell therein.

2 For he has founded it upon the seas [.linebr]#/# +
and established it upon the floods.

3 Who shall ascend upon the hill of the LORD? [.linebr]#/# +
And who shall stand in his holy place?

4 He who has clean hands and a pure heart, [.linebr]#/# +
who has not lifted up his soul to vanity [.linebr]#/# +
nor sworn deceitfully.

5 He shall receive a blessing from the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
and righteousness from the God of his salvation.

6 This is the generation of those who seek him, [.linebr]#/# +
who seek your face, O Jacob. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

7 Lift up your heads, O gates, [.linebr]#/# +
and be lifted up, you everlasting doors, [.linebr]#/# +
and the King of glory shall come in.

8 Who is this King of glory? [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD, strong and mighty, [.linebr]#/# +
the LORD, mighty in battle.

9 Lift up your heads, O gates, [.linebr]#/# +
even lift them up, you everlasting doors, [.linebr]#/# +
and the King of glory shall come in.

10 Who is this King of glory? [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD of hosts, [.linebr]#/# +
he is the King of glory. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.1]*: Quoted in xref:#fco010-026[1st Corinthians 10:26], xref:#fco010-026[10:28].

[#psa025%breakable]
=== Psalm 25

[.outline.text-center]
_David's confidence in prayer, 1-6. He prays for remission of sins, 7-15; and for help in affliction, 16-22._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

+[+ _ALEPH_ - א +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|To you, O LORD, I lift up my soul.
|===

+[+ _BET_ - ב +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|2 O my God, I trust in you. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not let me be ashamed. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not let my enemies triumph over me.
|===

+[+ _GIMEL_ - ג +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|3 Also, let no one who waits for you be ashamed. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them be ashamed who transgress without cause.
|===

+[+ _DALET_ - ד +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|4 Show me your ways, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Teach me your paths.
|===

+[+ _HE_ - ה +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|5 Lead me in your truth and teach me, [.linebr]#/# +
for you are the God of my salvation. [.linebr]#/# +
On you I wait all the day.
|===

+[+ _VAV_ - ו +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|6 Remember, O LORD, your tender mercies [.linebr]#/# +
and your loving kindnesses, [.linebr]#/# +
for they have always been from of old.
|===

+[+ _ZAYIN_ - ז +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|

[#psa026%breakable]
=== Psalm 26

[.outline.text-center]
_David resorts to God in confidence of his integrity, 1-12._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

Judge me, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
for I have walked in my integrity. [.linebr]#/# +
I have also trusted in the LORD; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, I shall not slide.

2 Examine me, O LORD, and prove me. [.linebr]#/# +
Try my mind and my heart.

3 For your loving-kindness is before my eyes, [.linebr]#/# +
and I have walked in your truth.

4 I have not sat with vain persons, [.linebr]#/# +
neither will I go in with dissemblers.

5 I have hated the congregation of evildoers [.linebr]#/# +
and will not sit with the wicked.

6 I will wash my hands in innocence [.linebr]#/# +
and will compass your altar, O LORD,

7 So that I may publish with the voice of thanksgiving [.linebr]#/# +
and tell of all your wondrous works.

8 LORD, I have loved the habitation of your house [.linebr]#/# +
and the place where your honor dwells.

9 Do not gather my soul with sinners [.linebr]#/# +
nor my life with bloody men,

10 In whose hands is mischief, [.linebr]#/# +
and their right hand is full of bribes.

11 But as for me, I will walk in my integrity. [.linebr]#/# +
Redeem me and be merciful to me.

12 My foot stands in an even place. [.linebr]#/# +
In the congregations I will bless the LORD.

[#psa027%breakable]
=== Psalm 27

[.outline.text-center]
_David sustains his faith by prayer, 1-14._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

The LORD is my light and my salvation. [.linebr]#/# +
Whom shall I fear? [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD is the strength of my life. [.linebr]#/# +
Of whom shall I be afraid?

2 When the wicked, [.linebr]#/# +
even my enemies and my foes, [.linebr]#/# +
came upon me to eat up my flesh, [.linebr]#/# +
they stumbled and fell.

3 Though a host should encamp against me, [.linebr]#/# +
my heart shall not fear. [.linebr]#/# +
Though war should rise against me, [.linebr]#/# +
in this I will be confident.

4 One thing I have desired of the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
that I will seek after: [.linebr]#/# +
that I may dwell in the house of the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
all the days of my life [.linebr]#/# +
to behold the beauty of the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
and to inquire in his temple.

5 For in the time of trouble he will hide me in his pavilion. [.linebr]#/# +
In the secret of his tabernacle he will hide me. [.linebr]#/# +
He will set me up upon a rock.

6 And now my head shall be lifted [.linebr]#/# +
above my enemies around me; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, I will offer in his tabernacle sacrifices of joy. [.linebr]#/# +
I will sing, I will even sing praises to the LORD.

7 Hear, O LORD, when I cry with my voice, [.linebr]#/# +
and have mercy upon me and answer me.

8 When you said, "Seek my face," my heart said to you, [.linebr]#/# +
"Your face, LORD, I will seek."

9 Do not hide your face from me. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not put your servant away in anger. [.linebr]#/# +
You have been my help. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not leave me, neither forsake me, [.linebr]#/# +
O God of my salvation.

10 When my father and my mother forsake me, [.linebr]#/# +
the LORD will take me up.

11 Teach me your way, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and lead me in a plain path [.linebr]#/# +
because of my enemies.

12 Do not deliver me over to the will of my enemies, [.linebr]#/# +
for false witnesses have risen against me, [.linebr]#/# +
and those who breathe out cruelty.

13 I would have fainted unless I had believed to see [.linebr]#/# +
the goodness of the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
in the land of the living.

14 Wait for the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Be of good courage, and he will strengthen your heart. [.linebr]#/# +
Wait, I say, for the LORD.

[#psa028%breakable]
=== Psalm 28

[.outline.text-center]
_David prays earnestly against his enemies, 1-5; and for the people, 6-9._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

To you I will cry, O LORD my rock. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not be silent to me, [.linebr]#/# +
lest, if you are silent to me, [.linebr]#/# +
I become like those who go down into the pit.

2 Hear the voice of my supplications when I cry to you, [.linebr]#/# +
when I lift my hands toward your holy oracle.

3 Do not draw me away with the wicked [.linebr]#/# +
and with the workers of iniquity, [.linebr]#/# +
who speak peace to their neighbors, [.linebr]#/# +
but mischief is in their hearts.

4 Give them according to their deeds [.linebr]#/# +
and according to the wickedness of their endeavors. [.linebr]#/# +
Give them after the work of their hands. [.linebr]#/# +
Render to them what they deserve.

5 Because they do not regard the works of the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
nor the operation of his hands, [.linebr]#/# +
he will destroy them and not build them up.

6 Blessed be the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
because he has heard the voice of my supplications.

7 The LORD is my strength and my shield. [.linebr]#/# +
My heart trusted in him, and I am helped; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, my heart greatly rejoices, [.linebr]#/# +
and with my song I will praise him.

8 The LORD is their strength, [.linebr]#/# +
and he is the saving strength of his anointed.

9 Save your people and bless your inheritance. [.linebr]#/# +
Feed them also and lift them up forever.

[#psa029%breakable]
=== Psalm 29

[.outline.text-center]
_David exhorts princes to give glory to God, 1, 2; by reason of his power, 3-10; and protection of his people, 11._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

Give to the LORD, O you mighty, [.linebr]#/# +
give to the LORD glory and strength.

2 Give to the LORD the glory due to his name. [.linebr]#/# +
Worship the LORD in the beauty of holiness.

3 The voice of the LORD is upon the waters. [.linebr]#/# +
The God of glory thunders. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD is upon many waters.

4 The voice of the LORD is powerful. [.linebr]#/# +
The voice of the LORD is full of majesty.

5 The voice of the LORD breaks the cedars. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD even breaks the cedars of Lebanon.

6 He makes them also to skip like a calf, [.linebr]#/# +
Lebanon and Sirion like a young wild ox.

7 The voice of the LORD divides the flames of fire.

8 The voice of the LORD shakes the wilderness. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD shakes the wilderness of Kadesh.

9 The voice of the LORD makes the deer bring forth [.linebr]#/# +
and makes the forests bare. [.linebr]#/# +
And in his temple everyone speaks of his glory.

10 The LORD sits upon the flood. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD even sits king forever.

11 The LORD will give strength to his people. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD will bless his people with peace.

[#psa030%breakable]
=== Psalm 30

[.outline.text-center]
_David praises God for his deliverance, 1-3. He exhorts others to praise him by example of God's dealings with him, 4-12._

1 [_A Psalm and Song: for the dedication of the house of David._]

I will extol you, O LORD, for you have lifted me up [.linebr]#/# +
and have not made my foes to rejoice over me.

2 O LORD my God, [.linebr]#/# +
I cried to you, and you have healed me.

3 O LORD, you have brought up my soul from the grave. [.linebr]#/# +
You have kept me alive [.linebr]#/# +
so that I should not go down to the pit.

4 Sing to the LORD, O saints of his, [.linebr]#/# +
and give thanks at the remembrance of his holiness.

5 For his anger endures only a moment. [.linebr]#/# +
In his favor is life. [.linebr]#/# +
Weeping may endure for a night, [.linebr]#/# +
but joy comes in the morning.

6 And in my prosperity, I said, [.linebr]#/# +
"I shall never be moved."

7 LORD, by your favor [.linebr]#/# +
you have made my mountain to stand strong. [.linebr]#/# +
You hid your face, [.linebr]#/# +
and I was troubled.

8 I cried to you, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
And to the LORD I made supplication.

9 What profit is there in my blood [.linebr]#/# +
when I go down to the pit? [.linebr]#/# +
Shall the dust praise you? [.linebr]#/# +
Shall it declare your truth?

10 Hear, O LORD, and have mercy upon me. [.linebr]#/# +
LORD, be my helper.

11 You have turned for me my mourning into dancing. [.linebr]#/# +
You have put off my sackcloth [.linebr]#/# +
and girded me with gladness,

12 To the end that my glory may sing praise to you and not be silent. [.linebr]#/# +
O LORD my God, I will give thanks to you forever.

[#psa031%breakable]
=== Psalm 31

[.outline.text-center]
_David, showing his confidence in God, craves his help, 1-6. He rejoices in his mercy, 7, 8. He prays in his calamity, 9-18. He praises God for his goodness, 19-24._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

In you, O LORD, I put my trust. [.linebr]#/# +
Let me never be ashamed. [.linebr]#/# +
Deliver me in your righteousness.

2 Bow down your ear to me. Deliver me speedily. [.linebr]#/# +
Be my strong rock, [.linebr]#/# +
a house of defense to save me.

3 For you are my rock and my fortress; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, for your name's sake lead me and guide me.

4 Pull me out of the net that they have laid secretly for me, [.linebr]#/# +
for you are my strength.

[[psa031-005]]5 Into your hand I commit my spirit. [.linebr]#/# +
You have redeemed me, O LORD God of truth.

6 I have hated those who regard lying vanities, [.linebr]#/# +
but I trust in the LORD.

7 I will be glad and rejoice in your mercy, [.linebr]#/# +
for you have considered my trouble. [.linebr]#/# +
You have known my soul in adversities,

8 And have not shut me up into the hand of the enemy. [.linebr]#/# +
You have set my foot in a large room.

9 Have mercy upon me, O LORD, for I am in trouble. [.linebr]#/# +
My eye is consumed with grief, even my soul and my belly.

10 For my life is spent with grief [.linebr]#/# +
and my years with sighing. [.linebr]#/# +
My strength fails because of my iniquity [.linebr]#/# +
and my bones are consumed.

11 I was a reproach among all my enemies, [.linebr]#/# +
but especially among my neighbors, [.linebr]#/# +
and a fear to my acquaintances. [.linebr]#/# +
Those who saw me outside fled from me.

12 I am forgotten like a dead man out of mind. [.linebr]#/# +
I am like a broken vessel.

13 For I have heard the slander of many. [.linebr]#/# +
Fear was on every side. [.linebr]#/# +
While they took counsel together against me, [.linebr]#/# +
they devised to take away my life.

14 But I trusted in you, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
I said, "You are my God."

15 My times are in your hand. [.linebr]#/# +
Deliver me from the hand of my enemies [.linebr]#/# +
and from those who persecute me.

16 Make your face to shine upon your servant. [.linebr]#/# +
Save me for your mercies' sake.

17 Do not let me be ashamed, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
for I have called upon you. [.linebr]#/# +
Let the wicked be ashamed. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them be silent in the grave.

18 Let the lying lips be put to silence, [.linebr]#/# +
which speak grievous things proudly [.linebr]#/# +
and contemptuously against the righteous.

19 Oh how great your goodness is, [.linebr]#/# +
which you have laid up for those who fear you, [.linebr]#/# +
which you have wrought for those who trust in you [.linebr]#/# +
before the sons of men!

20 You shall hide them in the secret of your presence [.linebr]#/# +
from the pride of man. [.linebr]#/# +
You shall keep them secretly in a pavilion [.linebr]#/# +
from the strife of tongues.

21 Blessed be the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
for he has shown me his wonderful kindness in a strong city.

22 For I said in my haste, [.linebr]#/# +
"I am cut off from before your eyes." [.linebr]#/# +
Nevertheless, you heard the voice of my supplications [.linebr]#/# +
when I cried to you.

23 O love the LORD, all his saints, [.linebr]#/# +
for the LORD preserves the faithful [.linebr]#/# +
and fully recompenses the proud doer.

24 Be of good courage, and he will strengthen your heart, [.linebr]#/# +
all you who hope in the LORD.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.5]*: Quoted in xref:#luk023-046[Luke 23:46].

[#psa032%breakable]
=== Psalm 32

[.outline.text-center]
_Blessedness consists in remission of sins, 1, 2. Confession of sins gives case to the conscience, 3-7. God's promises bring joy, 8-11._

[[psa032-001]]1 [_A Psalm of David. Maschil._]

Blessed is he whose transgression is forgiven, [.linebr]#/# +
whose sin is covered.

[[psa032-002]]2 Blessed is the man to whom the LORD does not impute iniquity [.linebr]#/# +
and in whose spirit there is no guile.

3 When I kept silence, my bones became old [.linebr]#/# +
through my roaring all the day long.

4 For day and night your hand was heavy upon me. [.linebr]#/# +
My moisture is turned into the drought of summer. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

5 I acknowledged my sin to you, [.linebr]#/# +
and my iniquity I have not hid. [.linebr]#/# +
I said, "I will confess my transgressions to the LORD," [.linebr]#/# +
and you forgave the iniquity of my sin. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

6 For this everyone who is godly shall pray to you [.linebr]#/# +
in a time when you may be found. [.linebr]#/# +
Surely in the floods of great waters [.linebr]#/# +
they shall not come near to him.

7 You are my hiding place. [.linebr]#/# +
You will preserve me from trouble. [.linebr]#/# +
You will surround me with songs of deliverance. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

8 I will instruct you and teach you in the way which you shall go. [.linebr]#/# +
I will guide you with my eye.

9 Do not be like the horse or like the mule, [.linebr]#/# +
which have no understanding, [.linebr]#/# +
whose mouth must be held in with bit and bridle, [.linebr]#/# +
lest they come near to you.

10 Many sorrows shall be to the wicked, [.linebr]#/# +
but he who trusts in the LORD, mercy shall encompass him.

11 Be glad in the LORD and rejoice, you righteous, [.linebr]#/# +
and shout for joy, all you who are upright in heart.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.1]*: Quoted in xref:#rom004-007[Romans 4:7]. *[v.2]*: Quoted in xref:#rom004-008[Romans 4:8].

[#psa033%breakable]
=== Psalm 33

[.outline.text-center]
_God is to be praised for his goodness, 1-5; for his power, 6-11; and for his providence, 12-19. Confidence is to be placed in God, 20-22._

1 Rejoice in the LORD, O you righteous, [.linebr]#/# +
for praise is fitting for the upright.

2 Praise the LORD with the harp. [.linebr]#/# +
Sing to him with the psaltery and an instrument of ten strings.

3 Sing to him a new song. [.linebr]#/# +
Play skillfully with a loud noise.

4 For the word of the LORD is right, [.linebr]#/# +
and all his works are done in truth.

5 He loves righteousness and judgment. [.linebr]#/# +
The earth is full of the goodness of the LORD.

6 By the word of the LORD the heavens were made, [.linebr]#/# +
and all the host of them by the breath of his mouth.

7 He gathers the waters of the sea together as a heap. [.linebr]#/# +
He lays up the depth in store-houses.

8 Let all the earth fear the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Let all the inhabitants of the world stand in awe of him.

9 For he spoke, and it was done. [.linebr]#/# +
He commanded, and it stood fast.

10 The LORD brings the counsel of the heathen to nothing. [.linebr]#/# +
He makes the devices of the people of no effect.

11 The counsel of the LORD stands forever, [.linebr]#/# +
the thoughts of his heart to all generations.

12 Blessed is the nation whose God is the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
and the people whom he has chosen for his own inheritance.

13 The LORD looks from heaven. [.linebr]#/# +
He beholds all the sons of men.

14 From the place of his habitation he looks [.linebr]#/# +
upon all the inhabitants of the earth.

15 He fashions their hearts alike. [.linebr]#/# +
He considers all their works.

16 There is no king saved by the multitude of a host. [.linebr]#/# +
A mighty man is not delivered by great strength.

17 A horse is a vain thing for safety, [.linebr]#/# +
neither shall he deliver any by his great strength.

18 Behold, the eye of the LORD is upon those who fear him, [.linebr]#/# +
upon those who hope in his mercy,

19 To deliver their soul from death [.linebr]#/# +
and to keep them alive in famine.

20 Our soul waits for the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
He is our help and our shield.

21 For our heart shall rejoice in him [.linebr]#/# +
because we have trusted in his holy name.

22 Let your mercy, O LORD, be upon us, [.linebr]#/# +
according as we hope in you.

[#psa034%breakable]
=== Psalm 34

[.outline.text-center]
_David praises God and exhorts others thereto by his experience, 1-7. They are blessed who trust in God, 8-10. He exhorts to the fear of God, 11-14. The privileges of the righteous, 15-22._

1 [_A Psalm of David: when he changed his behavior before Abimelech, who drove him away, and he departed._]

I will bless the LORD at all times. [.linebr]#/# +
His praise shall continually be in my mouth.

2 My soul shall make her boast in the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
The humble shall hear of it and be glad.

3 O magnify the LORD with me, [.linebr]#/# +
and let us exalt his name together.

4 I sought the LORD, and he heard me [.linebr]#/# +
and delivered me from all my fears.

5 They looked to him and were radiant, [.linebr]#/# +
and their faces were not ashamed.

6 This poor man cried, and the LORD heard him [.linebr]#/# +
and saved him out of all his troubles.

7 The angel of the LORD encamps around those who fear him [.linebr]#/# +
and delivers them.

[[psa034-008]]8 O taste and see that the LORD is good. [.linebr]#/# +
Blessed is the man who trusts in him.

9 O fear the LORD, you his saints, [.linebr]#/# +
for there is no lack with those who fear him.

10 The young lions lack and suffer hunger, [.linebr]#/# +
but those who seek the LORD shall not lack any good thing.

11 Come, you children, listen to me. [.linebr]#/# +
I will teach you the fear of the LORD.

[[psa034-012]]12 What man is he who desires life [.linebr]#/# +
and loves many days, that he may see good?

[[psa034-013]]13 Keep your tongue from evil [.linebr]#/# +
and your lips from speaking guile.

[[psa034-014]]14 Depart from evil and do good. [.linebr]#/# +
Seek peace and pursue it.

[[psa034-015]]15 The eyes of the LORD are upon the righteous, [.linebr]#/# +
and his ears are open to their cry.

[[psa034-016]]16 The face of the LORD is against those who do evil [.linebr]#/# +
to cut off the remembrance of them from the earth.

17 The righteous cry, and the LORD hears [.linebr]#/# +
and delivers them out of all their troubles.

[[psa034-018]]18 The LORD is near to those who are of a broken heart [.linebr]#/# +
and saves those who are of a contrite spirit.

19 Many are the afflictions of the righteous, [.linebr]#/# +
but the LORD delivers him out of them all.

[[psa034-020]]20 He keeps all his bones. [.linebr]#/# +
Not one of them is broken.

21 Evil shall slay the wicked, [.linebr]#/# +
and those who hate the righteous shall be desolate.

22 The LORD redeems the soul of his servants, [.linebr]#/# +
and none of those who trust in him shall be desolate.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.8]*: Quoted in xref:#fpe002-003[1st Peter 2:3]. *[v.12]*: Quoted in xref:#fpe003-010[1st Peter 3:10]. *[v.13]*: Quoted in xref:#fpe003-010[1st Peter 3:10]. *[v.14]*: Quoted in xref:#fpe003-011[1st Peter 3:11]. *[v.15]*: Quoted in xref:#fpe003-012[1st Peter 3:12]. *[v.16]*: Quoted in xref:#fpe003-012[1st Peter 3:12]. *[v.20]*: Quoted in xref:#jhn019-036[John 19:36].

[#psa035%breakable]
=== Psalm 35

[.outline.text-center]
_David prays for his own safety and shame for his enemies, 1-10. He bemoans their wrongful dealing, 11-21. Thereby he incites God against them, 22-28._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

Plead my cause, O LORD, with those who strive with me. [.linebr]#/# +
Fight against those who fight against me.

2 Take hold of shield and buckler [.linebr]#/# +
and stand up for my help.

3 Draw out the spear also and stop the way [.linebr]#/# +
against those who persecute me. [.linebr]#/# +
Say to my soul, "I am your salvation."

4 Let them be confounded and put to shame [.linebr]#/# +
who seek after my soul. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them be turned back and brought to shame [.linebr]#/# +
who devise my hurt.

5 Let them be like chaff before the wind, [.linebr]#/# +
and let the angel of the LORD chase them.

6 Let their way be dark and slippery, [.linebr]#/# +
and let the angel of the LORD persecute them.

7 For without cause they have hid for me their net in a pit, [.linebr]#/# +
which without cause they have dug for my soul.

8 Let destruction come upon him unexpectedly, [.linebr]#/# +
and let his net that he has hid catch himself. [.linebr]#/# +
Into that very destruction let him fall.

9 And my soul shall be joyful in the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
It shall rejoice in his salvation.

10 All my bones shall say, "LORD, who is like you, [.linebr]#/# +
delivering the poor from him who is too strong for him, [.linebr]#/# +
even the poor and the needy from him who robs him?"

11 False witnesses arose. [.linebr]#/# +
They laid to my charge things that I did not know.

12 They rewarded me evil for good [.linebr]#/# +
to the bereaving of my soul.

13 But as for me, when they were sick, [.linebr]#/# +
my clothing was sackcloth. [.linebr]#/# +
I humbled my soul with fasting, [.linebr]#/# +
and my prayer returned into my own bosom.

14 I behaved myself as though he had been my friend or brother. [.linebr]#/# +
I bowed down heavily like one who mourns for his mother.

15 But in my adversity they rejoiced and assembled themselves. [.linebr]#/# +
The abjects even assembled themselves against me, [.linebr]#/# +
and I did not know it. [.linebr]#/# +
They tore me and did not cease.

16 With hypocritical mockers in feasts, [.linebr]#/# +
they gnashed upon me with their teeth.

17 Lord, how long will you look on? [.linebr]#/# +
Rescue my soul from their destructions, [.linebr]#/# +
my darling from the lions.

18 I will give you thanks in the great congregation. [.linebr]#/# +
I will praise you among many people.

[[psa035-019]]19 Do not let those who are my enemies wrongfully rejoice over me, [.linebr]#/# +
neither let them wink with the eye [.linebr]#/# +
who hate me without a cause.

20 For they do not speak peace, [.linebr]#/# +
but they devise deceitful matters [.linebr]#/# +
against those who are quiet in the land.

21 They even opened their mouth wide against me [.linebr]#/# +
and said, "Aha, aha, our eye has seen it."

22 This you have seen, O LORD. Do not keep silence. [.linebr]#/# +
O Lord, do not be far from me.

23 Stir up yourself and awake to my judgment, [.linebr]#/# +
even to my cause, my God and my Lord.

24 Judge me, O LORD my God, [.linebr]#/# +
according to your righteousness, [.linebr]#/# +
and do not let them rejoice over me.

25 Do not let them say in their hearts, [.linebr]#/# +
"Ah, we would have it so." [.linebr]#/# +
Do not let them say, [.linebr]#/# +
"We have swallowed him up."

26 Let them be ashamed and confounded together [.linebr]#/# +
who rejoice at my hurt. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them be clothed with shame and dishonor [.linebr]#/# +
who magnify themselves against me.

27 Let them shout for joy and be glad [.linebr]#/# +
who favor my righteous cause. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them even say continually, [.linebr]#/# +
"Let the LORD be magnified, [.linebr]#/# +
who has pleasure in the prosperity of his servant."

28 And my tongue shall speak of your righteousness [.linebr]#/# +
and of your praise all the day long.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.19]*: Quoted in xref:#jhn015-025[John 15:25].

[#psa036%breakable]
=== Psalm 36

[.outline.text-center]
_The grievous estate of the wicked, 1-4. The excellency of God's mercy, 8, 9. David prays for favor to God's children, 10-12._

[[psa036-001]]1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David the Servant of the LORD._]

The transgression of the wicked says within my heart [.linebr]#/# +
that there is no fear of God before his eyes.

2 For he flatters himself in his own eyes [.linebr]#/# +
until his iniquity is found to be hateful.

3 The words of his mouth are iniquity and deceit. [.linebr]#/# +
He has ceased to be wise and to do good.

4 He devises mischief upon his bed. [.linebr]#/# +
He sets himself in a way that is not good. [.linebr]#/# +
He does not abhor evil.

5 Your mercy, O LORD, is in the heavens [.linebr]#/# +
and your faithfulness reaches to the clouds.

6 Your righteousness is like the great mountains. [.linebr]#/# +
Your judgments are a great deep. [.linebr]#/# +
O LORD, you preserve man and beast.

7 How excellent your loving-kindness is, O God! [.linebr]#/# +
Therefore, the children of men put their trust [.linebr]#/# +
under the shadow of your wings.

8 They shall be abundantly satisfied with the fatness of your house, [.linebr]#/# +
and you shall make them drink from the river of your delights.

9 For with you is the fountain of life. [.linebr]#/# +
In your light we shall see light.

10 O continue your loving-kindness to those who know you, [.linebr]#/# +
and your righteousness to the upright in heart.

11 Do not let the foot of pride come against me, [.linebr]#/# +
and do not let the hand of the wicked drive me away.

12 There the workers of iniquity have fallen. [.linebr]#/# +
They are cast down and shall not be able to rise.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.1]*: Quoted in xref:#rom003-018[Romans 3:18].

[#psa037%breakable]
=== Psalm 37

[.outline.text-center]
_David persuades to patience and confidence in God by the different estate of the godly and the wicked, 1-40._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

Do not fret yourself because of evildoers, [.linebr]#/# +
neither be envious against the workers of iniquity.

2 For they shall soon be cut down like the grass [.linebr]#/# +
and wither like the green herb.

3 Trust in the LORD and do good. [.linebr]#/# +
Dwell in the land, and truly you shall be fed.

4 Delight yourself also in the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and he will give you the desires of your heart.

5 Commit your way to the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Trust also in him, and he will bring it to pass.

6 And he will bring forth your righteousness like the light [.linebr]#/# +
and your judgment like the noon-day.

7 Rest in the LORD and wait patiently for him. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not fret yourself because of him who prospers in his way, [.linebr]#/# +
because of the man who brings wicked devices to pass.

8 Cease from anger and forsake wrath. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not fret yourself. It leads only to evil-doing.

9 For evildoers shall be cut off, [.linebr]#/# +
but those who wait upon the LORD, they shall inherit the earth.

10 For yet a little while, and the wicked shall not be. [.linebr]#/# +
You shall even diligently consider his place, and it shall not be.

11 But the meek shall inherit the earth [.linebr]#/# +
and delight themselves in the abundance of peace.

12 The wicked plots against the just [.linebr]#/# +
and gnashes upon him with his teeth.

13 The Lord will laugh at him, [.linebr]#/# +
for he sees that his day is coming.

14 The wicked have drawn out the sword and bent their bow [.linebr]#/# +
to cast down the poor and needy [.linebr]#/# +
and to slay those who are of upright deportment.

15 Their sword shall enter into their own heart, [.linebr]#/# +
and their bows shall be broken.

16 A little that a righteous man has is better [.linebr]#/# +
than the riches of many wicked.

17 For the arms of the wicked shall be broken, [.linebr]#/# +
but the LORD upholds the righteous.

18 The LORD knows the days of the upright, [.linebr]#/# +
and their inheritance shall be forever.

19 They shall not be ashamed in the evil time, [.linebr]#/# +
and in the days of famine they shall be satisfied.

20 But the wicked shall perish, [.linebr]#/# +
and the enemies of the LORD shall be like the fat of lambs. [.linebr]#/# +
They shall consume. Into smoke they shall consume away.

21 The wicked borrows and does not pay back, [.linebr]#/# +
but the righteous shows mercy and gives.

22 For those who are blessed by him shall inherit the earth, [.linebr]#/# +
and those who are cursed by him shall be cut off.

23 The steps of a good man are ordered by the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and he delights in his way.

24 Though he should fall, he shall not be utterly cast down, [.linebr]#/# +
for the LORD upholds him with his hand.

25 I have been young, and now am old, [.linebr]#/# +
yet I have not seen the righteous forsaken, [.linebr]#/# +
nor his children begging for bread.

26 He is ever merciful and lends, [.linebr]#/# +
and his offspring is blessed.

27 Depart from evil and do good, [.linebr]#/# +
and dwell forevermore.

28 For the LORD loves judgment [.linebr]#/# +
and does not forsake his saints. [.linebr]#/# +
They are preserved forever, [.linebr]#/# +
but the offspring of the wicked shall be cut off.

29 The righteous shall inherit the land [.linebr]#/# +
and dwell therein forever.

30 The mouth of the righteous speaks wisdom, [.linebr]#/# +
and his tongue talks of judgment.

31 The law of his God is in his heart. [.linebr]#/# +
None of his steps shall slide.

32 The wicked watches the righteous [.linebr]#/# +
and seeks to slay him.

33 The LORD will not leave him in his hand, [.linebr]#/# +
nor condemn him when he is judged.

34 Wait on the LORD and keep his way, [.linebr]#/# +
and he will exalt you to inherit the land. [.linebr]#/# +
When the wicked are cut off, you shall see it.

35 I have seen the wicked in great power [.linebr]#/# +
and spreading himself like a green bay tree.

36 Yet he passed away, and behold, he was no more. [.linebr]#/# +
I even sought him, but he could not be found.

37 Mark the perfect man and behold the upright, [.linebr]#/# +
for the end of that man is peace.

38 But the transgressors shall be destroyed together. [.linebr]#/# +
The end of the wicked shall be cut off.

39 But the salvation of the righteous is of the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
He is their strength in the time of trouble.

40 And the LORD will help them and deliver them. [.linebr]#/# +
He will deliver them from the wicked and save them [.linebr]#/# +
because they trust in him.

[#psa038%breakable]
=== Psalm 38

[.outline.text-center]
_David moves God to take compassion on his pitiful case, 1-22._

1 [_A Psalm of David: to bring to remembrance._]

O LORD, do not rebuke me in your wrath, [.linebr]#/# +
neither chasten me in your hot displeasure.

2 For your arrows stick firmly in me, [.linebr]#/# +
and your hand falls heavy upon me.

3 There is no soundness in my flesh because of your anger, [.linebr]#/# +
neither is there any rest in my bones because of my sin.

4 For my iniquities have gone over my head. [.linebr]#/# +
Like a heavy burden, they are too heavy for me.

5 My wounds are offensive and are corrupt [.linebr]#/# +
because of my foolishness.

6 I am troubled. I am bowed down greatly. [.linebr]#/# +
I go mourning all the day long.

7 For my loins are filled with a loathsome disease, [.linebr]#/# +
and there is no soundness in my flesh.

8 I am feeble and grievously broken. [.linebr]#/# +
I have roared by reason of the disquietness of my heart.

9 Lord, all my desire is before you, [.linebr]#/# +
and my groaning is not hid from you.

10 My heart pants. My strength fails me. [.linebr]#/# +
As for the light of my eyes, that also is gone from me.

11 My loved ones and my friends stand aloof from my affliction, [.linebr]#/# +
and my kinsmen stand afar off.

12 Those who also seek after my life lay snares for me. [.linebr]#/# +
And those who seek my hurt speak mischievous things [.linebr]#/# +
and plot deceits all the day long.

13 But I, like a deaf man, did not hear. [.linebr]#/# +
And I was like a mute man who does not open his mouth.

14 Thus I was like a man who does not hear, [.linebr]#/# +
and in whose mouth are no reproofs.

15 For in you, O LORD, I hope. [.linebr]#/# +
You will hear, O Lord my God.

16 For I said, "Hear me, lest otherwise they should rejoice over me. [.linebr]#/# +
When my foot slips, they magnify themselves against me."

17 For I am ready to fall, [.linebr]#/# +
and my sorrow is continually before me.

18 For I will declare my iniquity. [.linebr]#/# +
I will be sorry for my sin.

19 But my enemies are lively and they are strong, [.linebr]#/# +
and those who hate me wrongfully are multiplied.

20 Those who also render evil for good [.linebr]#/# +
are my adversaries because I follow the thing that is good.

21 Do not forsake me, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
O my God, do not be far from me.

22 Make haste to help me, [.linebr]#/# +
O Lord my salvation.

[#psa039%breakable]
=== Psalm 39

[.outline.text-center]
_David's care of his thoughts, 1-3. The consideration of the brevity and vanity of life, 4-6; the reverence of God's judgments, 7-9, and prayer, are his bridles for impatience, 10-13._

1 [_To the Chief Musician, even to Jeduthun. A Psalm of David._]

I said, "I will take heed to my ways [.linebr]#/# +
so that I do not sin with my tongue. [.linebr]#/# +
I will keep my mouth with a bridle [.linebr]#/# +
while the wicked is before me."

2 I was mute with silence. [.linebr]#/# +
I held my peace, even from good, [.linebr]#/# +
and my sorrow was stirred.

3 My heart was hot within me. [.linebr]#/# +
While I was musing, the fire burned. [.linebr]#/# +
Then I spoke with my tongue:

4 "LORD, make me to know my end [.linebr]#/# +
and the measure of my days, what it is, [.linebr]#/# +
so that I may know how frail I am.

5 Behold, you have made my days as a hand-breadth, [.linebr]#/# +
and my age is as nothing before you. [.linebr]#/# +
Truly every man at his best state is altogether vanity." [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+
