6 "Surely every man walks in a vain show. [.linebr]#/# +
Surely they are disquieted in vain. [.linebr]#/# +
He heaps up riches and does not know who gathers them.

7 And now, Lord, what do I wait for? [.linebr]#/# +
My hope is in you.

8 Deliver me from all my transgressions. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not make me the reproach of the foolish.

9 I was mute. I did not open my mouth [.linebr]#/# +
because you did it.

10 Remove your stroke away from me. [.linebr]#/# +
I am consumed by the blow of your hand.

11 When you, with rebukes, correct man for iniquity, [.linebr]#/# +
you make his beauty to consume away like a moth. [.linebr]#/# +
Surely every man is vanity." [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

12 "Hear my prayer, O LORD, and give ear to my cry. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not hold your peace at my tears, [.linebr]#/# +
for I am a stranger with you, [.linebr]#/# +
and a sojourner, as all my fathers were.

13 O spare me so that I may recover strength [.linebr]#/# +
before I go from here and am no more."

[#psa040%breakable]
=== Psalm 40

[.outline.text-center]
_The benefit of confidence in God, 1-5. Obedience is the best sacrifice, 6-10. The sense of David's evils inflames his prayer, 11-17._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

I waited patiently for the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and he inclined to me and heard my cry.

2 He brought me up also out of a horrible pit, [.linebr]#/# +
out of the miry clay, [.linebr]#/# +
and set my feet upon a rock [.linebr]#/# +
and established my goings.

3 And he has put a new song in my mouth, [.linebr]#/# +
even praise to our God. [.linebr]#/# +
Many shall see it and fear [.linebr]#/# +
and trust in the LORD.

4 Blessed is that man who makes the LORD his trust [.linebr]#/# +
and does not respect the proud [.linebr]#/# +
or those who turn aside to lies.

5 Many, O LORD, my God, [.linebr]#/# +
are your wonderful works which you have done [.linebr]#/# +
and your thoughts which are toward us. [.linebr]#/# +
They cannot be reckoned up in order to you. [.linebr]#/# +
If I would declare and speak of them, [.linebr]#/# +
they are more than can be numbered.

[[psa040-006]]6 Sacrifice and offering you did not desire. [.linebr]#/# +
You have opened my ears. [.linebr]#/# +
Burnt-offering and sin-offering you have not required.

[[psa040-007]]7 Then I said, "Behold, I come. [.linebr]#/# +
In the volume of the book it is written about me.

[[psa040-008]]8 I delight to do your will, O my God. [.linebr]#/# +
Your law is even within my heart."

9 I have preached righteousness in the great congregation. [.linebr]#/# +
Behold, I have not refrained my lips, O LORD, as you know.

10 I have not hid your righteousness within my heart. [.linebr]#/# +
I have declared your faithfulness and your salvation. [.linebr]#/# +
I have not concealed your loving-kindness and your truth [.linebr]#/# +
from the great congregation.

11 Do not withhold your tender mercies from me, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Let your loving-kindness and your truth continually preserve me.

12 For innumerable evils have encompassed me. [.linebr]#/# +
My iniquities have taken hold upon me [.linebr]#/# +
so that I am not able to look up. [.linebr]#/# +
They are more than the hairs of my head; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, my heart fails me.

13 Be pleased, O LORD, to deliver me. [.linebr]#/# +
O LORD, make haste to help me.

14 Let them be ashamed and confounded together [.linebr]#/# +
who seek after my soul to destroy it. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them be driven backward and put to shame [.linebr]#/# +
who wish me evil.

15 Let them be desolate by reason of their shame [.linebr]#/# +
who say to me, "Aha, aha."

16 Let all those who seek you rejoice and be glad in you. [.linebr]#/# +
Let those who love your salvation say continually, [.linebr]#/# +
"May the LORD be magnified."

17 But I am poor and needy, [.linebr]#/# +
yet the Lord thinks upon me. [.linebr]#/# +
You are my help and my deliverer. [.linebr]#/# +
Make no delay, O my God.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.6]*: Quoted in xref:#heb010-005[Hebrews 10:5-6], xref:#heb010-008[10:8]. *[v.7]*: Quoted in xref:#heb010-007[Hebrews 10:7], xref:#heb010-009[10:9]. *[v.8]*: Quoted in xref:#heb010-007[Hebrews 10:7], xref:#heb010-009[10:9].

[#psa041%breakable]
=== Psalm 41

[.outline.text-center]
_The recompense of the charitable, 1-3. David bemoans his enemies' treachery, 4-9. He flees to God for help, 10-13._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

Blessed is he who considers the poor. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD will deliver him in the time of trouble.

2 The LORD will preserve him and keep him alive, [.linebr]#/# +
and he shall be blessed upon the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
And you will not deliver him to the will of his enemies.

3 The LORD will strengthen him upon the bed of languishing. [.linebr]#/# +
You will restore his health in his sickness.

4 I said, "LORD, be merciful to me. [.linebr]#/# +
Heal my soul, for I have sinned against you."

5 My enemies speak evil of me, [.linebr]#/# +
"When shall he die and his name perish?"

6 And if he comes to see me, he speaks vanity. [.linebr]#/# +
His heart gathers iniquity to itself. [.linebr]#/# +
When he goes abroad, he tells it.

7 All who hate me whisper together against me. [.linebr]#/# +
They devise my hurt against me.

8 "An evil disease," they say, "cleaves fast to him. [.linebr]#/# +
And now that he lies he shall rise no more."

[[psa041-009]]9 Even my own familiar friend in whom I trusted, [.linebr]#/# +
who ate my bread, has lifted up his heel against me.

10 But you, O LORD, be merciful to me and raise me up [.linebr]#/# +
so that I may requite them.

11 By this I know that you favor me, [.linebr]#/# +
because my enemy does not triumph over me.

12 And as for me, you uphold me in my integrity [.linebr]#/# +
and set me before your face forever.

13 Blessed be the LORD God of Israel [.linebr]#/# +
from everlasting to everlasting. [.linebr]#/# +
Amen and amen.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.9]*: Quoted in xref:#jhn013-018[John 13:18].

[#psalms-book-2%breakable]
=== BOOK II

[#psa042%breakable]
=== Psalm 42

[.outline.text-center]
_David's zeal to serve God in the temple, 1-4. He encourages his soul to trust in God, 5-11._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. Maschil for the Sons of Korah._]

As the deer pants after the water brooks, [.linebr]#/# +
so my soul pants after you, O God.

2 My soul thirsts for God, for the living God. [.linebr]#/# +
When shall I come and appear before God?

3 My tears have been my food day and night [.linebr]#/# +
while they continually say to me, "Where is your God?"

4 When I remember these things, [.linebr]#/# +
I pour out my soul in me. [.linebr]#/# +
For I had gone with the multitude. [.linebr]#/# +
I went with them to the house of God, [.linebr]#/# +
with the voice of joy and praise, [.linebr]#/# +
with a multitude who kept holy-day.

5 Why are you cast down, O my soul? [.linebr]#/# +
And why are you disquieted in me? [.linebr]#/# +
Hope in God. For I shall again praise him [.linebr]#/# +
for the help of his countenance.

6 O my God, my soul is cast down within me; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, I will remember you from the land of the Jordan [.linebr]#/# +
and of the Hermonites, from the hill Mizar.

7 Deep calls to deep at the noise of your water-spouts. [.linebr]#/# +
All your waves and your billows have gone over me.

8 Yet the LORD will command his loving-kindness in the day-time, [.linebr]#/# +
and in the night his song shall be with me, [.linebr]#/# +
and my prayer to the God of my life.

9 I will say to God my rock, [.linebr]#/# +
"Why have you forgotten me? [.linebr]#/# +
Why do I go mourning [.linebr]#/# +
because of the oppression of the enemy?"

10 As with a sword in my bones, my enemies reproach me [.linebr]#/# +
while they daily say to me, "Where is your God?"

11 Why are you cast down, O my soul? [.linebr]#/# +
And why are you disquieted within me? [.linebr]#/# +
Hope in God. For I shall again praise him [.linebr]#/# +
who is the health of my countenance and my God.

[#psa043%breakable]
=== Psalm 43

[.outline.text-center]
_David, praying to be restored to the temple, promises to serve God joyfully, 1-4. He encourages his soul to trust in God, 5._

1 Judge me, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
and plead my cause against an ungodly nation. [.linebr]#/# +
O deliver me from the deceitful and unjust man.

2 For you are the God of my strength. [.linebr]#/# +
Why do you cast me off? [.linebr]#/# +
Why do I go mourning [.linebr]#/# +
because of the oppression of the enemy?

3 O send out your light and your truth. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them lead me. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them bring me to your holy hill [.linebr]#/# +
and to your tabernacles.

4 Then I will go to the altar of God, [.linebr]#/# +
to God, my exceeding joy. [.linebr]#/# +
Upon the harp I will even praise you, [.linebr]#/# +
O God my God.

5 Why are you cast down, O my soul? [.linebr]#/# +
And why are you disquieted within me? [.linebr]#/# +
Hope in God. For I shall again praise him [.linebr]#/# +
who is the health of my countenance and my God.

[#psa044%breakable]
=== Psalm 44

[.outline.text-center]
_The church, in memory of former favors, 1-6, bemoans her present evils, 7-16. Professing her integrity, 17-23, she fervently prays for help, 24-26._

1 [_To the Chief Musician for the Sons of Korah. Maschil._]

We have heard with our ears, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
Our fathers have told us what work you did in their days, [.linebr]#/# +
in the times of old:

2 How you drove out the heathen with your hand [.linebr]#/# +
and planted them, [.linebr]#/# +
how you afflicted the people [.linebr]#/# +
and cast them out.

3 For they did not obtain the land in possession by their own sword, [.linebr]#/# +
neither did their own arm save them, [.linebr]#/# +
but your right hand, your arm, [.linebr]#/# +
and the light of your countenance, [.linebr]#/# +
because you were favorable to them.

4 You are my King, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
Command deliverances for Jacob.

5 Through you we will push down our enemies. [.linebr]#/# +
Through your name we will tread them under who rise up against us.

6 For I will not trust in my bow, [.linebr]#/# +
neither shall my sword save me.

7 But you have saved us from our enemies [.linebr]#/# +
and have put them to shame who hated us.

8 In God we boast all the day long. [.linebr]#/# +
We will praise your name forever. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

9 But you have cast off and put us to shame [.linebr]#/# +
and do not go forth with our armies.

10 You make us to turn back from the enemy. [.linebr]#/# +
And those who hate us plunder for themselves.

11 You have given us like sheep appointed for food [.linebr]#/# +
and scattered us among the heathen.

12 You sell your people for nothing [.linebr]#/# +
and have not increased your wealth by their price.

13 You make us a reproach to our neighbors, [.linebr]#/# +
a scorn and a derision to those who are around us.

14 You make us a by-word among the heathen, [.linebr]#/# +
a shaking of the head among the people.

15 My disgrace is continually before me, [.linebr]#/# +
and the shame of my face has covered me,

16 Because of the voice of him who reproaches and blasphemes, [.linebr]#/# +
because of the enemy and avenger.

17 All this has come upon us, yet we have not forgotten you, [.linebr]#/# +
neither have we dealt falsely in your covenant.

18 Our heart has not turned back, [.linebr]#/# +
neither have our steps declined from your way,

19 Though you have severely broken us in the place of jackals [.linebr]#/# +
and covered us with the shadow of death.

20 If we have forgotten the name of our God [.linebr]#/# +
or stretched out our hands to a strange god,

21 Will God not search this out? [.linebr]#/# +
For he knows the secrets of the heart.

[[psa044-022]]22 Indeed, for your sake we are killed all the day long. [.linebr]#/# +
We are counted as sheep for the slaughter.

23 Awake, why do you sleep, O Lord? [.linebr]#/# +
Arise, do not cast us off forever.

24 Why do you hide your face [.linebr]#/# +
and forget our affliction and our oppression?

25 For our soul is bowed down to the dust. [.linebr]#/# +
Our belly cleaves to the earth.

26 Arise for our help [.linebr]#/# +
and redeem us for your mercies' sake.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.22]*: Quoted in xref:#rom008-036[Romans 8:36].

[#psa045%breakable]
=== Psalm 45

[.outline.text-center]
_The majesty and grace of Christ's kingdom, 1-9. The duty of the church and the benefits thereof, 10-17._

1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Shoshannim for the Sons of Korah. Maschil. A Song of Love._]

My heart is inditing a good matter. [.linebr]#/# +
I speak of the things which I have made concerning the king. [.linebr]#/# +
My tongue is the pen of a ready writer.

2 You are fairer than the children of men. [.linebr]#/# +
Grace is poured into your lips; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, God has blessed you forever.

3 Gird your sword upon your thigh, O most mighty, [.linebr]#/# +
with your glory and your majesty.

4 And in your majesty ride prosperously [.linebr]#/# +
because of truth, meekness, and righteousness. [.linebr]#/# +
And your right hand shall teach you awesome things.

5 Your arrows are sharp [.linebr]#/# +
in the heart of the king's enemies, [.linebr]#/# +
by which the people fall under you.

[[psa045-006]]6 Your throne, O God, is forever and ever. [.linebr]#/# +
The scepter of your kingdom is a scepter of justice.

[[psa045-007]]7 You love righteousness and hate wickedness; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, God, your God, has anointed you [.linebr]#/# +
with the oil of gladness above your fellows.

8 All your garments smell of myrrh, aloes, and cassia. [.linebr]#/# +
Out of the ivory palaces stringed instruments have made you glad.

9 Kings' daughters were among your honorable women. [.linebr]#/# +
Upon your right hand stood the queen in gold of Ophir.

10 Listen, O daughter. Consider, and incline your ear. [.linebr]#/# +
Forget your own people and your father's house,

11 And the king shall greatly desire your beauty. [.linebr]#/# +
Worship him, for he is your lord.

12 And the daughter of Tyre shall be there with a gift. [.linebr]#/# +
Even the rich among the people shall entreat your favor.

13 The king's daughter is all glorious within. [.linebr]#/# +
Her clothing is wrought with gold.

14 She shall be brought to the king in clothing of needle-work. [.linebr]#/# +
The virgins, her companions who follow her, [.linebr]#/# +
shall be brought to you.

15 With gladness and rejoicing they shall be brought. [.linebr]#/# +
They shall enter into the king's palace.

16 In place of your fathers will be your children, [.linebr]#/# +
whom you may make princes in all the earth.

17 I will make your name to be remembered in all generations; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, the people shall praise you forever and ever.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.6]*: Quoted in xref:#heb001-008[Hebrews 1:8]. *[v.7]*: Quoted in xref:#heb001-009[Hebrews 1:9].

[#psa046%breakable]
=== Psalm 46

[.outline.text-center]
_The confidence which the church has in God, 1-7. An exhortation to behold it, 8-11._

1 [_To the Chief Musician for the Sons of Korah. A Song upon Alamoth._]

God is our refuge and strength, [.linebr]#/# +
a very present help in trouble.

2 Therefore, we will not fear [.linebr]#/# +
though the earth is changed, [.linebr]#/# +
though the mountains are carried [.linebr]#/# +
into the midst of the sea,

3 Though its waters roar and are disturbed, [.linebr]#/# +
though the mountains shake with its swelling. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

4 There is a river, [.linebr]#/# +
the streams of which shall make the city of God glad, [.linebr]#/# +
the holy place of the tabernacles of the Most High.

5 God is in the midst of her. She shall not be moved. [.linebr]#/# +
God shall help her at the turning of dawn.

6 The heathen raged. The kingdoms were moved. [.linebr]#/# +
He uttered his voice, and the earth melted.

7 The LORD of hosts is with us. [.linebr]#/# +
The God of Jacob is our refuge. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

8 Come, behold the works of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
what desolations he has made in the earth.

9 He makes wars to cease to the end of the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
He breaks the bow and cuts the spear apart. [.linebr]#/# +
He burns the chariot in the fire.

10 "Be still and know that I am God. [.linebr]#/# +
I will be exalted among the heathen. [.linebr]#/# +
I will be exalted in the earth."

11 The LORD of hosts is with us. [.linebr]#/# +
The God of Jacob is our refuge. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

[#psa047%breakable]
=== Psalm 47

[.outline.text-center]
_The nations are exhorted cheerfully to entertain the kingdom of Christ, 1-9._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm for the Sons of Korah._]

O clap your hands, all you people. [.linebr]#/# +
Shout to God with the voice of triumph.

2 For the LORD most high is awesome. [.linebr]#/# +
He is a great King over all the earth.

3 He shall subdue the people under us [.linebr]#/# +
and the nations under our feet.

4 He shall choose our inheritance for us, [.linebr]#/# +
the excellence of Jacob whom he loved. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

5 God has gone up with a shout, [.linebr]#/# +
the LORD with the sound of a trumpet.

6 Sing praises to God, sing praises. [.linebr]#/# +
Sing praises to our King, sing praises.

7 For God is the King of all the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
Sing praises with understanding.

8 God reigns over the heathen. [.linebr]#/# +
God sits upon the throne of his holiness.

9 The princes of the people are assembled, [.linebr]#/# +
even the people of the God of Abraham. [.linebr]#/# +
For the shields of the earth belong to God. [.linebr]#/# +
He is greatly exalted.

[#psa048%breakable]
=== Psalm 48

[.outline.text-center]
_The ornaments and privileges of the church, 1-14._

1 [_A Song and Psalm for the Sons of Korah._]

The LORD is great and greatly to be praised [.linebr]#/# +
in the city of our God, in the mountain of his holiness.

[[psa048-002]]2 Beautiful in elevation, the joy of the whole earth, [.linebr]#/# +
is mount Zion, on the sides of the north, [.linebr]#/# +
the city of the great King.

3 God is known in her palaces as a refuge.

4 For behold, the kings were assembled. [.linebr]#/# +
They passed by together.

5 They saw it, and so they wondered. [.linebr]#/# +
They were troubled and hastened away.

6 Fear took hold upon them there, [.linebr]#/# +
and pain, as of a woman in travail.

7 You break the ships of Tarshish [.linebr]#/# +
with an east wind.

8 As we have heard, so we have seen [.linebr]#/# +
in the city of the LORD of hosts, [.linebr]#/# +
in the city of our God. [.linebr]#/# +
God will establish it forever. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

9 We have thought of your loving-kindness, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
in the midst of your temple.

10 According to your name, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
so is your praise to the ends of the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
Your right hand is full of righteousness.

11 Let mount Zion rejoice, [.linebr]#/# +
let the daughters of Judah be glad [.linebr]#/# +
because of your judgments.

12 Walk around Zion and encompass her. [.linebr]#/# +
Number her towers,

13 Mark well her bulwarks, [.linebr]#/# +
and consider her palaces [.linebr]#/# +
so that you may tell it to the generation following.

14 For this God is our God forever and ever. [.linebr]#/# +
He will be our guide even to death.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.2]*: Quoted in xref:#mth005-035[Matthew 5:35].

[#psa049%breakable]
=== Psalm 49

[.outline.text-center]
_An earnest persuasion to build the faith of resurrection, not on worldly power, but on God, 1-15. Worldly prosperity is not to be admired, 16-20._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm for the Sons of Korah._]

Hear this, all you people. [.linebr]#/# +
Give ear, all you inhabitants of the world,

2 Both low and high, [.linebr]#/# +
rich and poor together.

3 My mouth shall speak of wisdom. [.linebr]#/# +
The meditation of my heart shall be of understanding.

4 I will incline my ear to a parable. [.linebr]#/# +
I will open my dark saying upon the harp.

5 Why should I fear in the days of evil [.linebr]#/# +
when the iniquity of my heels encompasses me?

6 Those who trust in their wealth [.linebr]#/# +
and boast themselves in the multitude of their riches,

7 None of them can by any means redeem his brother, [.linebr]#/# +
nor give to God a ransom for him

8 (For the redemption of their soul is costly, [.linebr]#/# +
and it ceases forever),

9 That he should still live forever [.linebr]#/# +
and not see corruption.

10 For he sees that wise men die; [.linebr]#/# +
likewise the fool and the brutish person perish [.linebr]#/# +
and leave their wealth to others.

11 Their inward thought is that their houses shall continue forever [.linebr]#/# +
and their dwelling places to all generations. [.linebr]#/# +
They call their lands after their own names.

12 Nevertheless, man being in honor does not abide. [.linebr]#/# +
He is like the beasts that perish.

13 Their way is their folly, [.linebr]#/# +
yet their posterity approve their sayings. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

14 Like sheep they are laid in the grave. [.linebr]#/# +
Death shall feed on them. [.linebr]#/# +
The upright shall have dominion over them in the morning. [.linebr]#/# +
Their beauty shall consume [.linebr]#/# +
in the grave from their dwelling.

15 But God will redeem my soul from the power of the grave, [.linebr]#/# +
for he shall receive me. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

16 Do not be afraid when one is made rich, [.linebr]#/# +
when the glory of his house is increased,

17 For when he dies he shall carry nothing away. [.linebr]#/# +
His glory shall not descend after him.

18 Though while he lived he blessed his soul— [.linebr]#/# +
and men will praise you when you do well to yourself—

19 He shall go to the generation of his fathers. [.linebr]#/# +
They shall never see light.

20 A man who is in honor and does not understand [.linebr]#/# +
is like the beasts that perish.

[#psa050%breakable]
=== Psalm 50

[.outline.text-center]
_The majesty of God in the church, 1-4. His order to gather his saints, 5, 6. The pleasure of God is not in ceremonies, 7-13, but in sincerity of obedience, 14-23._

1 [_A Psalm of Asaph._]

The mighty God, even the LORD, has spoken [.linebr]#/# +
and called the earth from the rising to the setting of the sun.

2 Out of Zion, the perfection of beauty, [.linebr]#/# +
God has shined.

3 Our God shall come and shall not keep silence. [.linebr]#/# +
A fire shall devour before him [.linebr]#/# +
and it shall be very tempestuous around him.

4 He shall call to the heavens from above [.linebr]#/# +
and to the earth so that he may judge his people.

5 "Gather my saints together to me, [.linebr]#/# +
those who have made a covenant with me by sacrifice."

6 And the heavens shall declare his righteousness, [.linebr]#/# +
for God is judge himself. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

7 "Hear, O my people, and I will speak, [.linebr]#/# +
O Israel, and I will testify against you. [.linebr]#/# +
I am God, even your God.

8 I will not reprove you for your sacrifices [.linebr]#/# +
or your burnt-offerings which have been continually before me.

9 I will take no bull out of your house, [.linebr]#/# +
nor male goats out of your folds.

10 For every beast of the forest is mine, [.linebr]#/# +
and the livestock upon a thousand hills.

11 I know all the birds of the mountains. [.linebr]#/# +
And the wild beasts of the field are mine.

12 If I were hungry, I would not tell you, [.linebr]#/# +
for the world is mine, and the fullness thereof.

13 Will I eat the flesh of bulls [.linebr]#/# +
or drink the blood of goats?

14 Offer to God thanksgiving [.linebr]#/# +
and pay your vows to the Most High.

15 And call upon me in the day of trouble. [.linebr]#/# +
I will deliver you, and you shall glorify me."

16 But to the wicked, God says, [.linebr]#/# +
"What have you to do to declare my statutes, [.linebr]#/# +
or that you should take my covenant in your mouth,

17 Seeing you hate instruction [.linebr]#/# +
and cast my words behind you?

18 When you saw a thief, you consented with him. [.linebr]#/# +
You have been partaker with adulterers.

19 You give your mouth to evil [.linebr]#/# +
and your tongue frames deceit.

20 You sit and speak against your brother. [.linebr]#/# +
You slander your own mother's son.

21 These things you have done, and I kept silence. [.linebr]#/# +
You thought that I was altogether such a one as yourself. [.linebr]#/# +
But I will reprove you and set them in order before your eyes.

22 Now consider this, you who forget God, [.linebr]#/# +
lest I tear you in pieces and there be no one to deliver:

23 Whoever offers praise glorifies me, [.linebr]#/# +
and to him who orders his deportment aright [.linebr]#/# +
I will show the salvation of God."

[#psa051%breakable]
=== Psalm 51

[.outline.text-center]
_David prays for remission of sins, whereof he makes a deep confession, 1-5. He prays for sanctification, 6-15. God does not delight in sacrifice, but in sincerity, 16, 17. He prays for the church, 18, 19._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David: when Nathan the prophet came to him after he had gone in to Bath-sheba._]

Have mercy upon me, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
according to your loving-kindness. [.linebr]#/# +
According to the multitude of your tender mercies, [.linebr]#/# +
blot out my transgressions.

2 Wash me thoroughly from my iniquity [.linebr]#/# +
and cleanse me from my sin.

3 For I acknowledge my transgressions, [.linebr]#/# +
and my sin is always before me.

[[psa051-004]]4 Against you, you only, I have sinned [.linebr]#/# +
and done this evil in your sight, [.linebr]#/# +
so that you may be justified when you speak [.linebr]#/# +
and clear when you judge.

5 Behold, I was shaped in iniquity, [.linebr]#/# +
and in sin my mother conceived me.

6 Behold, you desire truth in the inward parts. [.linebr]#/# +
And in the hidden part you shall make me to know wisdom.

7 Purge me with hyssop, and I shall be clean. [.linebr]#/# +
Wash me, and I shall be whiter than snow.

8 Make me to hear joy and gladness [.linebr]#/# +
so that the bones which you have broken may rejoice.

9 Hide your face from my sins [.linebr]#/# +
and blot out all my iniquities.

10 Create in me a clean heart, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
and renew a right spirit within me.

11 Do not cast me away from your presence, [.linebr]#/# +
and do not take your Holy Spirit from me.

12 Restore to me the joy of your salvation, [.linebr]#/# +
and uphold me with your free spirit.

13 Then I will teach transgressors your ways, [.linebr]#/# +
and sinners shall be converted to you.

14 Deliver me from blood-guiltiness, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
God of my salvation, [.linebr]#/# +
and my tongue shall sing aloud of your righteousness.

15 O Lord, open my lips, [.linebr]#/# +
and my mouth shall show forth your praise.

16 For you do not desire sacrifice, or else I would give it. [.linebr]#/# +
You do not delight in burnt-offering.

17 The sacrifices of God are a broken spirit. [.linebr]#/# +
A broken and a contrite heart, O God, you will not despise.

18 Do good in your good pleasure to Zion. [.linebr]#/# +
Build the walls of Jerusalem.

19 Then you shall be pleased with the sacrifices of righteousness, [.linebr]#/# +
with burnt-offering and whole burnt-offering. [.linebr]#/# +
Then they shall offer bulls upon your altar.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.4]*: Quoted in xref:#rom003-004[Romans 3:4].

[#psa052%breakable]
=== Psalm 52

[.outline.text-center]
_David, condemning the spitefulness of Doeg, prophesies his destruction, 1-5. The righteous shall rejoice at it, 6, 7. David, upon his confidence in God's mercy, gives thanks, 8, 9._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. Maschil. A Psalm of David: when Doeg the Edomite came and told Saul and said to him, "David has come to the house of Ahimelech."_]

Why do you boast yourself in mischief, O mighty man? [.linebr]#/# +
The goodness of God endures continually.

2 Your tongue devises mischiefs, [.linebr]#/# +
like a sharp razor, working deceitfully.

3 You love evil more than good [.linebr]#/# +
and lying rather than speaking righteousness. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

4 You love all devouring words, [.linebr]#/# +
O deceitful tongue.

5 God shall likewise destroy you forever. [.linebr]#/# +
He shall take you away and pluck you out of your dwelling-place. [.linebr]#/# +
He shall root you out of the land of the living. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

6 The righteous also shall see and fear. [.linebr]#/# +
They shall laugh at him:

7 "Behold, this is the man who did not make God his strength, [.linebr]#/# +
but trusted in the abundance of his riches [.linebr]#/# +
and strengthened himself in his wickedness."

8 But I am like a green olive tree in the house of God. [.linebr]#/# +
I trust in the mercy of God forever and ever.

9 I will praise you forever because you have done it. [.linebr]#/# +
I will wait on your name, for it is good, [.linebr]#/# +
in the presence of your saints.

[#psa053%breakable]
=== Psalm 53

[.outline.text-center]
_David describes the corruption of a natural man, 1-3. He convinces the wicked by the light of their own conscience, 4, 5. He glories in the salvation of God, 6._

[[psa053-001]]1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Mahalath. Maschil. A Psalm of David._]

The fool has said in his heart, "There is no God." [.linebr]#/# +
They are corrupt and have done abominable iniquity. [.linebr]#/# +
There is no one who does good.

[[psa053-002]]2 God looked down from heaven upon the children of men [.linebr]#/# +
to see if there were any who understood, [.linebr]#/# +
who sought God.

[[psa053-003]]3 Every one of them has gone back. [.linebr]#/# +
They have altogether become filthy. [.linebr]#/# +
There is no one who does good, not even one.

4 Have the workers of iniquity no knowledge, [.linebr]#/# +
who eat up my people like they eat bread [.linebr]#/# +
and have not called upon God?

5 There they were in great fear, [.linebr]#/# +
where no fear was, [.linebr]#/# +
for God has scattered the bones [.linebr]#/# +
of him who encamps against you. [.linebr]#/# +
You have put them to shame [.linebr]#/# +
because God has despised them.

6 O that the salvation of Israel would come out of Zion! [.linebr]#/# +
When God brings back the captivity of his people, [.linebr]#/# +
Jacob shall rejoice and Israel shall be glad.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.1]*: Quoted in xref:#rom003-010[Romans 3:10]. *[v.2]*: Quoted in xref:#rom003-011[Romans 3:11]. *[v.3]*: Quoted in xref:#rom003-012[Romans 3:12].

[#psa054%breakable]
=== Psalm 54

[.outline.text-center]
_David, bemoaning the Ziphims, prays for salvation, 1-3. Upon his confidence in God's help he promises sacrifice, 4-7._

1 [_To the Chief Musician on Neginoth. Maschil. A Psalm of David: when the Ziphims came and said to Saul, "Does David not hide himself with us?"_]

Save me, O God, by your name, [.linebr]#/# +
and judge me by your strength.

2 Hear my prayer, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
Give ear to the words of my mouth.

3 For strangers have risen up against me, [.linebr]#/# +
and oppressors seek after my soul. [.linebr]#/# +
They have not set God before them. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

4 Behold, God is my helper. [.linebr]#/# +
The Lord is with those who uphold my soul.

5 He will reward evil to my enemies. [.linebr]#/# +
Cut them off in your truth.

6 I will freely sacrifice to you. [.linebr]#/# +
I will praise your name, O LORD, for it is good.

7 For he has delivered me out of all trouble, [.linebr]#/# +
and my eye has seen its desire upon my enemies.

[#psa055%breakable]
=== Psalm 55

[.outline.text-center]
_David, in his prayer, bemoans his fearful case, 1-8. He prays against his enemies, of whose wickedness and treachery he makes accusation, 9-15. He comforts himself in God's preservation of him and confusion of his enemies, 16-23._

1 [_To the Chief Musician on Neginoth. Maschil. A Psalm of David._]

Give ear to my prayer, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
and do not hide yourself from my supplication.

2 Attend to me and hear me. [.linebr]#/# +
I mourn in my complaint and make a noise,

3 Because of the voice of the enemy, [.linebr]#/# +
because of the oppression of the wicked. [.linebr]#/# +
For they cast iniquity upon me, [.linebr]#/# +
and in wrath they hate me.

4 My heart is severely pained within me, [.linebr]#/# +
and the terrors of death have fallen upon me.

5 Fearfulness and trembling have come upon me, [.linebr]#/# +
and horror has overwhelmed me.

6 And I said, "O that I had wings like a dove! [.linebr]#/# +
For then I would fly away and be at rest.

7 Behold, then I would wander far off [.linebr]#/# +
and remain in the wilderness." [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

8 "I would hasten my escape [.linebr]#/# +
from the windy storm and tempest."

9 Destroy, O Lord, and divide their languages, [.linebr]#/# +
for I have seen violence and strife in the city.

10 Day and night they go around it upon its walls. [.linebr]#/# +
Mischief and sorrow are also in the midst of it.

11 Wickedness is in the midst of it. [.linebr]#/# +
Deceit and guile do not depart from her streets.

12 For it was not an enemy who reproached me— [.linebr]#/# +
then I could have borne it— [.linebr]#/# +
neither was it he who hated me who magnified himself against me— [.linebr]#/# +
then I would have hid myself from him.

13 But it was you, a man my equal, [.linebr]#/# +
my guide, and my acquaintance.

14 We took sweet counsel together [.linebr]#/# +
and walked to the house of God in company.

15 Let death seize upon them, [.linebr]#/# +
and let them go down alive into hell, [.linebr]#/# +
for wickedness is in their dwellings and among them.

16 As for me, I will call upon God, [.linebr]#/# +
and the LORD will save me.

17 Evening, morning, and at noon, I will pray and cry aloud, [.linebr]#/# +
and he will hear my voice.

18 He has delivered my soul in peace [.linebr]#/# +
from the battle that was against me, [.linebr]#/# +
for there were many with me.

19 God will hear and afflict them, [.linebr]#/# +
even he who abides of old. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+ +
Because they have no changes, [.linebr]#/# +
therefore they do not fear God.

20 He has put forth his hands [.linebr]#/# +
against those who are at peace with him. [.linebr]#/# +
He has broken his covenant.

21 The words of his mouth were smoother than butter, [.linebr]#/# +
but war was in his heart. [.linebr]#/# +
His words were softer than oil, [.linebr]#/# +
yet they were drawn swords.

[[psa055-022]]22 Cast your burden upon the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and he will sustain you. [.linebr]#/# +
He will never allow the righteous to be moved.

23 But you, O God, will bring them down [.linebr]#/# +
into the pit of destruction. [.linebr]#/# +
Bloody and deceitful men [.linebr]#/# +
shall not live out half their days. [.linebr]#/# +
But I will trust in you.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.22]*: Quoted in xref:#fpe005-007[1st Peter 5:7].

[#psa056%breakable]
=== Psalm 56

[.outline.text-center]
_David, praying to God in confidence of his word, bemoans his enemies, 1-8. He professes his confidence in God's word and promises to praise him, 9-13._

1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Jonathelem-rechokim. Michtam of David: when the Philistines took him in Gath._]

Be merciful to me, O God, for man would swallow me up. [.linebr]#/# +
Fighting daily he oppresses me.

2 My enemies would swallow me up daily, [.linebr]#/# +
for they are many who fight against me, O Most High.

3 In the time when I am afraid, [.linebr]#/# +
I will trust in you.

4 In God (I will praise his word), [.linebr]#/# +
in God I have put my trust. [.linebr]#/# +
I will not fear [.linebr]#/# +
what flesh can do to me.

5 Every day they wrest my words. [.linebr]#/# +
All their thoughts are against me for evil.

6 They assemble themselves, they hide themselves, [.linebr]#/# +
they mark my steps [.linebr]#/# +
when they wait for my soul.

7 Shall they escape by iniquity? [.linebr]#/# +
In your anger cast down the people, O God.

8 You number my wanderings. [.linebr]#/# +
Put my tears into your bottle. [.linebr]#/# +
Are they not in your book?

9 When I cry to you, my enemies shall turn back. [.linebr]#/# +
I know this, for God is for me.

10 In God (I will praise his word), [.linebr]#/# +
in the LORD (I will praise his word),

11 In God I have put my trust. [.linebr]#/# +
I will not be afraid [.linebr]#/# +
of what man can do to me.

12 Your vows are upon me, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
I will render praises to you.

13 For you have delivered my soul from death. [.linebr]#/# +
Will you not deliver my feet from falling [.linebr]#/# +
so that I may walk before God [.linebr]#/# +
in the light of the living?

[#psa057%breakable]
=== Psalm 57

[.outline.text-center]
_David, in prayer fleeing to God, bemoans his dangerous case, 1-6. He encourages himself to praise God, 7-11._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. Al-taschith. Michtam of David: when he fled from Saul in the cave._]

Be merciful to me, O God, be merciful to me, [.linebr]#/# +
for my soul trusts in you. [.linebr]#/# +
Even in the shadow of your wings I will make my refuge [.linebr]#/# +
until these calamities have passed.

2 I will cry to God most high, [.linebr]#/# +
to God who performs all things for me.

3 He shall send from heaven and save me [.linebr]#/# +
from the reproach of him who would swallow me up. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+ +
God shall send forth his mercy and his truth.

4 My soul is among lions. [.linebr]#/# +
And I lie even among those who are set on fire, [.linebr]#/# +
even the sons of men, whose teeth are spears and arrows [.linebr]#/# +
and their tongue a sharp sword.

5 Be exalted, O God, above the heavens. [.linebr]#/# +
Let your glory be above all the earth.

6 They have prepared a net for my steps. [.linebr]#/# +
My soul is bowed down. [.linebr]#/# +
They have dug a pit before me, [.linebr]#/# +
into the midst of which they have fallen themselves. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

7 My heart is fixed, O God, my heart is fixed. [.linebr]#/# +
I will sing and give praise.

8 Awake, my glory. Awake, psaltery and harp. [.linebr]#/# +
I myself will awake early.

9 I will praise you, O Lord, among the people. [.linebr]#/# +
I will sing to you among the nations.

10 For your mercy is great to the heavens [.linebr]#/# +
and your truth to the clouds.

11 Be exalted, O God, above the heavens. [.linebr]#/# +
Let your glory be above all the earth.

[#psa058%breakable]
=== Psalm 58

[.outline.text-center]
_David reproves wicked judges, 1, 2; describes the nature of the wicked, 3-5; devotes them to God's judgments, 6-9; at which the righteous shall rejoice, 10, 11._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. Al-taschith. Michtam of David._]

Do you indeed speak righteousness, O congregation? [.linebr]#/# +
Do you judge uprightly, O sons of men?

2 Indeed, in heart you work wickedness. [.linebr]#/# +
You weigh the violence of your hands in the earth.

3 The wicked are estranged from their birth. [.linebr]#/# +
They go astray as soon as they are born, speaking lies.

4 Their poison is like the poison of a serpent. [.linebr]#/# +
They are like the deaf adder that stops her ear,

5 Which will not listen to the voice of charmers, [.linebr]#/# +
charming ever so wisely.

6 Break their teeth, O God, in their mouth. [.linebr]#/# +
Break out the great teeth of the young lions, O LORD.

7 Let them melt away as waters which run continually. [.linebr]#/# +
When he bends his bow to shoot his arrows, [.linebr]#/# +
let them be as though they were cut off.

8 As a snail which melts, [.linebr]#/# +
let every one of them pass away [.linebr]#/# +
like the untimely birth of a woman [.linebr]#/# +
so that they may not see the sun.

9 Before your pots can feel the thorns, [.linebr]#/# +
he shall take them away as with a whirlwind, [.linebr]#/# +
both living, and in his wrath.

10 The righteous shall rejoice when he sees the vengeance. [.linebr]#/# +
He shall wash his feet in the blood of the wicked,

11 So that a man shall say, [.linebr]#/# +
"Truly there is a reward for the righteous. [.linebr]#/# +
Truly he is a God who judges in the earth."

[#psa059%breakable]
=== Psalm 59

[.outline.text-center]
_David prays to be delivered from his enemies, 1-5, whose desperate wickedness he describes, 6, 7. He trusts in God, 8-10. He prays against them, 11-15. He praises God, 16, 17._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. Al-taschith. Michtam of David: when Saul sent and they watched the house to kill him._]

Deliver me from my enemies, O my God. [.linebr]#/# +
Defend me from those who rise up against me.

2 Deliver me from the workers of iniquity [.linebr]#/# +
and save me from bloody men.

3 For behold, they lie in wait for my soul. [.linebr]#/# +
The mighty are gathered against me, [.linebr]#/# +
not for my transgression nor for my sin, O LORD.

4 They run and prepare themselves without my fault. [.linebr]#/# +
Awake to help me, and behold.

5 You therefore, O LORD God of hosts, the God of Israel, [.linebr]#/# +
awake to visit all the heathen. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not be merciful to any wicked transgressors. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

6 They return at evening. [.linebr]#/# +
They make a noise like a dog [.linebr]#/# +
and go throughout the city.

7 Behold, they belch out with their mouth. [.linebr]#/# +
Swords are in their lips, [.linebr]#/# +
for they say, "Who hears?"

8 But you, O LORD, shall laugh at them. [.linebr]#/# +
You shall have all the heathen in derision.

9 Because of his strength I will wait upon you, [.linebr]#/# +
for God is my defense.

10 As for my God, his mercy shall go before me. [.linebr]#/# +
God will let me see my desire upon my enemies.

11 Do not slay them, lest my people forget. [.linebr]#/# +
Scatter them by your power and bring them down, [.linebr]#/# +
O Lord our shield.

12 For the sin of their mouth and the words of their lips, [.linebr]#/# +
let them even be taken in their pride, [.linebr]#/# +
and also for cursing and lying which they speak.

13 Consume them in wrath, [.linebr]#/# +
consume them, so that they may not be. [.linebr]#/# +
And let them know that God rules in Jacob [.linebr]#/# +
to the ends of the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

14 And at evening let them return. [.linebr]#/# +
And let them make a noise like a dog [.linebr]#/# +
and go throughout the city.

15 Let them wander up and down for food [.linebr]#/# +
and wait all night if they are not satisfied.

16 But I will sing of your power. [.linebr]#/# +
I will even sing aloud of your mercy in the morning, [.linebr]#/# +
for you have been my defense [.linebr]#/# +
and refuge in the day of my trouble.

17 To you, O my strength, I will sing, [.linebr]#/# +
for God is my defense and the God of my mercy.

[#psa060%breakable]
=== Psalm 60

[.outline.text-center]
_David, bemoaning the desolation which had fallen on the land, 1-3, now upon better hope, prays for deliverance, 4, 5. Comforting himself in God's promises, he craves that help whereon he trusts, 6-12._

1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Shushan-eduth. Michtam of David for Teaching: when he strove with Aram-naharaim and with Aram-zobah, when Joab returned and smote twelve thousand of Edom in the valley of salt._]

O God, you have cast us off. [.linebr]#/# +
You have scattered us. [.linebr]#/# +
You have been displeased. [.linebr]#/# +
O turn yourself to us again.

2 You have made the earth to tremble. [.linebr]#/# +
You have broken it. [.linebr]#/# +
Heal its breaches, for it shakes.

3 You have shown your people hard things. [.linebr]#/# +
You have made us to drink the wine of astonishment.

4 You have given a banner to those who fear you [.linebr]#/# +
so that it may be displayed because of the truth. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

5 So that your beloved may be delivered, [.linebr]#/# +
save with your right hand and hear me.

6 God has spoken in his holiness, "I will rejoice. [.linebr]#/# +
I will divide Shechem [.linebr]#/# +
and measure out the valley of Succoth.

7 Gilead is mine. And Manasseh is mine. [.linebr]#/# +
Ephraim also is the strength of my head. [.linebr]#/# +
Judah is my lawgiver.

8 Moab is my wash-pot. [.linebr]#/# +
Over Edom I will cast out my shoe. [.linebr]#/# +
Over Philistia I shout in triumph."

9 Who will bring me into the strong city? [.linebr]#/# +
Who will lead me into Edom?

10 Will you not, O God, who had cast us off, [.linebr]#/# +
and you, O God, who did not go out with our armies?

11 Give us help from trouble, [.linebr]#/# +
for the help of man is vain.

12 Through God we shall do valiantly, [.linebr]#/# +
for he will tread down our enemies.

[#psa061%breakable]
=== Psalm 61

[.outline.text-center]
_David flees to God upon his former experience, 1-3. He vows perpetual service to him because of his promises, 4-8._

1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Neginah. A Psalm of David._]

Hear my cry, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
Attend to my prayer.

2 From the end of the earth I will cry to you [.linebr]#/# +
when my heart is overwhelmed. [.linebr]#/# +
Lead me to the rock that is higher than I am.

3 For you have been a shelter for me [.linebr]#/# +
and a strong tower from the enemy.

4 I will abide in your tabernacle forever. [.linebr]#/# +
I will trust in the covert of your wings. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

5 For you, O God, have heard my vows. [.linebr]#/# +
You have given me the heritage [.linebr]#/# +
of those who fear your name.

6 You will prolong the king's life. [.linebr]#/# +
His years shall be like many generations.

7 He shall abide before God forever. [.linebr]#/# +
O prepare mercy and truth, [.linebr]#/# +
which may preserve him.

8 So I will sing praise to your name forever [.linebr]#/# +
when I daily perform my vows.

[#psa062%breakable]
=== Psalm 62

[.outline.text-center]
_David, professing his confidence in God, discourages his enemies, 1-4. In the same confidence he encourages the godly, 5-8. No trust is to be put in worldly things, 9, 10. Power and mercy belong to God, 11, 12._

1 [_To the Chief Musician, to Jeduthun. A Psalm of David._]

Truly my soul waits upon God. [.linebr]#/# +
My salvation comes from him.

2 Only he is my rock and my salvation. [.linebr]#/# +
He is my defense. [.linebr]#/# +
I shall not be greatly moved.

3 How long will you devise mischief against a man? [.linebr]#/# +
All of you shall be slain. [.linebr]#/# +
You shall be like a bowing wall and like a tottering fence.

4 They only consult to cast him down from his excellence. [.linebr]#/# +
They delight in lies. [.linebr]#/# +
They bless with their mouth, but they curse inwardly. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

5 My soul, wait only upon God, [.linebr]#/# +
for my expectation is from him.

6 Only he is my rock and my salvation. [.linebr]#/# +
He is my defense. [.linebr]#/# +
I shall not be moved.

7 In God is my salvation and my glory. [.linebr]#/# +
The rock of my strength, my refuge is in God.

8 Trust in him at all times, you people. [.linebr]#/# +
Pour out your heart before him. [.linebr]#/# +
God is a refuge for us. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

9 Surely men of low degree are vanity, [.linebr]#/# +
and men of high degree are a lie. [.linebr]#/# +
They will be laid in the balance. [.linebr]#/# +
They are altogether lighter than vanity.

10 Do not trust in oppression, [.linebr]#/# +
and do not become vain in robbery. [.linebr]#/# +
If riches increase, do not set your heart upon them.

11 God has spoken once, [.linebr]#/# +
and twice I have heard this: [.linebr]#/# +
that power belongs to God,

[[psa062-012]]12 And to you, O Lord, belongs mercy. [.linebr]#/# +
For you render to every man according to his work.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.12]*: Quoted in xref:#mth016-027[Matthew 16:27]; xref:#rom002-006[Romans 2:6].

[#psa063%breakable]
=== Psalm 63

[.outline.text-center]
_David's thirst for God, 1-3. His manner of blessing God, 4-8. His confidence of his enemies' destruction and of his own safety, 9-11._

1 [_A Psalm of David: when he was in the wilderness of Judah._]

O God, you are my God. [.linebr]#/# +
Early I will seek you. [.linebr]#/# +
My soul thirsts for you. [.linebr]#/# +
My flesh longs for you [.linebr]#/# +
in a dry and thirsty land where there is no water.

2 Thus I have seen you in the sanctuary, [.linebr]#/# +
seeing your power and your glory.

3 Because your loving-kindness is better than life, [.linebr]#/# +
my lips shall praise you.

4 Thus I will bless you while I live. [.linebr]#/# +
I will lift up my hands in your name.

5 My soul shall be satisfied as with marrow and fatness, [.linebr]#/# +
and my mouth shall praise you with joyful lips,

6 When I remember you upon my bed [.linebr]#/# +
and meditate on you in the night watches.

7 Because you have been my help, [.linebr]#/# +
therefore in the shadow of your wings I will rejoice.

8 My soul follows hard after you. [.linebr]#/# +
Your right hand upholds me.

9 But those who seek my soul to destroy it [.linebr]#/# +
shall go into the lower parts of the earth.

10 They shall fall by the sword. [.linebr]#/# +
They shall be a portion for foxes.

11 But the king shall rejoice in God. [.linebr]#/# +
Everyone who swears by him shall glory. [.linebr]#/# +
But the mouth of those who speak lies shall be stopped.

[#psa064%breakable]
=== Psalm 64

[.outline.text-center]
_David prays for preservation from the wicked, whom he describes, 1-6. He promises himself to see such an evident destruction of his enemies, as the righteous shall rejoice at it, 7-10._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

Hear my voice, O God, in my prayer. [.linebr]#/# +
Preserve my life from fear of the enemy.

2 Hide me from the secret counsel of the wicked, [.linebr]#/# +
from the insurrection of the workers of iniquity,

3 Who whet their tongue like a sword [.linebr]#/# +
and bend their bows to shoot their arrows, even bitter words,

4 So that they may shoot in secret at the perfect. [.linebr]#/# +
Suddenly they shoot at him and do not fear.

5 They encourage themselves in an evil matter. [.linebr]#/# +
They talk about laying snares secretly. [.linebr]#/# +
They say, "Who will see them?"

6 They search out iniquities. [.linebr]#/# +
They accomplish a diligent search. [.linebr]#/# +
Both the inward thought and the heart of every one of them is deep.

7 But God shall shoot at them with an arrow. [.linebr]#/# +
Suddenly they shall be wounded.

8 Thus they shall make their own tongue to fall upon themselves. [.linebr]#/# +
All who see them shall flee away.

9 And all men shall fear [.linebr]#/# +
and declare the work of God, [.linebr]#/# +
for they shall wisely consider his work.

10 The righteous shall be glad in the LORD and trust in him, [.linebr]#/# +
and all the upright in heart shall glory.

[#psa065%breakable]
=== Psalm 65

[.outline.text-center]
_David praises God for his grace, 1-3. The blessedness of God's chosen by reason of benefits, 4-13._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm and Song of David._]

Praise waits for you, O God, in Zion. [.linebr]#/# +
And to you the vow shall be performed.

2 O you who hear prayer, [.linebr]#/# +
to you all flesh shall come.

3 Iniquities prevail against me. [.linebr]#/# +
As for our transgressions, you shall purge them away.

4 Blessed is the man whom you choose and cause to approach you [.linebr]#/# +
so that he may dwell in your courts. [.linebr]#/# +
We shall be satisfied with the goodness of your house, [.linebr]#/# +
even of your holy temple.

5 By terrible things in righteousness you will answer us, [.linebr]#/# +
O God of our salvation. [.linebr]#/# +
You are the confidence of all the ends of the earth [.linebr]#/# +
and of those who are afar off upon the sea,

6 Who by his strength firmly sets the mountains, [.linebr]#/# +
being girded with power,

7 Who stills the noise of the seas, [.linebr]#/# +
the noise of their waves, [.linebr]#/# +
and the tumult of the people.

8 Also those who dwell in the uttermost parts are in awe of your signs. [.linebr]#/# +
You make the outgoings of the morning and evening to rejoice.

9 You visit the earth and water it. [.linebr]#/# +
You greatly enrich it with the river of God, [.linebr]#/# +
which is full of water. [.linebr]#/# +
You prepare their grain when you have thus provided for it.

10 You water its ridges abundantly. [.linebr]#/# +
You settle its furrows. [.linebr]#/# +
You make it soft with showers. [.linebr]#/# +
You bless its springing.

11 You crown the year with your goodness, [.linebr]#/# +
and your paths drop fatness.

12 They drop upon the pastures of the wilderness, [.linebr]#/# +
and the little hills rejoice on every side.

13 The pastures are clothed with flocks. [.linebr]#/# +
The valleys are also covered over with grain. [.linebr]#/# +
They shout for joy. They also sing.

[#psa066%breakable]
=== Psalm 66

[.outline.text-center]
_David exhorts to praise God, 1-4; to observe his great works, 5-7; to bless him for his gracious benefits, 8-11. He vows for himself religious service to God, 12-15. He declares God's special goodness to himself, 16-20._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Song or Psalm._]

Make a joyful noise to God, all you lands.

2 Sing forth the honor of his name. [.linebr]#/# +
Make his praise glorious.

3 Say to God, "How awesome you are in your works! [.linebr]#/# +
Through the greatness of your power [.linebr]#/# +
your enemies shall submit themselves to you.

4 All the earth shall worship you [.linebr]#/# +
and sing to you. [.linebr]#/# +
They shall sing to your name." [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

5 Come and see the works of God. [.linebr]#/# +
He is awesome in his doings toward the children of men.

6 He turned the sea into dry land. [.linebr]#/# +
They went through the flood on foot. [.linebr]#/# +
There we rejoiced in him.

7 He rules by his power forever. [.linebr]#/# +
His eyes behold the nations. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not let the rebellious exalt themselves. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

8 O bless our God, you people, [.linebr]#/# +
and make the voice of his praise to be heard,

9 Who holds our soul in life [.linebr]#/# +
and does not allow our feet to be moved.

10 For you, O God, have proved us. [.linebr]#/# +
You have tried us like silver is tried.

11 You have brought us into the net. [.linebr]#/# +
You have laid affliction upon our loins.

12 You have caused men to ride over our heads. [.linebr]#/# +
We went through fire and through water, [.linebr]#/# +
but you brought us out into a wealthy place.

13 I will go into your house with burnt-offerings. [.linebr]#/# +
I will pay you my vows,

14 Which my lips have uttered [.linebr]#/# +
and my mouth has spoken when I was in trouble.

15 I will offer to you burnt-sacrifices of fattened calves [.linebr]#/# +
with the incense of rams. [.linebr]#/# +
I will offer bulls with goats. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

16 Come and hear, all you who fear God, [.linebr]#/# +
and I will declare what he has done for my soul.

17 I cried to him with my mouth, [.linebr]#/# +
and he was extolled with my tongue.

18 If I regard iniquity in my heart, [.linebr]#/# +
the Lord will not hear me.

19 But truly God has heard me. [.linebr]#/# +
He has attended to the voice of my prayer.

20 Blessed be God [.linebr]#/# +
who has not turned away my prayer [.linebr]#/# +
or his mercy from me.

[#psa067%breakable]
=== Psalm 67

[.outline.text-center]
_A prayer for the enlargement of God's kingdom, 1, 2; to the joy of the people, 3-5; and the increase of God's blessings, 6, 7._

1 [_To the Chief Musician on Neginoth. A Psalm or Song._]

May God be merciful to us and bless us [.linebr]#/# +
and cause his face to shine upon us. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

2 Then your way may be known upon earth, [.linebr]#/# +
your saving health among all nations.

3 Let the people praise you, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
Let all the people praise you.

4 O let the nations be glad and sing for joy, [.linebr]#/# +
for you shall judge the people righteously [.linebr]#/# +
and govern the nations upon earth. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

5 Let the people praise you, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
Let all the people praise you.

6 Then the earth shall yield her increase, [.linebr]#/# +
and God, even our own God, will bless us.

7 God will bless us, [.linebr]#/# +
and all the ends of the earth shall fear him.

[#psa068%breakable]
=== Psalm 68

[.outline.text-center]
_A prayer at the removing of the ark, 1-3. An exhortation to praise God for his mercies, 4-6; for his care of the church, 7-18; for his great works, 19-35._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm or Song of David._]

Let God arise. Let his enemies be scattered. [.linebr]#/# +
Let those who also hate him flee before him.

2 As smoke is driven away, so drive them away. [.linebr]#/# +
As wax melts before the fire, [.linebr]#/# +
so let the wicked perish at the presence of God.

3 But let the righteous be glad. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them rejoice before God. [.linebr]#/# +
Indeed, let them exceedingly rejoice.

4 Sing to God, sing praises to his name. [.linebr]#/# +
Extol him who rides upon the heavens [.linebr]#/# +
by his name, YAH, [.linebr]#/# +
and rejoice before him.

5 A father of the fatherless and a judge of the widows [.linebr]#/# +
is God in his holy habitation.

6 God sets the solitary in families. [.linebr]#/# +
He brings out those who are bound with chains. [.linebr]#/# +
But the rebellious dwell in a dry land.

7 O God, when you went forth before your people, [.linebr]#/# +
when you marched through the wilderness, [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

8 The earth shook, [.linebr]#/# +
the heavens also dropped at the presence of God. [.linebr]#/# +
Even Sinai itself was moved [.linebr]#/# +
at the presence of God, the God of Israel.

9 You, O God, sent a plentiful rain, [.linebr]#/# +
by which you confirmed your inheritance when it was weary.

10 Your congregation has dwelt therein. [.linebr]#/# +
You, O God, have prepared your goodness for the poor.

11 The Lord gave the word. [.linebr]#/# +
The company of those who published it was great.

12 Kings of armies fled apace. [.linebr]#/# +
And she who waited at home divided the plunder.

13 Though you have lain among the sheep-folds, [.linebr]#/# +
the wings of a dove are covered with silver, [.linebr]#/# +
and her feathers with yellow gold.

14 When the Almighty scattered kings in it, [.linebr]#/# +
it was white as snow in Salmon.

15 The hill of God is like the hill of Bashan, [.linebr]#/# +
a high hill like the hill of Bashan.

16 Why do you leap, you lofty hills? [.linebr]#/# +
This is the hill which God desires to dwell in. [.linebr]#/# +
Indeed, the LORD will dwell in it forever.

17 The chariots of God are twenty thousand, [.linebr]#/# +
even thousands of angels. [.linebr]#/# +
The Lord is among them. [.linebr]#/# +
Sinai is in the holy place.

[[psa068-018]]18 You have ascended on high. [.linebr]#/# +
You have led captivity captive. [.linebr]#/# +
You have received gifts among men, [.linebr]#/# +
even among the rebellious also, [.linebr]#/# +
so that the LORD God might dwell with them.

19 Blessed be the Lord who daily loads us with benefits, [.linebr]#/# +
even the God of our salvation. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

20 He who is our God is the God of salvation. [.linebr]#/# +
And the issues from death belong to GOD the Lord.

21 But God will wound the head of his enemies [.linebr]#/# +
and the hairy scalp of such a one as goes on still in his trespasses.

22 The Lord said, "I will bring back from Bashan, [.linebr]#/# +
I will bring my people back from the depths of the sea,

23 So that your foot may be dipped [.linebr]#/# +
in the blood of your enemies [.linebr]#/# +
and the tongue of your dogs in the same."

24 They have seen your goings, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
even the goings of my God, my King, in the sanctuary.

25 The singers went before. [.linebr]#/# +
The players on instruments followed after. [.linebr]#/# +
Among them were the young women playing with tambourines.

26 Bless God in the congregations, [.linebr]#/# +
even the Lord, from the fountain of Israel.

27 There is the youngest, Benjamin, with their ruler, [.linebr]#/# +
the princes of Judah and their counsel, [.linebr]#/# +
the princes of Zebulun, and the princes of Naphtali.

28 Your God has commanded your strength. [.linebr]#/# +
Strengthen, O God, that which you have wrought for us.

29 Because of your temple at Jerusalem, [.linebr]#/# +
kings shall bring presents to you.

30 Rebuke the wild beast of the reeds, [.linebr]#/# +
the multitude of the bulls with the calves of the people, [.linebr]#/# +
until each submits himself with pieces of silver. [.linebr]#/# +
Scatter the people who delight in war.

31 Princes shall come out of Egypt. [.linebr]#/# +
Cush shall soon stretch out her hands to God.

32 Sing to God, you kingdoms of the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
O sing praises to the Lord, [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

33 To him who rides upon the heavens of heavens, which are of old. [.linebr]#/# +
Behold, he sends out his voice—a mighty voice.

34 Ascribe strength to God. [.linebr]#/# +
His excellence is over Israel, [.linebr]#/# +
and his strength is in the clouds.

35 O God, you are awesome out of your holy places. [.linebr]#/# +
The God of Israel is he who gives strength and power to his people. [.linebr]#/# +
Blessed be God.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.18]*: Quoted in xref:#eph004-008[Ephesians 4:8].

[#psa069%breakable]
=== Psalm 69

[.outline.text-center]
_David bemoans his affliction, 1-12. He prays for deliverance, 13-21. He devotes his enemies to destruction, 22-29. He praises God with thanksgiving, 30-36._

1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Shoshannim. A Psalm of David._]

Save me, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
for the waters have come to my soul.

2 I sink in deep mire [.linebr]#/# +
where there is no standing. [.linebr]#/# +
I have come into deep waters [.linebr]#/# +
where the floods overflow me.

3 I am weary of my crying. [.linebr]#/# +
My throat is dried. [.linebr]#/# +
My eyes fail while I wait for my God.

[[psa069-004]]4 Those who hate me without a cause [.linebr]#/# +
are more than the hairs of my head. [.linebr]#/# +
Those who would destroy me are mighty, [.linebr]#/# +
being my enemies without cause. [.linebr]#/# +
Then I restored that which I did not take away.

5 O God, you know my foolishness [.linebr]#/# +
and my sins are not hid from you.

6 Do not let those who wait on you, [.linebr]#/# +
O Lord GOD of hosts, [.linebr]#/# +
be ashamed for my sake. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not let those who seek you [.linebr]#/# +
be confounded for my sake, [.linebr]#/# +
O God of Israel.

7 Because for your sake I have borne reproach. [.linebr]#/# +
Shame has covered my face.

8 I have become a stranger to my brothers [.linebr]#/# +
and a foreigner to my mother's children.

[[psa069-009]]9 For the zeal of your house has eaten me up. [.linebr]#/# +
And the reproaches of those who reproached you [.linebr]#/# +
have fallen upon me.

10 When I wept and chastened my soul with fasting, [.linebr]#/# +
that was to my reproach.

11 I also made sackcloth my garment [.linebr]#/# +
and became a proverb to them.

12 Those who sit in the gate speak against me. [.linebr]#/# +
I was the song of the drunkards.

13 But as for me, my prayer is to you, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
in an acceptable time. [.linebr]#/# +
O God, in the multitude of your mercy, [.linebr]#/# +
hear me in the truth of your salvation.

14 Deliver me out of the mire [.linebr]#/# +
and do not let me sink. [.linebr]#/# +
Let me be delivered from those who hate me [.linebr]#/# +
and out of the deep waters.

15 Do not let the flood waters overflow me, [.linebr]#/# +
neither let the deep swallow me up [.linebr]#/# +
or the pit shut her mouth upon me.

16 Hear me, O LORD, for your loving-kindness is good. [.linebr]#/# +
Turn to me according to the multitude of your tender mercies.

17 And do not hide your face from your servant, [.linebr]#/# +
for I am in trouble. Hear me speedily.

18 Draw near to my soul and redeem it. [.linebr]#/# +
Deliver me because of my enemies.

19 You have known my reproach, my shame, and my dishonor. [.linebr]#/# +
My adversaries are all before you.

20 Reproach has broken my heart, and I am full of heaviness. [.linebr]#/# +
And I looked for some to take pity, but there was none, [.linebr]#/# +
and for comforters, but I found none.

21 They also gave me gall for my food, [.linebr]#/# +
and in my thirst they gave me vinegar to drink.

[[psa069-022]]22 Let their table become a snare before them. [.linebr]#/# +
And that which should have been for their welfare, [.linebr]#/# +
let it become a trap.

[[psa069-023]]23 Let their eyes be darkened so that they do not see, [.linebr]#/# +
and make their loins continually shake.

24 Pour out your indignation upon them, [.linebr]#/# +
and let your wrathful anger take hold of them.

[[psa069-025]]25 Let their habitation be desolate, [.linebr]#/# +
and let no one dwell in their tents.

26 For they persecute him whom you have smitten [.linebr]#/# +
and talk to the grief of those whom you have wounded.

27 Add iniquity to their iniquity. [.linebr]#/# +
And do not let them come into your righteousness.

28 Let them be blotted out of the book of the living [.linebr]#/# +
and not be written with the righteous.

29 But I am poor and sorrowful. [.linebr]#/# +
Let your salvation, O God, set me up on high.

30 I will praise the name of God with a song [.linebr]#/# +
and will magnify him with thanksgiving.

31 This also shall please the LORD better than an ox [.linebr]#/# +
or bull that has horns and hooves.

32 The humble shall see this and be glad. [.linebr]#/# +
And you who seek God, your heart shall live.

33 For the LORD hears the poor [.linebr]#/# +
and does not despise his prisoners.

34 Let the heaven and earth praise him, [.linebr]#/# +
the seas and everything that moves therein.

35 For God will save Zion and build the cities of Judah [.linebr]#/# +
so that they may dwell there and have it in possession.

36 The offspring of his servants shall also inherit it. [.linebr]#/# +
And those who love his name shall dwell therein.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.4]*: Reference, xref:#jhn015-025[John 15:25]. *[v.9]*: Quoted in xref:#jhn002-017[John 2:17]; xref:#rom015-003[Romans 15:3]. *[v.22]*: Quoted in xref:#rom011-009[Romans 11:9]. *[v.23]*: Quoted in xref:#rom011-010[Romans 11:10]. *[v.25]*: Quoted in xref:#act001-020[Acts 1:20].

[#psa070%breakable]
=== Psalm 70

[.outline.text-center]
_David solicits God to the speedy destruction of the wicked and the preservation of the godly, 1-5._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David: to bring to remembrance._]

Make haste, O God, to deliver me. [.linebr]#/# +
Make haste to help me, O LORD.

2 Let them be ashamed and confounded [.linebr]#/# +
who seek after my soul. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them be turned backward and put to shame [.linebr]#/# +
who desire my hurt.

3 Let them be turned back for a reward of their shame [.linebr]#/# +
who say, "Aha, aha."

4 Let all those who seek you rejoice and be glad in you. [.linebr]#/# +
And let those who love your salvation say continually, [.linebr]#/# +
"Let God be magnified."

5 But I am poor and needy. [.linebr]#/# +
Make haste to me, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
You are my help and my deliverer. [.linebr]#/# +
O LORD, make no delay.

[#psa071%breakable]
=== Psalm 71

[.outline.text-center]
_David, in confidence of faith and experience of God's favor, prays both for himself and against the enemies of his soul, 1-13. He promises constancy, 14-16. He prays for perseverance, 17, 18. He praises God and promises to do it cheerfully, 19-24._

1 In you, O LORD, I put my trust. [.linebr]#/# +
Let me never be put to shame.

2 Deliver me in your righteousness and cause me to escape. [.linebr]#/# +
Incline your ear to me and save me.

3 Be my strong habitation to which I may continually resort. [.linebr]#/# +
You have given commandment to save me, [.linebr]#/# +
for you are my rock and my fortress.

4 Deliver me, O my God, from the hand of the wicked, [.linebr]#/# +
from the hand of the unrighteous and cruel man.

5 For you are my hope, O Lord GOD. [.linebr]#/# +
You are my trust from my youth.

6 I have been sustained by you from my birth. [.linebr]#/# +
You are he who brought me into life. [.linebr]#/# +
My praise shall be continually of you.

7 I have become a wonder to many, [.linebr]#/# +
but you are my strong refuge.

8 Let my mouth be filled with your praise [.linebr]#/# +
and with your honor all the day.

9 Do not cast me off in the time of old age. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not forsake me when my strength fails.

10 For my enemies speak against me, [.linebr]#/# +
and those who lie in wait for my soul take counsel together,

11 Saying, "God has forsaken him. [.linebr]#/# +
Persecute and take him, for there is no one to deliver him."

12 O God, do not be far from me. [.linebr]#/# +
O my God, make haste for my help.

13 Let them be confounded and consumed [.linebr]#/# +
who are adversaries to my soul. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them be covered with reproach and dishonor [.linebr]#/# +
who seek my hurt.

14 But I will hope continually [.linebr]#/# +
and will praise you more and more.

15 My mouth shall show forth your righteousness [.linebr]#/# +
and your salvation all the day, [.linebr]#/# +
for I do not know the numbers thereof.

16 I will go in the strength of the Lord GOD. [.linebr]#/# +
I will make mention of your righteousness, even of yours only.

17 O God, you have taught me from my youth, [.linebr]#/# +
and until now I have declared your wondrous works.

18 And even when I am old and gray-headed, [.linebr]#/# +
O God, do not forsake me, [.linebr]#/# +
until I have shown your strength to this generation [.linebr]#/# +
and your power to everyone who is to come.

19 Your righteousness also, O God, is very high, [.linebr]#/# +
who have done great things. O God, who is like you?

20 You, who have shown me great and severe troubles, [.linebr]#/# +
will revive me again [.linebr]#/# +
and bring me back from the depths of the earth.

21 You will increase my greatness [.linebr]#/# +
and comfort me on every side.

22 I will also praise you with the psaltery, [.linebr]#/# +
even your truth, O my God. [.linebr]#/# +
To you I will sing with the harp, [.linebr]#/# +
O Holy One of Israel.

23 My lips shall greatly rejoice when I sing to you, [.linebr]#/# +
along with my soul which you have redeemed.

24 My tongue shall also talk [.linebr]#/# +
of your righteousness all the day long. [.linebr]#/# +
For they are confounded, [.linebr]#/# +
for they are brought to shame who seek my hurt.

[#psa072%breakable]
=== Psalm 72

[.outline.text-center]
_David, praying for Solomon, shows the goodness and glory of his kingdom, and in type of Christ's kingdom, 1-17. He blesses God, 18-20._

1 [_A Psalm for Solomon._]

Give the king your judgments, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
and your righteousness to the king's son.

2 He shall judge your people with righteousness [.linebr]#/# +
and your poor with judgment.

3 The mountains shall bring peace to the people, [.linebr]#/# +
and the little hills, by righteousness.

4 He shall judge the poor of the people. [.linebr]#/# +
He shall save the children of the needy [.linebr]#/# +
and break the oppressor in pieces.

5 They shall fear you as long as the sun and moon endure, [.linebr]#/# +
throughout all generations.

6 He shall come down like rain upon the mown grass, [.linebr]#/# +
like showers that water the earth.

7 In his days the righteous shall flourish, [.linebr]#/# +
and abundance of peace so long as the moon endures.

8 He shall also have dominion from sea to sea [.linebr]#/# +
and from the river to the ends of the earth.

9 Those who dwell in the wilderness shall bow before him, [.linebr]#/# +
and his enemies shall lick the dust.

10 The kings of Tarshish and of the islands shall bring presents. [.linebr]#/# +
The kings of Sheba and Seba shall offer gifts.

11 Indeed, all kings shall fall down before him. [.linebr]#/# +
All nations shall serve him.

12 For he shall deliver the needy when he cries, [.linebr]#/# +
and also the poor and him who has no helper.

13 He shall spare the poor and needy [.linebr]#/# +
and save the souls of the needy.

14 He shall redeem their soul from deceit and violence, [.linebr]#/# +
and precious shall be their blood in his sight.

15 And he shall live, and to him the gold of Sheba shall be given. [.linebr]#/# +
Prayer shall also be made for him continually, [.linebr]#/# +
and daily he shall be praised.

16 There shall be a handful of grain in the earth [.linebr]#/# +
upon the top of the mountains. [.linebr]#/# +
Its fruit shall shake like Lebanon. [.linebr]#/# +
And those of the city shall flourish like grass of the earth.

17 His name shall endure forever. [.linebr]#/# +
His name shall be continued as long as the sun. [.linebr]#/# +
And men shall be blessed in him. [.linebr]#/# +
All nations shall call him blessed.

18 Blessed be the LORD God, the God of Israel, [.linebr]#/# +
who only does wondrous things.

19 And blessed be his glorious name forever. [.linebr]#/# +
And let the whole earth be filled with his glory. [.linebr]#/# +
Amen and amen.

20 [_The prayers of David the son of Jesse have ended._]

[#psalms-book-3%breakable]
=== BOOK III

[#psa073%breakable]
=== Psalm 73

[.outline.text-center]
_The prophet, prevailing in a temptation, 1, shows the occasion thereof, the prosperity of the wicked, 2-12; the wound given thereby, diffidence, 13, 14; the victory over it, and knowledge of God's purpose in destroying the wicked and sustaining the righteous, 15-28._

1 [_A Psalm of Asaph._]

Truly God is good to Israel, [.linebr]#/# +
even to those who are of a clean heart.

2 But as for me, my feet were almost gone. [.linebr]#/# +
My steps had well near slipped.

3 For I was envious at the foolish [.linebr]#/# +
when I saw the prosperity of the wicked.

4 For there are no pangs in their death, [.linebr]#/# +
but their strength is firm.

5 They are not in trouble like other men, [.linebr]#/# +
neither are they afflicted like other men.

6 Therefore, pride encompasses them like a chain. [.linebr]#/# +
Violence covers them like a garment.

7 Their eyes stand out with fatness. [.linebr]#/# +
The imaginations of their heart transgressed.

8 They are corrupt and speak wickedly concerning oppression. [.linebr]#/# +
They speak loftily.

9 They set their mouth against the heavens [.linebr]#/# +
and their tongue walks through the earth.

10 Therefore, his people return here. [.linebr]#/# +
And waters of a full cup are wrung out to them.

11 And they say, "How does God know? [.linebr]#/# +
And is there knowledge in the Most High?"

12 Behold, these are the ungodly [.linebr]#/# +
who prosper in the world. They increase in riches.

13 Truly I have cleansed my heart in vain [.linebr]#/# +
and washed my hands in innocence.

14 For all the day long I have been afflicted [.linebr]#/# +
and chastened every morning.

15 If I had said, "I will speak thus," [.linebr]#/# +
behold, I would have offended against the generation of your children.

16 When I thought to know this, [.linebr]#/# +
it was too painful for me,

17 Until I went into the sanctuary of God. [.linebr]#/# +
Then I understood their end.

18 Surely you set them in slippery places. [.linebr]#/# +
You cast them down into destruction.

19 How they are brought into desolation in a moment! [.linebr]#/# +
They are utterly consumed with terrors.

20 As a dream when one awakes, [.linebr]#/# +
so, O Lord, when you awake, you will despise their image.

21 Thus my soul was grieved [.linebr]#/# +
and I was pricked in my heart.

22 So foolish was I, and ignorant. [.linebr]#/# +
I was like a beast before you.

23 Nevertheless, I am continually with you. [.linebr]#/# +
You have held me by my right hand.

24 You will guide me with your counsel, [.linebr]#/# +
and afterward, receive me to glory.

25 Whom do I have in heaven but you? [.linebr]#/# +
And there is no one upon earth that I desire besides you.

26 My flesh and my heart fails, [.linebr]#/# +
but God is the strength of my heart and my portion forever.

27 For behold, those who are far from you shall perish. [.linebr]#/# +
You have destroyed all those who go astray from you.

28 But it is good for me to draw near to God. [.linebr]#/# +
I have put my trust in the Lord GOD [.linebr]#/# +
so that I may declare all your works.

[#psa074%breakable]
=== Psalm 74

[.outline.text-center]
_The prophet bemoans the desolation of the sanctuary, 1-9. He moves God to help in consideration of his power, 10-17; of his reproachful enemies, of his children, and of his covenant, 18-23._

1 [_Maschil of Asaph._]

O God, why have you cast us off forever? [.linebr]#/# +
Why does your anger smoke against the sheep of your pasture?

2 Remember your congregation which you have purchased of old, [.linebr]#/# +
the rod of your inheritance which you have redeemed, [.linebr]#/# +
this mount Zion in which you have dwelt.

3 Lift up your feet to the perpetual desolations, [.linebr]#/# +
even all that the enemy has done wickedly in the sanctuary.

4 Your enemies roar in the midst of your congregations. [.linebr]#/# +
They set up their ensigns for signs.

5 They seemed like men who lifted up axes [.linebr]#/# +
upon the thick trees.

6 But now they break down its carved work [.linebr]#/# +
at once with axes and hammers.

7 They have cast fire into your sanctuary. [.linebr]#/# +
They have defiled by casting down [.linebr]#/# +
the dwelling-place of your name to the ground.

8 They said in their hearts, "Let us destroy them together." [.linebr]#/# +
They have burned up all the synagogues of God in the land.

9 We do not see our signs. [.linebr]#/# +
There is no longer any prophet, [.linebr]#/# +
neither is there among us any who knows how long.

10 O God, how long shall the adversary reproach? [.linebr]#/# +
Shall the enemy blaspheme your name forever?

11 Why do you withdraw your hand, [.linebr]#/# +
even your right hand? Pluck it out of your bosom.

12 For God is my King of old, [.linebr]#/# +
working salvation in the midst of the earth.

13 You divided the sea by your strength. [.linebr]#/# +
You broke the heads of the sea-monsters in the waters.

14 You broke the head of leviathan in pieces [.linebr]#/# +
and gave him to be food for the people inhabiting the wilderness.

15 You cleaved the fountain and the flood. [.linebr]#/# +
You dried up mighty rivers.

16 The day is yours, the night also is yours. [.linebr]#/# +
You have prepared the light and the sun.

17 You have set all the borders of the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
You have made summer and winter.

18 Remember this: the enemy has reproached, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and the foolish people have blasphemed your name.

19 O do not deliver the soul of your turtle-dove to the multitude of the wicked. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not forget the congregation of your poor forever.

20 Have respect to the covenant, [.linebr]#/# +
for the dark places of the earth are full of the habitations of cruelty.

21 O do not let the oppressed return ashamed. [.linebr]#/# +
Let the poor and needy praise your name.

22 Arise, O God, plead your own cause. [.linebr]#/# +
Remember how the foolish man reproaches you daily.

23 Do not forget the voice of your enemies. [.linebr]#/# +
The tumult of those who rise against you increases continually.

[#psa075%breakable]
=== Psalm 75

[.outline.text-center]
_The prophet praises God, 1. He promises to judge uprightly, 2, 3. He rebukes the proud by consideration of God's providence, 4-8. He praises God and promises to execute justice, 9, 10._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. Al-taschith. A Psalm or Song of Asaph._]

To you, O God, we give thanks, [.linebr]#/# +
to you we give thanks, for your name is near. [.linebr]#/# +
Your wondrous works we declare.

2 "When I receive the congregation, [.linebr]#/# +
I will judge uprightly.

3 The earth and all its inhabitants are dissolved. [.linebr]#/# +
I bear up its pillars." [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+
