4 "I said to the fools, 'Do not deal foolishly,' [.linebr]#/# +
and to the wicked, 'Do not lift up the horn.

5 Do not lift up your horn on high. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not speak with a stiff neck.'"

6 For promotion comes neither from the east, [.linebr]#/# +
nor from the west, nor from the south.

7 But God is the judge. [.linebr]#/# +
He puts down one and sets up another.

8 For in the hand of the LORD there is a cup, [.linebr]#/# +
and the wine is red. [.linebr]#/# +
It is full of mixture, [.linebr]#/# +
and he pours out of the same. [.linebr]#/# +
But all the wicked of the earth [.linebr]#/# +
shall wring out its dregs and drink them.

9 But I will declare it forever. [.linebr]#/# +
I will sing praises to the God of Jacob.

10 All the horns of the wicked I will also cut off, [.linebr]#/# +
but the horns of the righteous shall be exalted.

[#psa076%breakable]
=== Psalm 76

[.outline.text-center]
_A declaration of God's majesty in the church, 1-10. An exhortation to serve him reverently, 11, 12._

1 [_To the Chief Musician on Neginoth. A Psalm or Song of Asaph._]

God is known in Judah. [.linebr]#/# +
His name is great in Israel.

2 Also in Salem is his tabernacle [.linebr]#/# +
and his dwelling place in Zion.

3 There he broke the arrows of the bow, [.linebr]#/# +
the shield, the sword, and the battle. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

4 You are more glorious and excellent [.linebr]#/# +
than the mountains of prey.

5 The stout-hearted are plundered. [.linebr]#/# +
They have slept their sleep. [.linebr]#/# +
And none of the men of might have found their hands.

6 At your rebuke, O God of Jacob, [.linebr]#/# +
both the chariot and horse are cast into a dead sleep.

7 You, even you, are to be feared. [.linebr]#/# +
And who may stand in your sight when you are angry?

8 You caused judgment to be heard from heaven. [.linebr]#/# +
The earth feared and was still,

9 When God arose to judgment [.linebr]#/# +
to save all the meek of the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

10 Surely the wrath of man shall praise you. [.linebr]#/# +
The remainder of wrath you will restrain.

11 Make vows and fulfill them to the LORD your God. [.linebr]#/# +
Let all who are around him bring presents [.linebr]#/# +
to him who ought to be feared.

12 He shall cut off the spirit of princes. [.linebr]#/# +
He is fearful to the kings of the earth.

[#psa077%breakable]
=== Psalm 77

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist shows what fierce combat he had with diffidence, 1-9. The victory which he had by consideration of God's great and gracious works, 10-20._

1 [_To the Chief Musician, to Jeduthun. A Psalm of Asaph._]

I cried to God with my voice, [.linebr]#/# +
even to God with my voice, and he gave ear to me.

2 In the day of my trouble I sought the Lord. [.linebr]#/# +
My hand was stretched out in the night and did not cease. [.linebr]#/# +
My soul refused to be comforted.

3 I remembered God and was troubled. [.linebr]#/# +
I complained and my spirit was overwhelmed. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

4 You hold my eyes waking. [.linebr]#/# +
I am so troubled that I cannot speak.

5 I have considered the days of old, [.linebr]#/# +
the years of ancient times.

6 I call to remembrance my song in the night. [.linebr]#/# +
I mused within my heart, [.linebr]#/# +
and my spirit made diligent search.

7 Will the Lord cast off forever? [.linebr]#/# +
And will he no longer be favorable?

8 Is his mercy wholly gone forever? [.linebr]#/# +
Does his promise fail forevermore?

9 Has God forgotten to be gracious? [.linebr]#/# +
Has he in anger shut up his tender mercies? [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

10 And I said, "This is my infirmity, [.linebr]#/# +
but I will remember the years of the right hand of the Most High."

11 I will remember the works of the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Surely I will remember your wonders of old.

12 I will also meditate on all your work [.linebr]#/# +
and talk of your doings.

13 Your way, O God, is in the sanctuary. [.linebr]#/# +
Who is so great a God as our God?

14 You are the God who does wonders. [.linebr]#/# +
You have declared your strength among the people.

15 You have with your arm redeemed your people, [.linebr]#/# +
the sons of Jacob and Joseph. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

16 The waters saw you, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
the waters saw you. They were afraid. [.linebr]#/# +
The depths were also disturbed.

17 The clouds poured out water. [.linebr]#/# +
The skies sent out a sound. [.linebr]#/# +
Your arrows also went abroad.

18 The voice of your thunder was in the heaven. [.linebr]#/# +
The lightnings lightened the world. [.linebr]#/# +
The earth trembled and shook.

19 Your way is in the sea [.linebr]#/# +
and your paths in the great waters, [.linebr]#/# +
and your footsteps are not known.

20 You led your people like a flock [.linebr]#/# +
by the hand of Moses and Aaron.

[#psa078%breakable]
=== Psalm 78

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation both to learn and to preach the law of God, 1-8. The story of God's wrath against the incredulous and disobedient, 9-66. The Israelites being rejected, God chose Judah, Zion, and David, 67-72._

1 [_Maschil of Asaph._]

Give ear, O my people, to my law. [.linebr]#/# +
Incline your ear to the words of my mouth.

[[psa078-002]]2 I will open my mouth in a parable. [.linebr]#/# +
I will utter dark sayings of old,

3 Which we have heard and known [.linebr]#/# +
and our fathers have told us.

4 We will not hide them from their children, [.linebr]#/# +
showing to the generation to come the praises of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
his strength, and his wonderful works that he has done.

5 For he established a testimony in Jacob [.linebr]#/# +
and appointed a law in Israel, [.linebr]#/# +
which he commanded our fathers, [.linebr]#/# +
that they should make them known to their children,

6 So that the generation to come might know them, [.linebr]#/# +
even the children who should be born, [.linebr]#/# +
who should arise and declare them to their children;

7 So that they might set their hope in God [.linebr]#/# +
and not forget the works of God, [.linebr]#/# +
but keep his commandments,

8 And might not be as their fathers, [.linebr]#/# +
a stubborn and rebellious generation, [.linebr]#/# +
a generation that did not set their heart aright [.linebr]#/# +
and whose spirit was not steadfast with God.

9 The children of Ephraim, being armed and carrying bows, [.linebr]#/# +
turned back in the day of battle.

10 They did not keep the covenant of God [.linebr]#/# +
and refused to walk in his law,

11 And forgot his works [.linebr]#/# +
and his wonders that he had shown them.

12 He did marvelous things in the sight of their fathers, [.linebr]#/# +
in the land of Egypt, in the field of Zoan.

13 He divided the sea and caused them to pass through. [.linebr]#/# +
He made the waters to stand like a heap.

14 In the day-time he also led them with a cloud, [.linebr]#/# +
and all the night with a light of fire.

15 He cleaved the rocks in the wilderness [.linebr]#/# +
and gave them drink as abundant as the depths.

16 He also brought streams out of the rock [.linebr]#/# +
and caused waters to run down like rivers.

17 Yet they still went on to sin against him [.linebr]#/# +
by provoking the Most High in the wilderness.

18 And they tested God in their heart [.linebr]#/# +
by asking food for their desire.

19 They even spoke against God. [.linebr]#/# +
They said, "Can God furnish a table in the wilderness?

20 Behold, he smote the rock so that the waters gushed out [.linebr]#/# +
and the streams overflowed. [.linebr]#/# +
Can he give bread also? [.linebr]#/# +
Can he provide flesh for his people?"

21 Therefore, the LORD heard this and was angry. [.linebr]#/# +
Thus a fire was kindled against Jacob, [.linebr]#/# +
and anger also came up against Israel,

22 Because they did not believe in God [.linebr]#/# +
and did not trust in his salvation,

23 Though he commanded the clouds from above [.linebr]#/# +
and opened the doors of heaven,

[[psa078-024]]24 And rained down manna upon them to eat [.linebr]#/# +
and gave them the grain of heaven.

25 Man ate angels' food. [.linebr]#/# +
He sent them food to the full.

26 He caused an east wind to blow in the heaven. [.linebr]#/# +
And by his power he brought in the south wind.

27 He also rained flesh upon them like dust, [.linebr]#/# +
and feathered birds like the sand of the sea.

28 And he let it fall in the midst of their camp [.linebr]#/# +
around their habitations.

29 So they ate and were well filled, [.linebr]#/# +
for he gave them their own desire.

30 They were not estranged from their desire. [.linebr]#/# +
But while their food was still in their mouths,

31 The wrath of God came upon them [.linebr]#/# +
and slew the fattest of them [.linebr]#/# +
and smote down the chosen men of Israel.

32 For all this they sinned still [.linebr]#/# +
and did not believe in his wondrous works.

33 Therefore, he consumed their days in vanity [.linebr]#/# +
and their years in trouble.

34 When he slew them, they sought him. [.linebr]#/# +
They returned and inquired early after God.

35 And they remembered that God was their rock [.linebr]#/# +
and the high God their redeemer.

36 Nevertheless, they flattered him with their mouth [.linebr]#/# +
and they lied to him with their tongues.

37 For their heart was not right with him, [.linebr]#/# +
neither were they steadfast in his covenant.

38 But he, being full of compassion, [.linebr]#/# +
forgave their iniquity and did not destroy them. [.linebr]#/# +
Many a time he even turned his anger away [.linebr]#/# +
and did not stir up all his wrath.

39 For he remembered that they were only flesh, [.linebr]#/# +
a wind that passes away and does not return.

40 How often they provoked him in the wilderness [.linebr]#/# +
and grieved him in the desert!

41 They even turned back and tested God [.linebr]#/# +
and limited the Holy One of Israel.

42 They did not remember his hand, [.linebr]#/# +
nor the day when he delivered them from the enemy,

43 How he had wrought his signs in Egypt [.linebr]#/# +
and his wonders in the field of Zoan,

44 And had turned their rivers into blood, [.linebr]#/# +
and also their floods, so that they could not drink.

45 He sent swarms of flies among them which devoured them, [.linebr]#/# +
and also frogs which destroyed them.

46 He also gave their increase to the ravaging-locust [.linebr]#/# +
and their labor to the swarming-locust.

47 He destroyed their vines with hail [.linebr]#/# +
and their sycamore trees with frost.

48 He also gave up their livestock to the hail [.linebr]#/# +
and their flocks to hot thunderbolts.

49 He cast upon them the fierceness of his anger, [.linebr]#/# +
wrath, indignation, and trouble, [.linebr]#/# +
by sending evil angels among them.

50 He made a way to his anger. [.linebr]#/# +
He did not spare their soul from death, [.linebr]#/# +
but gave their life over to the pestilence,

51 And smote all the first-born in Egypt, [.linebr]#/# +
the chief of their strength in the tabernacles of Ham,

52 But made his own people to go forth like sheep [.linebr]#/# +
and guided them in the wilderness like a flock.

53 And he led them on safely so that they did not fear. [.linebr]#/# +
But the sea overwhelmed their enemies.

54 And he brought them to the border of his sanctuary, [.linebr]#/# +
even to this mountain, which his right hand had purchased.

55 He also cast out the heathen before them. [.linebr]#/# +
He divided them an inheritance by line [.linebr]#/# +
and made the tribes of Israel to dwell in their tents.

56 Yet they tested and provoked the most high God [.linebr]#/# +
and did not keep his testimonies,

57 But turned back and dealt unfaithfully like their fathers. [.linebr]#/# +
They were turned aside like a deceitful bow.

58 For they provoked him to anger with their high places [.linebr]#/# +
and moved him to jealousy with their engraved images.

59 When God heard this, he was angry [.linebr]#/# +
and greatly abhorred Israel,

60 So that he forsook the tabernacle of Shiloh, [.linebr]#/# +
the tent which he placed among men,

61 And delivered his strength into captivity [.linebr]#/# +
and his glory into the enemy's hand.

62 He also gave over his people to the sword [.linebr]#/# +
and was angry with his inheritance.

63 The fire consumed their young men, [.linebr]#/# +
and their young women were not given to marriage.

64 Their priests fell by the sword, [.linebr]#/# +
and their widows made no lamentation.

65 Then the Lord awoke like someone out of sleep [.linebr]#/# +
and like a mighty man who shouts by reason of wine.

66 And he smote his enemies backward. [.linebr]#/# +
He put them to a perpetual reproach.

67 Moreover, he refused the tabernacle of Joseph [.linebr]#/# +
and did not choose the tribe of Ephraim,

68 But chose the tribe of Judah, [.linebr]#/# +
the mount Zion which he loved.

69 And he built his sanctuary like high palaces, [.linebr]#/# +
like the earth which he has established forever.

70 He also chose David his servant [.linebr]#/# +
and took him from the sheep-folds.

71 From following the ewes great with young he brought him [.linebr]#/# +
to feed Jacob his people and Israel his inheritance.

72 Thus he fed them according to the integrity of his heart [.linebr]#/# +
and guided them by the skillfulness of his hands.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.2]*: Quoted in xref:#mth013-035[Matthew 13:35]. *[v.24]*: Quoted in xref:#jhn006-031[John 6:31].

[#psa079%breakable]
=== Psalm 79

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist bemoans the desolation of Jerusalem, 1-7. He prays for deliverance, 8-12; and promises thankfulness, 13._

1 [_A Psalm of Asaph._]

O God, the heathen have come into your inheritance. [.linebr]#/# +
They have defiled your holy temple. [.linebr]#/# +
They have laid Jerusalem on heaps.

2 They have given the dead bodies of your servants [.linebr]#/# +
to be food for the birds of the heaven, [.linebr]#/# +
the flesh of your saints to the beasts of the earth.

3 They have shed their blood like water around Jerusalem, [.linebr]#/# +
and there was no one to bury them.

4 We have become a reproach to our neighbors, [.linebr]#/# +
a scorn and derision to those who are around us.

5 How long, LORD? Will you be angry forever? [.linebr]#/# +
Shall your jealousy burn like fire?

6 Pour out your wrath upon the heathen [.linebr]#/# +
who have not known you [.linebr]#/# +
and upon the kingdoms [.linebr]#/# +
that have not called upon your name.

7 For they have devoured Jacob [.linebr]#/# +
and laid waste his dwelling-place.

8 O do not hold former iniquities against us. [.linebr]#/# +
Let your tender mercies speedily meet us, [.linebr]#/# +
for we are brought very low.

9 Help us, O God of our salvation, [.linebr]#/# +
for the glory of your name, [.linebr]#/# +
and deliver us and purge away our sins [.linebr]#/# +
for your name's sake.

10 Why should the heathen say, "Where is their God?" [.linebr]#/# +
Let him be known among the heathen in our sight [.linebr]#/# +
by avenging the blood of your servants which is shed.

11 Let the sighing of the prisoner come before you. [.linebr]#/# +
According to the greatness of your power [.linebr]#/# +
preserve those who are appointed to die.

12 And render to our neighbors seven-fold into their bosom [.linebr]#/# +
their reproach with which they have reproached you, O Lord.

13 So we your people and sheep of your pasture [.linebr]#/# +
will give you thanks forever. [.linebr]#/# +
We will show forth your praise to all generations.

[#psa080%breakable]
=== Psalm 80

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist in his prayer bemoans the miseries of the church, 1-7. God's former favors are turned into judgments, 8-13. He prays for deliverance, 14-19._

1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Shoshannim Eduth. A Psalm of Asaph._]

Give ear, O Shepherd of Israel, [.linebr]#/# +
you who lead Joseph like a flock. [.linebr]#/# +
You who dwell between the cherubim, shine forth.

2 Before Ephraim and Benjamin and Manasseh, [.linebr]#/# +
stir up your strength [.linebr]#/# +
and come and save us.

3 Turn us back, O God, [.linebr]#/# +
and cause your face to shine, and we shall be saved.

4 O LORD God of hosts, [.linebr]#/# +
how long will you be angry against the prayer of your people?

5 You feed them with the bread of tears [.linebr]#/# +
and give them tears to drink in great measure.

6 You make us a strife to our neighbors, [.linebr]#/# +
and our enemies laugh among themselves.

7 Turn us back, O God of hosts, [.linebr]#/# +
and cause your face to shine, and we shall be saved.

8 You have brought a vine out of Egypt. [.linebr]#/# +
You have cast out the heathen and planted it.

9 You cleared a place before it, [.linebr]#/# +
and it took deep root and filled the land.

10 The hills were covered with its shade, [.linebr]#/# +
and its boughs were like the beautiful cedars.

11 She sent out her boughs to the sea [.linebr]#/# +
and her branches to the river.

12 Why have you then broken down her hedges [.linebr]#/# +
so that all those who pass by the way pluck her?

13 The boar from the forest wastes it, [.linebr]#/# +
and the wild beast of the field devours it.

14 Return, we implore you, O God of hosts. [.linebr]#/# +
Look down from heaven and behold. Visit this vine,

15 The vineyard which your right hand planted, [.linebr]#/# +
the branch that you made strong for yourself.

16 It is burnt with fire. It is cut down. [.linebr]#/# +
They perish at the rebuke of your countenance.

17 Let your hand be upon the man of your right hand, [.linebr]#/# +
upon the son of man whom you made strong for yourself.

18 Then we will not go back from you. [.linebr]#/# +
Revive us, and we will call upon your name.

19 Turn us back, O LORD God of hosts, [.linebr]#/# +
cause your face to shine, and we shall be saved.

[#psa081%breakable]
=== Psalm 81

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to a solemn praising of God, 1-3. God challenges that duty by reason of his benefits, 4-7. God, exhorting to obedience, admonishes them for their disobedience, which proves their own hurt, 8-16._

1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Gittith. A Psalm of Asaph._]

Sing aloud to God our strength. [.linebr]#/# +
Make a joyful noise to the God of Jacob.

2 Take a psalm and bring here the tambourine, [.linebr]#/# +
the pleasant harp with the psaltery.

3 Blow the trumpet at the new moon, [.linebr]#/# +
and at the full moon on our solemn feast day.

4 For this was a statute for Israel [.linebr]#/# +
and a law of the God of Jacob.

5 He ordained this in Joseph for a testimony [.linebr]#/# +
when he went out through the land of Egypt. [.linebr]#/# +
I heard a language that I did not understand:

6 "I removed his shoulder from the burden. [.linebr]#/# +
His hands were delivered from the pots.

7 You called in trouble, and I delivered you. [.linebr]#/# +
I answered you in the secret place of thunder. [.linebr]#/# +
I proved you at the waters of Meribah." [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

8 "Hear, O my people, and I will testify to you, [.linebr]#/# +
O Israel, if you would listen to me.

9 There shall no strange god be in you, [.linebr]#/# +
neither shall you worship any strange god.

10 I am the LORD your God [.linebr]#/# +
who brought you out of the land of Egypt. [.linebr]#/# +
Open your mouth wide, and I will fill it.

11 But my people would not listen to my voice, [.linebr]#/# +
and Israel would not obey me.

12 So I gave them up to the lust of their hearts, [.linebr]#/# +
and they walked in their own counsels.

13 O that my people had listened to me [.linebr]#/# +
and Israel had walked in my ways!

14 I would soon subdue their enemies [.linebr]#/# +
and turn my hand against their adversaries.

15 The haters of the LORD should have submitted themselves to him, [.linebr]#/# +
and their time should have endured forever.

16 He would have fed them also with the finest of the wheat. [.linebr]#/# +
And with honey out of the rock I would satisfy you."

[#psa082%breakable]
=== Psalm 82

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist, having exhorted the judges, 1-4, and reproved their negligence, 5-7, prays God to judge, 8._

1 [_A Psalm of Asaph._]

God stands in the congregation of the mighty. [.linebr]#/# +
He judges among the gods.

2 "How long will you judge unjustly [.linebr]#/# +
and accept the persons of the wicked?" [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

3 "Defend the poor and fatherless. [.linebr]#/# +
Do justice to the afflicted and needy.

4 Deliver the poor and needy. [.linebr]#/# +
Deliver them from the hand of the wicked.

5 They do not know, neither will they understand. [.linebr]#/# +
They walk on in darkness. [.linebr]#/# +
All the foundations of the earth are out of course.

[[psa082-006]]6 I have said, 'You are gods, [.linebr]#/# +
and all of you are children of the Most High.

7 But you shall die like men [.linebr]#/# +
and fall like one of the princes.'"

8 Arise, O God, judge the earth, [.linebr]#/# +
for you will inherit all nations.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.6]*: Quoted in xref:#jhn010-034[John 10:34].

[#psa083%breakable]
=== Psalm 83

[.outline.text-center]
_A call to God for help because of the enemies' conspiracies, 1-8. A prayer against those who oppress the Church, 9-18._

1 [_A Song or Psalm of Asaph._]

Do not keep silent, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not hold your peace and do not be still, O God.

2 For behold, your enemies make a tumult, [.linebr]#/# +
and those who hate you have lifted up the head.

3 They have taken crafty counsel against your people [.linebr]#/# +
and consulted against your hidden ones.

4 They have said, "Come, and let us cut them off from being a nation [.linebr]#/# +
so that the name of Israel may no longer be in remembrance."

5 For they have consulted together with one consent. [.linebr]#/# +
They are confederated against you:

6 The tabernacles of Edom and the Ishmaelites, [.linebr]#/# +
of Moab and the Hagarenes,

7 Gebal, Ammon, and Amalek, [.linebr]#/# +
the Philistines with the inhabitants of Tyre.

8 Assur is also joined with them. [.linebr]#/# +
They have helped the children of Lot. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

9 Do to them as to the Midianites, [.linebr]#/# +
as to Sisera and to Jabin at the brook of Kison,

10 Who perished at En-dor. [.linebr]#/# +
They became like dung for the earth.

11 Make their nobles like Oreb and like Zeeb, [.linebr]#/# +
even all their princes like Zebah and like Zalmunna,

12 Who said, "Let us take for ourselves [.linebr]#/# +
the houses of God in possession."

13 O my God, make them like a wheel, [.linebr]#/# +
like the stubble before the wind.

14 As the fire burns a forest [.linebr]#/# +
and as the flame sets the mountains on fire,

15 So persecute them with your tempest [.linebr]#/# +
and make them afraid with your storm.

16 Fill their faces with shame [.linebr]#/# +
so that they may seek your name, O LORD.

17 Let them be confounded and troubled forever. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them even be put to shame and perish,

18 So that men may know that you, whose name alone is YAHWEH, [.linebr]#/# +
are the most high over all the earth.

[#psa084%breakable]
=== Psalm 84

[.outline.text-center]
_The prophet, longing for the fellowship of the sanctuary, 1-3, shows how blessed those are who dwell therein, 4-7. He prays to be restored to it, 8-12._

1 [_To the Chief Musician upon Gittith. A Psalm for the Sons of Korah._]

How amiable your tabernacles are, [.linebr]#/# +
O LORD of hosts!

2 My soul longs and even faints for the courts of the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
My heart and my flesh cry out for the living God.

3 Even the sparrow has found a house, [.linebr]#/# +
and the swallow a nest for herself, [.linebr]#/# +
where she may lay her young [.linebr]#/# +
near your altars, O LORD of hosts, [.linebr]#/# +
my King and my God.

4 Blessed are those who dwell in your house. [.linebr]#/# +
They are always praising you. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

5 Blessed is the man whose strength is in you, [.linebr]#/# +
in whose heart are the ways of them.

6 Passing through the valley of Baca they make it a well. [.linebr]#/# +
The rain also fills the pools.

7 They go from strength to strength. [.linebr]#/# +
Every one of them in Zion appears before God.

8 O LORD God of hosts, hear my prayer. [.linebr]#/# +
Give ear, O God of Jacob. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

9 Behold, O God our shield, [.linebr]#/# +
and look upon the face of your anointed.

10 For a day in your courts is better than a thousand [elsewhere]. [.linebr]#/# +
I would rather be a door-keeper in the house of my God [.linebr]#/# +
than dwell in the tents of wickedness.

11 For the LORD God is a sun and shield. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD will give grace and glory. [.linebr]#/# +
No good will he withhold from those who walk uprightly.

12 O LORD of hosts, [.linebr]#/# +
blessed is the man who trusts in you.

[#psa085%breakable]
=== Psalm 85

[.outline.text-center]
_The Psalmist, out of the experience of former mercies, prays for the continuance thereof, 1-7. He promises to wait thereon, out of confidence of God's goodness, 8-13._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm for the Sons of Korah._]

LORD, you have been favorable to your land. [.linebr]#/# +
You have brought back the captivity of Jacob.

2 You have forgiven the iniquity of your people. [.linebr]#/# +
You have covered all their sin. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

3 You have taken away all your wrath. [.linebr]#/# +
You have turned yourself from the fierceness of your anger.

4 Turn us, O God of our salvation, [.linebr]#/# +
and cause your anger toward us to cease.

5 Will you be angry with us forever? [.linebr]#/# +
Will you draw out your anger to all generations?

6 Will you not revive us again [.linebr]#/# +
so that your people may rejoice in you?

7 Show us your mercy, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and grant us your salvation.

8 I will hear what God, Yahweh, will speak, [.linebr]#/# +
for he will speak peace to his people and to his saints. [.linebr]#/# +
But do not let them turn back to folly.

9 Surely his salvation is near those who fear him [.linebr]#/# +
so that glory may dwell in our land.

10 Mercy and truth are met together. [.linebr]#/# +
Righteousness and peace have kissed each other.

11 Truth shall spring out of the earth, [.linebr]#/# +
and righteousness shall look down from heaven.

12 Indeed, the LORD will give that which is good, [.linebr]#/# +
and our land shall yield her increase.

13 Righteousness shall go before him [.linebr]#/# +
and set us in the way of his steps.

[#psa086%breakable]
=== Psalm 86

[.outline.text-center]
_David strengthens his prayer by the consciousness of his religion, 1-4; by the goodness and power of God 5-10. He desires the continuance of former grace, 11-13. After describing his enemies and appealing to God, he craves some token of God's goodness, 14-17._

1 [_A Prayer of David._]

Bow down your ear, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Hear me, for I am poor and needy.

2 Preserve my soul, for I am holy. [.linebr]#/# +
O you, my God, save your servant who trusts in you.

3 Be merciful to me, O Lord, [.linebr]#/# +
for I cry to you daily.

4 Bring joy to the soul of your servant, [.linebr]#/# +
for to you, O Lord, I lift up my soul.

5 For you, Lord, are good and ready to forgive [.linebr]#/# +
and abundant in mercy to all those who call upon you.

6 Give ear, O LORD, to my prayer [.linebr]#/# +
and attend to the voice of my supplications.

7 In the day of my trouble I will call upon you, [.linebr]#/# +
for you will answer me.

8 Among the gods there is no one like you, O Lord, [.linebr]#/# +
neither are there any works like your works.

[[psa086-009]]9 All nations whom you have made [.linebr]#/# +
shall come and worship before you, [.linebr]#/# +
O Lord, and shall glorify your name.

10 For you are great and do wondrous things. [.linebr]#/# +
You are God alone.

11 Teach me your way, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
I will walk in your truth. [.linebr]#/# +
Unite my heart to fear your name.

12 I will praise you, O Lord my God, with all my heart [.linebr]#/# +
and I will glorify your name forevermore.

13 For your mercy is great toward me, [.linebr]#/# +
and you have delivered my soul from the lowest hell.

14 O God, the proud have risen against me, [.linebr]#/# +
and the assemblies of violent men have sought after my soul. [.linebr]#/# +
They have not set you before them.

15 But you, O Lord, are a God full of compassion and gracious. [.linebr]#/# +
You are patient and abundant in mercy and truth.

16 O turn to me and have mercy upon me. [.linebr]#/# +
Give your strength to your servant [.linebr]#/# +
and save the son of your woman-servant.

17 Show me a token for good [.linebr]#/# +
so that those who hate me may see it and be ashamed, [.linebr]#/# +
because you, LORD, have helped me and comforted me.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.9]*: Quoted in xref:#rev015-004[Revelation 15:4].

[#psa087%breakable]
=== Psalm 87

[.outline.text-center]
_The nature and glory of the church, 1-3. The increase, honor, and comfort of the members thereof, 4-7._

1 [_A Psalm or Song for the Sons of Korah._]

His foundation is in the holy mountains.

2 The LORD loves the gates of Zion [.linebr]#/# +
more than all the dwellings of Jacob.

3 Glorious things are spoken of you, [.linebr]#/# +
O city of God. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

4 "I will make mention of Rahab and Babylon [.linebr]#/# +
to those who know me. [.linebr]#/# +
Behold, Philistia, Tyre, and also Cush: [.linebr]#/# +
'This one was born there.'"

5 And of Zion it shall be said, [.linebr]#/# +
"This and that man was born in her. [.linebr]#/# +
And the Highest himself shall establish her."

6 The LORD shall reckon when he registers the people: [.linebr]#/# +
"This man was born there." [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

7 The singers as well as the players on instruments shall be there. [.linebr]#/# +
All my springs are in you.

[#psa088%breakable]
=== Psalm 88

[.outline.text-center]
_A prayer containing a grievous complaint, 1-18._

1 [_A Song or Psalm for the Sons of Korah, to the Chief Musician upon Mahalath Leannoth. Maschil of Heman the Ezrahite._]

O LORD God of my salvation, [.linebr]#/# +
I have cried day and night before you.

2 Let my prayer come before you. [.linebr]#/# +
Incline your ear to my cry,

3 For my soul is full of troubles, [.linebr]#/# +
and my life draws near to the grave.

4 I am counted with those who go down into the pit. [.linebr]#/# +
I am like a man who has no strength,

5 Free among the dead, [.linebr]#/# +
like the slain who lie in the grave, [.linebr]#/# +
whom you no longer remember, [.linebr]#/# +
and they are cut off from your hand.

6 You have laid me in the lowest pit, [.linebr]#/# +
in darkness, in the deeps.

7 Your wrath lies hard upon me, [.linebr]#/# +
and you have afflicted me with all your waves. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

8 You have put away my acquaintances far from me. [.linebr]#/# +
You have made me an abomination to them. [.linebr]#/# +
I am shut up and I cannot come forth.

9 My eye mourns by reason of affliction. [.linebr]#/# +
LORD, I have called daily upon you. [.linebr]#/# +
I have stretched out my hands to you.

10 Will you show wonders to the dead? [.linebr]#/# +
Shall the dead arise and praise you? [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

11 Shall your loving-kindness be declared in the grave, [.linebr]#/# +
or your faithfulness in destruction?

12 Shall your wonders be known in the dark [.linebr]#/# +
and your righteousness in the land of forgetfulness?

13 But to you I have cried, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and in the morning my prayer shall come before you.

14 LORD, why do you cast off my soul? [.linebr]#/# +
Why do you hide your face from me?

15 I am afflicted and ready to die from my youth. [.linebr]#/# +
While I suffer your terrors I am distracted.

16 Your fierce wrath goes over me. [.linebr]#/# +
Your terrors have cut me off.

17 They came around me daily like water. [.linebr]#/# +
They encompassed me together.

18 You have put loved one and friend far from me [.linebr]#/# +
and my acquaintances into darkness.

[#psa089%breakable]
=== Psalm 89

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist praises God for his covenant, 1-4; for his wonderful power, 5-14; for the care of his church, 15-18; for his favor to the kingdom of David, 19-37. Then bemoaning contrary events, 38-45, he expostulates, prays, and blesses God, 46-52._

1 [_Maschil of Ethan the Ezrahite._]

I will sing of the mercies of the LORD forever. [.linebr]#/# +
With my mouth I will make your faithfulness known to all generations.

2 For I have said, "Mercy shall be built up forever. [.linebr]#/# +
You will establish your faithfulness in the very heavens."

3 "I have made a covenant with my chosen. [.linebr]#/# +
I have sworn to David my servant,

4 'I will establish your offspring forever [.linebr]#/# +
and build up your throne to all generations.'" [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

5 And the heavens shall praise your wonders, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and also your faithfulness in the congregation of the saints.

6 For who in the heaven can be compared to the LORD? [.linebr]#/# +
Who among the sons of the mighty can be compared to the LORD?

7 God is greatly to be feared in the assembly of the saints [.linebr]#/# +
and to be had in reverence by all those who are around him.

8 O LORD God of hosts, [.linebr]#/# +
who is mighty like you, O Yah? [.linebr]#/# +
And your faithfulness is around you.

9 You rule the raging of the sea. [.linebr]#/# +
When its waves arise, you still them.

10 You have broken Rahab in pieces like one who is slain. [.linebr]#/# +
You have scattered your enemies with your strong arm.

11 The heavens are yours, the earth also is yours. [.linebr]#/# +
As for the world and its fullness, you have founded them.

12 The north and the south, you have created them. [.linebr]#/# +
Tabor and Hermon shall rejoice in your name.

13 You have a mighty arm. [.linebr]#/# +
Your hand is strong and your right hand is high.

14 Justice and judgment are the habitation of your throne. [.linebr]#/# +
Mercy and truth shall go before your face.

15 Blessed are the people who know the joyful sound. [.linebr]#/# +
They shall walk, O LORD, in the light of your countenance.

16 In your name they shall rejoice all the day, [.linebr]#/# +
and in your righteousness they shall be exalted.

17 For you are the glory of their strength, [.linebr]#/# +
and in your favor our horn shall be exalted.

18 For the LORD is our defense, [.linebr]#/# +
and the Holy One of Israel is our king.

19 Then you spoke in a vision to your holy one [.linebr]#/# +
and said, "I have laid help upon one who is mighty. [.linebr]#/# +
I have exalted one chosen out of the people.

[[psa089-020]]20 I have found David my servant. [.linebr]#/# +
With my holy oil I have anointed him.

21 With him my hand shall be established. [.linebr]#/# +
My arm shall also strengthen him.

22 The enemy shall not exact upon him, [.linebr]#/# +
nor the son of wickedness afflict him.

23 And I will beat down his foes before his face [.linebr]#/# +
and afflict those who hate him.

24 But my faithfulness and my mercy shall be with him, [.linebr]#/# +
and in my name his horn shall be exalted.

25 I will set his hand on the sea [.linebr]#/# +
and his right hand on the rivers.

26 He shall cry to me, 'You are my father, [.linebr]#/# +
my God, and the rock of my salvation.'

27 Also I will make him my first-born, [.linebr]#/# +
higher than the kings of the earth.

28 I will keep my mercy for him forevermore, [.linebr]#/# +
and my covenant shall stand firmly with him.

29 I will also make his offspring to endure forever, [.linebr]#/# +
and his throne as the days of heaven.

30 If his children forsake my law [.linebr]#/# +
and do not walk in my judgments,

31 If they break my statutes [.linebr]#/# +
and do not keep my commandments,

32 Then I will visit their transgression with the rod [.linebr]#/# +
and their iniquity with stripes.

33 Nevertheless, I will not utterly take my loving-kindness from him, [.linebr]#/# +
nor allow my faithfulness to fail.

34 I will not break my covenant, [.linebr]#/# +
nor alter the thing that has gone out of my lips.

35 Once I have sworn by my holiness, [.linebr]#/# +
I will not lie to David.

36 His offspring shall endure forever, [.linebr]#/# +
and his throne as the sun before me.

37 It shall be established forever like the moon, [.linebr]#/# +
like the faithful witness in the sky." [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

38 But you have cast off and abhorred, [.linebr]#/# +
you have been angry with your anointed.

39 You have made the covenant of your servant void. [.linebr]#/# +
You have profaned his crown by casting it to the ground.

40 You have broken all his hedges down. [.linebr]#/# +
You have brought his strongholds to ruin.

41 All who pass by the way plunder him. [.linebr]#/# +
He is a reproach to his neighbors.

42 You have set up the right hand of his adversaries. [.linebr]#/# +
You have made all his enemies to rejoice.

43 You have also turned the edge of his sword [.linebr]#/# +
and have not made him to stand in the battle.

44 You have made his glory to cease [.linebr]#/# +
and cast his throne down to the ground.

45 The days of his youth you have shortened. [.linebr]#/# +
You have covered him with shame. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

46 How long, LORD, will you hide yourself? [.linebr]#/# +
Forever? Shall your wrath burn like fire?

47 Remember how short my time is. [.linebr]#/# +
Why have you made all men in vain?

48 What man is he who lives and shall not see death? [.linebr]#/# +
Shall he deliver his soul from the hand of the grave? [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

49 Lord, where are your former loving-kindnesses [.linebr]#/# +
which you swore to David in your truth?

50 Remember, Lord, the reproach of your servants, [.linebr]#/# +
how I bear in my bosom the reproach of all the mighty people,

51 With which your enemies have reproached, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
with which they have reproached the footsteps of your anointed.

52 Blessed be the LORD forevermore. [.linebr]#/# +
Amen and amen.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.20]*: Quoted in xref:#act013-022[Acts 13:22].

[#psalms-book-4%breakable]
=== BOOK IV

[#psa090%breakable]
=== Psalm 90

[.outline.text-center]
_Moses sets forth God's providence, 1, 2. The frailty of the state of man, 3-9, and brevity of life, 10, 11. He prays for the knowledge and sensible experience of God's good providence, 12-17._

1 [_A Prayer of Moses the Man of God._]

Lord, you have been our dwelling-place [.linebr]#/# +
in all generations.

2 Before the mountains were brought forth, [.linebr]#/# +
or before you had formed the earth and the world, [.linebr]#/# +
even from everlasting to everlasting, you are God.

3 You turn man to destruction [.linebr]#/# +
and say, "Return, you children of men."

4 For a thousand years in your sight [.linebr]#/# +
are like yesterday when it is past [.linebr]#/# +
and like a watch in the night.

5 You carry them away as with a flood. They are like a dream. [.linebr]#/# +
In the morning they are like grass which grows.

6 In the morning it flourishes and grows. [.linebr]#/# +
In the evening it is cut down and withers.

7 For we are consumed by your anger, [.linebr]#/# +
and by your wrath we are troubled.

8 You have set our iniquities before you, [.linebr]#/# +
our secret sins in the light of your countenance.

9 For all our days are passed away in your wrath. [.linebr]#/# +
We spend our years as a tale that is told.

10 The days of our years are seventy years. [.linebr]#/# +
And if by reason of strength they are eighty years, [.linebr]#/# +
yet their strength is labor and sorrow, [.linebr]#/# +
for it is soon cut off, and we fly away.

11 Who knows the power of your anger? [.linebr]#/# +
Even according to your fear, so is your wrath.

12 So teach us to number our days [.linebr]#/# +
so that we may apply our hearts to wisdom.

13 Return, O LORD, how long? [.linebr]#/# +
And repent concerning your servants.

14 O satisfy us early with your mercy [.linebr]#/# +
so that we may rejoice and be glad all our days.

15 Make us glad according to the days in which you have afflicted us [.linebr]#/# +
and the years in which we have seen evil.

16 Let your work appear to your servants [.linebr]#/# +
and your glory to their children.

17 And let the beauty of the LORD our God be upon us. [.linebr]#/# +
And establish the work of our hands upon us. [.linebr]#/# +
Yes, the work of our hands, establish it.

[#psa091%breakable]
=== Psalm 91

[.outline.text-center]
_The state of the godly, 1, 2. Their safety, 3-8. Their habitation, 9, 10. Their servants, 11-13. Their friend; with the effects of them all, 14-16._

1 He who dwells in the secret place of the Most High [.linebr]#/# +
shall abide under the shadow of the Almighty.

2 I will say of the LORD, "He is my refuge and my fortress, [.linebr]#/# +
my God in whom I trust."

3 Surely he shall deliver you from the snare of the fowler [.linebr]#/# +
and from the noisome pestilence.

4 He shall cover you with his feathers, [.linebr]#/# +
and under his wings you shall trust. [.linebr]#/# +
His truth shall be your shield and buckler.

5 You shall not be afraid of the terror by night, [.linebr]#/# +
nor of the arrow that flies by day,

6 Nor of the pestilence that walks in darkness, [.linebr]#/# +
nor of the destruction that wastes at noon-day.

7 A thousand shall fall at your side, [.linebr]#/# +
and ten thousand at your right hand, [.linebr]#/# +
but it shall not come near you.

8 Only with your eyes you shall behold [.linebr]#/# +
and see the reward of the wicked.

9 For you, LORD, are my refuge! [.linebr]#/# +
You have made the Most High your habitation.

10 There shall no evil befall you, [.linebr]#/# +
neither shall any plague come near your dwelling.

[[psa091-011]]11 For he shall give his angels charge over you [.linebr]#/# +
to keep you in all your ways.

[[psa091-012]]12 They shall bear you up in their hands, [.linebr]#/# +
lest you dash your foot against a stone.

13 You shall tread upon the lion and the adder. [.linebr]#/# +
The young lion and the serpent you shall trample under feet.

14 "Because he has set his love upon me, therefore I will deliver him. [.linebr]#/# +
I will set him on high because he has known my name.

15 He shall call upon me, and I will answer him. [.linebr]#/# +
I will be with him in trouble. [.linebr]#/# +
I will deliver him and honor him.

16 With long life I will satisfy him [.linebr]#/# +
and show him my salvation."

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.11]*: Quoted in xref:#mth004-006[Matthew 4:6]; xref:#luk004-010[Luke 4:10]. *[v.12]*: Quoted in xref:#mth004-006[Matthew 4:6]; xref:#luk004-011[Luke 4:11].

[#psa092%breakable]
=== Psalm 92

[.outline.text-center]
_The prophet exhorts to praise God, 1-3, for his great works, 4, 5; for his judgments on the wicked, 6-9; and for his goodness to the godly, 10-15._

1 [_A Psalm or Song for the Sabbath Day._]

It is a good thing to give thanks to the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
and to sing praises to your name, O Most High,

2 To show forth your loving-kindness in the morning [.linebr]#/# +
and your faithfulness every night,

3 Upon an instrument of ten strings and upon the psaltery, [.linebr]#/# +
upon the harp with a solemn sound.

4 For you, LORD, have made me glad through your work. [.linebr]#/# +
I will triumph in the works of your hands.

5 O LORD, how great your works are! [.linebr]#/# +
And your thoughts are very deep.

6 A brutish man does not know, [.linebr]#/# +
neither does a fool understand this.

7 When the wicked spring like the grass [.linebr]#/# +
and when all the workers of iniquity flourish, [.linebr]#/# +
it is that they shall be destroyed forever.

8 But you, LORD, are most high forevermore.

9 For behold, your enemies, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
for behold, your enemies shall perish. [.linebr]#/# +
All the workers of iniquity shall be scattered.

10 But you shall exalt my horn like the horn of a wild ox. [.linebr]#/# +
I shall be anointed with fresh oil.

11 My eye has also seen my enemies, [.linebr]#/# +
and my ears shall hear the wicked [.linebr]#/# +
who rise up against me.

12 The righteous shall flourish like the palm-tree. [.linebr]#/# +
He shall grow like a cedar in Lebanon.

13 Those who are planted in the house of the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
shall flourish in the courts of our God.

14 They shall still bring forth fruit in old age. [.linebr]#/# +
They shall be fat and flourishing,

15 To show that the LORD is upright. [.linebr]#/# +
He is my rock, and there is no unrighteousness in him.

[#psa093%breakable]
=== Psalm 93

[.outline.text-center]
_The majesty, stability, power, and holiness of Christ's kingdom, 1-5._

1 The LORD reigns. [.linebr]#/# +
He is clothed with majesty. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD is clothed with strength, [.linebr]#/# +
with which he has girded himself. [.linebr]#/# +
The world is also established so that it cannot be moved.

2 Your throne is established of old. [.linebr]#/# +
You are from everlasting.

3 The floods have lifted up, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
the floods have lifted up their voice. [.linebr]#/# +
The floods lift their waves.

4 The LORD on high is mightier [.linebr]#/# +
than the noise of many waters, [.linebr]#/# +
even mightier than the mighty waves of the sea.

5 Your testimonies are very sure. [.linebr]#/# +
Holiness is suitable for your house, O LORD, forever.

[#psa094%breakable]
=== Psalm 94

[.outline.text-center]
_The prophet, calling for justice, bemoans tyranny and impiety, 1-7. He teaches God's providence, 8-11. He shows the blessedness of affliction, 12-15. God is the defender of the afflicted, 16-23._

1 O LORD God, to whom vengeance belongs, [.linebr]#/# +
O God, to whom vengeance belongs, show yourself.

2 Lift up yourself, judge of the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
Render a reward to the proud.

3 LORD, how long shall the wicked, [.linebr]#/# +
how long shall the wicked triumph?

4 How long shall they utter and speak hard things, [.linebr]#/# +
and all the workers of iniquity boast themselves?

5 They break your people in pieces, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and afflict your heritage.

6 They slay the widow and the stranger [.linebr]#/# +
and murder the fatherless.

7 Yet they say, "The LORD will not see, [.linebr]#/# +
neither will the God of Jacob regard it."

8 Understand, you brutish among the people. [.linebr]#/# +
And you fools, when will you be wise?

9 He who planted the ear, shall he not hear? [.linebr]#/# +
He who formed the eye, shall he not see?

10 He who chastises the heathen, shall he not correct? [.linebr]#/# +
He who teaches man knowledge, shall he not know?

[[psa094-011]]11 The LORD knows the thoughts of man, [.linebr]#/# +
that they are vanity.

12 Blessed is the man whom you chasten, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and teach him out of your law,

13 So that you may give him rest from the days of adversity [.linebr]#/# +
until the pit is dug for the wicked.

[[psa094-014]]14 For the LORD will not cast off his people, [.linebr]#/# +
neither will he forsake his inheritance.

15 But judgment shall return to righteousness, [.linebr]#/# +
and all the upright in heart shall follow it.

16 Who will rise up for me against the evil-doers? [.linebr]#/# +
Or who will stand up for me against the workers of iniquity?

17 Unless the LORD had been my help, [.linebr]#/# +
my soul would have almost dwelt in silence.

18 When I said, "My foot slips," [.linebr]#/# +
your mercy, O LORD, held me up.

19 In the multitude of my thoughts within me, [.linebr]#/# +
your comforts delight my soul.

20 Shall the throne of iniquity have fellowship with you, [.linebr]#/# +
which frames mischief by a law?

21 They assemble themselves against the soul of the righteous [.linebr]#/# +
and condemn the innocent blood.

22 But the LORD is my defense, [.linebr]#/# +
and my God is the rock of my refuge.

23 And he will bring upon them their own iniquity [.linebr]#/# +
and will cut them off in their own wickedness. [.linebr]#/# +
Indeed, the LORD our God will cut them off.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.11]*: Quoted in xref:#fco003-020[1st Corinthians 3:20]. *[v.14]*: Quoted in xref:#rom011-002[Romans 11:2].

[#psa095%breakable]
=== Psalm 95

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to praise God, 1, 2, for his greatness, 3-5; and for his goodness, 6, 7; and not to test him, 8-11._

1 O come, let us sing to the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Let us make a joyful noise to the rock of our salvation.

2 Let us come before his presence with thanksgiving [.linebr]#/# +
and make a joyful noise to him with psalms.

3 For the LORD is a great God [.linebr]#/# +
and a great King above all gods.

4 In his hand are the deep places of the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
The strength of the hills is his also.

5 The sea is his, and he made it. [.linebr]#/# +
And his hands formed the dry land.

6 O come, let us worship and bow down. [.linebr]#/# +
Let us kneel before the LORD our maker.

[[psa095-007]]7 For he is our God, [.linebr]#/# +
and we are the people of his pasture [.linebr]#/# +
and the sheep of his hand. [.linebr]#/# +
Today, if you will hear his voice,

[[psa095-008]]8 Do not harden your heart, as at Meribah, [.linebr]#/# +
and as in the day of Massah in the wilderness,

[[psa095-009]]9 When your fathers tested me, [.linebr]#/# +
proved me, and saw my work.

[[psa095-010]]10 Forty long years I was grieved with this generation, [.linebr]#/# +
and said, "It is a people who err in their heart, [.linebr]#/# +
and they have not known my ways,"

[[psa095-011]]11 To whom I swore in my wrath, [.linebr]#/# +
"They shall not enter into my rest."

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.7]*: Quoted in xref:#heb003-007[Hebrews 3:7], xref:#heb003-015[3:15], xref:#heb004-007[4:7]. *[v.8]*: Quoted in xref:#heb003-008[Hebrews 3:8], xref:#heb003-015[3:15], xref:#heb004-007[4:7]. *[v.9]*: Quoted in xref:#heb003-009[Hebrews 3:9]. *[v.10]*: Quoted in xref:#heb003-010[Hebrews 3:10]. *[v.11]*: Quoted in xref:#heb003-011[Hebrews 3:11], xref:#heb004-003[4:3], xref:#heb004-005[4:5].

[#psa096%breakable]
=== Psalm 96

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to praise God, 1-3, for his greatness, 4-7; for his kingdom, 8-10; for his general judgment, 11-13._

1 O sing to the LORD a new song. [.linebr]#/# +
Sing to the LORD, all the earth.

2 Sing to the LORD. Bless his name. [.linebr]#/# +
Show forth his salvation from day to day.

3 Declare his glory among the heathen, [.linebr]#/# +
his wonders among all people.

4 For the LORD is great and greatly to be praised. [.linebr]#/# +
He is to be feared above all gods.

5 For all the gods of the nations are idols, [.linebr]#/# +
but the LORD made the heavens.

6 Honor and majesty are before him. [.linebr]#/# +
Strength and beauty are in his sanctuary.

7 Give to the LORD, O kindreds of the people, [.linebr]#/# +
give to the LORD glory and strength.

8 Give to the LORD the glory due to his name. [.linebr]#/# +
Bring an offering and come into his courts.

9 O worship the LORD in the beauty of holiness. [.linebr]#/# +
Fear before him, all the earth.

10 Say among the heathen that the LORD reigns. [.linebr]#/# +
The world shall also be established so that it shall not be moved. [.linebr]#/# +
He will judge the people righteously.

11 Let the heavens rejoice, and let the earth be glad. [.linebr]#/# +
Let the sea roar, and its fullness.

12 Let the field be joyful, and all that is in it. [.linebr]#/# +
Then all the trees of the forest shall rejoice before the LORD.

13 For he comes, [.linebr]#/# +
for he comes to judge the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
He will judge the world with righteousness, [.linebr]#/# +
and the people with his truth.

[#psa097%breakable]
=== Psalm 97

[.outline.text-center]
_The majesty of God's kingdom, 1-6. The church rejoices at God's judgments upon idolaters, 7-9. An exhortation to godliness and gladness, 10-12._

1 The LORD reigns. Let the earth rejoice. [.linebr]#/# +
Let the multitude of islands be glad.

2 Clouds and darkness surround him. [.linebr]#/# +
Righteousness and judgment are the habitation of his throne.

3 A fire goes before him [.linebr]#/# +
and burns up his enemies all around.

4 His lightnings enlightened the world. [.linebr]#/# +
The earth saw and trembled.

5 The hills melted like wax at the presence of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
at the presence of the Lord of the whole earth.

6 The heavens declare his righteousness, [.linebr]#/# +
and all the people see his glory.

[[psa097-007]]7 Confounded are all those who serve engraved images, [.linebr]#/# +
who boast themselves of idols. [.linebr]#/# +
Worship him, all you gods.

8 Zion heard and was glad. [.linebr]#/# +
And the daughters of Judah rejoiced [.linebr]#/# +
because of your judgments, O LORD.

9 For you, LORD, are high above all the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
You are exalted far above all gods.

10 You who love the LORD, hate evil. [.linebr]#/# +
He preserves the souls of his saints. [.linebr]#/# +
He delivers them out of the hand of the wicked.

11 Light is sown for the righteous, [.linebr]#/# +
and gladness for the upright in heart.

12 Rejoice in the LORD, you righteous, [.linebr]#/# +
and give thanks at the remembrance of his holiness.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.7]*: Possibly quoted in xref:#heb001-006[Hebrews 1:6].

[#psa098%breakable]
=== Psalm 98

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist exhorts the Jews, 1-3, the Gentiles, 4-6, and all the creatures to praise God, 7-9._

1 [_A Psalm._]

O sing to the LORD a new song, [.linebr]#/# +
for he has done marvelous things. [.linebr]#/# +
His right hand and his holy arm [.linebr]#/# +
have gotten him the victory.

2 The LORD has made his salvation known. [.linebr]#/# +
His righteousness he has openly shown [.linebr]#/# +
in the sight of the heathen.

3 He has remembered his mercy and his truth [.linebr]#/# +
toward the house of Israel. [.linebr]#/# +
All the ends of the earth [.linebr]#/# +
have seen the salvation of our God.

4 Make a joyful noise to the LORD, all the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
Make a loud noise, rejoice, and sing praise.

5 Sing to the LORD with the harp, [.linebr]#/# +
with the harp and the voice of a psalm.

6 With trumpets and the sound of the horn [.linebr]#/# +
make a joyful noise before the LORD, the King.

7 Let the sea roar and its fullness, [.linebr]#/# +
the world and those who dwell therein.

8 Let the floods clap their hands. [.linebr]#/# +
Let the hills be joyful together

9 Before the LORD, for he comes to judge the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
With righteousness he will judge the world, [.linebr]#/# +
and the people with equity.

[#psa099%breakable]
=== Psalm 99

[.outline.text-center]
_The prophet, setting forth the kingdom of God in Zion, 1-4, exhorts all, by the example of their forefathers, to worship God at his holy hill, 5-9._

1 The LORD reigns. Let the people tremble. [.linebr]#/# +
He sits between the cherubim. Let the earth be moved.

2 The LORD is great in Zion [.linebr]#/# +
and he is high above all people.

3 Let them praise your great and awesome name, [.linebr]#/# +
for it is holy.

4 The king's strength also loves judgment. [.linebr]#/# +
You establish equity. [.linebr]#/# +
You execute judgment and righteousness in Jacob.

5 Exalt the LORD our God [.linebr]#/# +
and worship at his footstool, [.linebr]#/# +
for he is holy.

6 Moses and Aaron were among his priests, [.linebr]#/# +
and Samuel was among those who call upon his name. [.linebr]#/# +
They called upon the LORD, and he answered them.

7 He spoke to them in the cloudy pillar. [.linebr]#/# +
They kept his testimonies [.linebr]#/# +
and the ordinance that he gave them.

8 You answered them, O LORD our God. [.linebr]#/# +
You were a God who forgave them, [.linebr]#/# +
though you took vengeance on their inventions.

9 Exalt the LORD our God [.linebr]#/# +
and worship at his holy hill, [.linebr]#/# +
for the LORD our God is holy.

[#psa100%breakable]
=== Psalm 100

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to praise God cheerfully, 1, 2, for his greatness, 3; and for his power, 4, 5._

1 [_A Psalm of Praise._]

Make a joyful noise to the LORD, all you lands.

2 Serve the LORD with gladness. [.linebr]#/# +
Come before his presence with singing.

3 Know that the LORD himself is God. [.linebr]#/# +
It is he who has made us, and not we ourselves. [.linebr]#/# +
We are his people and the sheep of his pasture.

4 Enter into his gates with thanksgiving [.linebr]#/# +
and into his courts with praise. [.linebr]#/# +
Be thankful to him and bless his name.

5 For the LORD is good. His mercy is everlasting, [.linebr]#/# +
and his truth endures to all generations.

[#psa101%breakable]
=== Psalm 101

[.outline.text-center]
_David makes a vow and profession of godliness, 1-8._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

I will sing of mercy and judgment. [.linebr]#/# +
To you, O LORD, I will sing.

2 I will behave myself wisely in a perfect way. [.linebr]#/# +
O when will you come to me? [.linebr]#/# +
I will walk within my house with a perfect heart.

3 I will set no wicked thing before my eyes. [.linebr]#/# +
I hate the work of those who turn aside. [.linebr]#/# +
It shall not cleave to me.

4 A perverse heart shall depart from me. [.linebr]#/# +
I will not know a wicked person.

5 Whoever secretly slanders his neighbor, [.linebr]#/# +
I will cut him off. [.linebr]#/# +
Him who has a high look and a proud heart, [.linebr]#/# +
I will not endure.

6 My eyes shall be upon the faithful of the land [.linebr]#/# +
so that they may dwell with me. [.linebr]#/# +
He who walks in a perfect way, [.linebr]#/# +
he shall serve me.

7 He who works deceit [.linebr]#/# +
shall not dwell within my house. [.linebr]#/# +
He who tells lies [.linebr]#/# +
shall not remain in my sight.

8 Early I will destroy all the wicked of the land [.linebr]#/# +
so that I may cut off all who practice wickedness [.linebr]#/# +
from the city of the LORD.

[#psa102%breakable]
=== Psalm 102

[.outline.text-center]
_In his prayer, the prophet makes a grievous complaint, 1-11. He takes comfort in the eternity and mercy of God, 12-17. The mercies of God are to be recorded, 18-22. He sustains his weakness by the unchangeableness of God, 23-28._

1 [_A Prayer of the Afflicted: when he is overwhelmed and pours out his complaint before the LORD._]

Hear my prayer, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and let my cry come to you.

2 Do not hide your face from me [.linebr]#/# +
in the day when I am in trouble. [.linebr]#/# +
Incline your ear to me. [.linebr]#/# +
In the day when I call, answer me speedily.

3 For my days are consumed like smoke, [.linebr]#/# +
and my bones are burned like a hearth.

4 My heart is smitten and withered like grass [.linebr]#/# +
so that I forget to eat my bread.

5 By reason of the voice of my groaning, [.linebr]#/# +
my bones cleave to my skin.

6 I am like a pelican of the wilderness. [.linebr]#/# +
I am like an owl of the desert.

7 I watch and am like a sparrow [.linebr]#/# +
alone upon the housetop.

8 My enemies reproach me all the day, [.linebr]#/# +
and those who are enraged against me have sworn against me.

9 For I have eaten ashes like bread [.linebr]#/# +
and mingled my drink with weeping

10 Because of your indignation and your wrath. [.linebr]#/# +
For you have lifted me up and cast me down.

11 My days are like a shadow that declines, [.linebr]#/# +
and I am withered like grass.

12 But you, O LORD, shall endure forever, [.linebr]#/# +
and your remembrance to all generations.

13 You shall arise and have mercy upon Zion, [.linebr]#/# +
for the time to favor her, [.linebr]#/# +
even the set time, has come.

14 For your servants take pleasure in her stones [.linebr]#/# +
and favor the dust thereof.

15 So the heathen shall fear the name of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and all the kings of the earth your glory.

16 When the LORD builds up Zion, [.linebr]#/# +
he will appear in his glory.

17 He will regard the prayer of the destitute [.linebr]#/# +
and not despise their prayer.

18 This shall be written for the generation to come. [.linebr]#/# +
And the people which shall be created shall praise the LORD.

19 For he has looked down from the height of his sanctuary. [.linebr]#/# +
From heaven the LORD has beheld the earth,

20 To hear the groaning of the prisoner, [.linebr]#/# +
to release those who are appointed to death,

21 To declare the name of the LORD in Zion [.linebr]#/# +
and his praise in Jerusalem,

22 When the people are assembled, [.linebr]#/# +
and also the kingdoms, to serve the LORD.

23 He weakened my strength in the way. [.linebr]#/# +
He shortened my days.

24 I said, "O my God, do not take me away [.linebr]#/# +
in the midst of my days. [.linebr]#/# +
Your years are throughout all generations.

[[psa102-025]]25 Of old you have laid the foundation of the earth, [.linebr]#/# +
and the heavens are the work of your hands.

[[psa102-026]]26 They shall perish, but you will endure. [.linebr]#/# +
Indeed, all of them shall grow old like a garment. [.linebr]#/# +
Like a vesture you will change them, [.linebr]#/# +
and they shall be changed.

[[psa102-027]]27 But you are the same, [.linebr]#/# +
and your years will have no end.

28 The children of your servants shall continue, [.linebr]#/# +
and their offspring shall be established before you."

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.25]*: Quoted in xref:#heb001-010[Hebrews 1:10]. *[v.26]*: Quoted in xref:#heb001-011[Hebrews 1:11-12]. *[v.27]*: Quoted in xref:#heb001-012[Hebrews 1:12].

[#psa103%breakable]
=== Psalm 103

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to bless God for his mercy, 1-14, and for the constancy thereof, 15-22._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

Bless the LORD, O my soul. [.linebr]#/# +
And all that is within me, bless his holy name.

2 Bless the LORD, O my soul, [.linebr]#/# +
and do not forget all his benefits.

3 It is he who forgives all your iniquities, [.linebr]#/# +
who heals all your diseases,

4 Who redeems your life from destruction, [.linebr]#/# +
who crowns you with loving-kindness and tender mercies,

5 Who satisfies your mouth with good things [.linebr]#/# +
so that your youth is renewed like the eagle's.

6 The LORD executes righteousness [.linebr]#/# +
and judgment for all who are oppressed.

7 He made his ways known to Moses, [.linebr]#/# +
his acts to the children of Israel.

8 The LORD is merciful and gracious, [.linebr]#/# +
slow to anger, and abundant in mercy.

9 He will not always chide, [.linebr]#/# +
neither will he keep his anger forever.

10 He has not dealt with us according to our sins [.linebr]#/# +
or rewarded us according to our iniquities.

11 For as the heaven is high above the earth, [.linebr]#/# +
so is his mercy great toward those who fear him.

12 As far as the east is from the west, [.linebr]#/# +
so far has he removed our transgressions from us.

13 As a father pities his children, [.linebr]#/# +
so the LORD pities those who fear him.

14 For he knows our frame. [.linebr]#/# +
He remembers that we are dust.

15 As for man, his days are like grass. [.linebr]#/# +
As a flower of the field, so he flourishes.

16 For the wind passes over it, and it is gone, [.linebr]#/# +
and its place shall know it no more.

[[psa103-017]]17 But the mercy of the LORD is from everlasting to everlasting [.linebr]#/# +
upon those who fear him, [.linebr]#/# +
and his righteousness to children's children,

18 To those who keep his covenant, [.linebr]#/# +
and to those who remember his commandments to do them.

19 The LORD has prepared his throne in the heavens, [.linebr]#/# +
and his kingdom rules over all.

20 Bless the LORD, you angels of his, [.linebr]#/# +
who excel in strength, who do his commandments, [.linebr]#/# +
listening to the voice of his word.

21 Bless the LORD, all you hosts of his, [.linebr]#/# +
you ministers of his, who do his pleasure.

22 Bless the LORD, all his works [.linebr]#/# +
in all places of his dominion. [.linebr]#/# +
Bless the LORD, O my soul.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.17]*: Quoted in xref:#luk001-050[Luke 1:50].

[#psa104%breakable]
=== Psalm 104

[.outline.text-center]
_A meditation upon the mighty power, 1-6, and wonderful providence of God, 7-30. God's glory is eternal, 31, 32. The prophet vows perpetually to praise God, 33-35._

1 Bless the LORD, O my soul. [.linebr]#/# +
O LORD my God, you are very great. [.linebr]#/# +
You are clothed with honor and majesty,

2 Who covers himself with light as with a garment, [.linebr]#/# +
who stretches out the heavens like a curtain,

3 Who lays the beams of his chambers in the waters, [.linebr]#/# +
who makes the clouds his chariot, [.linebr]#/# +
who walks upon the wings of the wind,

[[psa104-004]]4 Who makes his angels spirits, [.linebr]#/# +
his ministers a flaming fire,

5 Who laid the foundations of the earth [.linebr]#/# +
so that it should not be moved forever.

6 You covered it with the deep as with a garment. [.linebr]#/# +
The waters stood above the mountains.

7 At your rebuke they fled. [.linebr]#/# +
At the voice of your thunder they hastened away.

8 They go up by the mountains. They go down by the valleys [.linebr]#/# +
to the place which you have founded for them.

9 You have set a bound that they may not pass over [.linebr]#/# +
so that they do not turn back to cover the earth.

10 He sends the springs into the valleys, [.linebr]#/# +
which run among the hills.

11 They give drink to every beast of the field. [.linebr]#/# +
The wild donkeys quench their thirst.

12 By them the birds of the heaven shall have their habitation, [.linebr]#/# +
which sing among the branches.

13 He waters the hills from his chambers. [.linebr]#/# +
The earth is satisfied with the fruit of your works.

14 He causes the grass to grow for the livestock [.linebr]#/# +
and the herb for the service of man [.linebr]#/# +
so that he may bring forth food out of the earth:

15 Wine that rejoices the heart of man, [.linebr]#/# +
oil to cause his face to shine, [.linebr]#/# +
and bread which strengthens man's heart.

16 The trees of the LORD are full of sap, [.linebr]#/# +
the cedars of Lebanon, which he has planted.

17 There the birds make their nests. [.linebr]#/# +
As for the stork, the fir-trees are her house.

18 The high hills are a refuge for the wild goats, [.linebr]#/# +
and the rocks for the conies.

19 He appoints the moon for seasons. [.linebr]#/# +
The sun knows his going down.

20 You make darkness, and it is night, [.linebr]#/# +
in which all the beasts of the forest creep forth.

21 The young lions roar after their prey [.linebr]#/# +
and seek their food from God.

22 The sun arises, and they collect [.linebr]#/# +
and lay themselves down in their dens.

23 Man goes forth to his work [.linebr]#/# +
and to his labor until the evening.

24 O LORD, how manifold your works are! [.linebr]#/# +
In wisdom you have made them all. [.linebr]#/# +
The earth is full of your riches.

25 Thus is this great and wide sea [.linebr]#/# +
in which are moving things innumerable, [.linebr]#/# +
both small and great beasts.

26 There go the ships. [.linebr]#/# +
There is that leviathan which you have made to play therein.

27 These all wait upon you [.linebr]#/# +
so that you may give them their food in due season.

28 That which you give them, they gather. [.linebr]#/# +
You open your hand, and they are filled with good.

29 You hide your face, and they are troubled. [.linebr]#/# +
You take away their breath, and they die [.linebr]#/# +
and return to their dust.

30 You send forth your Spirit, and they are created. [.linebr]#/# +
And you renew the face of the earth.

31 The glory of the LORD shall endure forever. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD shall rejoice in his works.

32 He looks at the earth, and it trembles. [.linebr]#/# +
He touches the hills, and they smoke.

33 I will sing to the LORD as long as I live. [.linebr]#/# +
I will sing praise to my God while I have my being.

34 My meditation of him shall be sweet. [.linebr]#/# +
I will be glad in the LORD.

35 Let sinners be consumed out of the earth, [.linebr]#/# +
and let the wicked be no more. [.linebr]#/# +
Bless the LORD, O my soul. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.4]*: Quoted in xref:#heb001-007[Hebrews 1:7].

[#psa105%breakable]
=== Psalm 105

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to praise God and to seek out his works, 1-6. The story of God's providence over Abraham, 7-15; over Joseph, 16-22; over Jacob in Egypt, 23-25; over Moses delivering the Israelites, 26-36; over the Israelites brought out of Egypt, fed in the wilderness, and planted in Canaan, 37-45._

1 O give thanks to the LORD. Call upon his name. [.linebr]#/# +
Make his deeds known among the people.

2 Sing to him. Sing psalms to him. [.linebr]#/# +
Talk of all his wondrous works.

3 Glory in his holy name. [.linebr]#/# +
Let the heart of those who seek the LORD rejoice.

4 Seek the LORD and his strength. [.linebr]#/# +
Seek his face evermore.

5 Remember his wonderful works which he has done, [.linebr]#/# +
his wonders, and the judgments of his mouth,

6 O you offspring of Abraham his servant, [.linebr]#/# +
you children of Jacob his chosen.

7 He is the LORD our God. [.linebr]#/# +
His judgments are in all the earth.

8 He has remembered his covenant forever, [.linebr]#/# +
the word which he commanded to a thousand generations,

9 Which covenant he made with Abraham, [.linebr]#/# +
and his oath to Isaac,

10 And confirmed the same to Jacob for a law [.linebr]#/# +
and to Israel for an everlasting covenant,

11 Saying, "To you I will give the land of Canaan, [.linebr]#/# +
the lot of your inheritance,"

12 When they were a few men in number, [.linebr]#/# +
even very few, and strangers in it.

13 When they went from one nation to another, [.linebr]#/# +
from one kingdom to another people,

14 He allowed no man to do them wrong. [.linebr]#/# +
He even reproved kings for their sakes,

15 Saying, "Do not touch my anointed [.linebr]#/# +
and do my prophets no harm."

16 Moreover, he called for a famine upon the land. [.linebr]#/# +
He broke the whole staff of bread.

17 He sent a man before them, [.linebr]#/# +
even Joseph, who was sold for a servant.

18 They hurt his feet with fetters, [.linebr]#/# +
and he was laid in iron.

19 Until the time that his word came to pass, [.linebr]#/# +
the word of the LORD tried him.

20 The king sent and released him, [.linebr]#/# +
even the ruler of the people, and let him go free.

21 He made him lord of his house [.linebr]#/# +
and ruler of all his substance,

22 To bind his princes at his pleasure [.linebr]#/# +
and teach his elders wisdom.

23 Israel also came into Egypt, [.linebr]#/# +
and Jacob sojourned in the land of Ham.

24 And he increased his people greatly [.linebr]#/# +
and made them stronger than their enemies.

25 He turned their heart to hate his people, [.linebr]#/# +
to deal subtly with his servants.

26 He sent Moses his servant [.linebr]#/# +
and Aaron whom he had chosen.

27 They showed his signs among them [.linebr]#/# +
and wonders in the land of Ham.

28 He sent darkness and made it dark, [.linebr]#/# +
and they did not rebel against his word.

29 He turned their waters into blood [.linebr]#/# +
and slew their fish.

30 Their land brought forth frogs in abundance [.linebr]#/# +
in the chambers of their kings.

31 He spoke, and there came swarms of flies [.linebr]#/# +
and lice in all their borders.

32 He gave them hail for rain [.linebr]#/# +
and flaming fire in their land.

33 He also smote their vines and their fig-trees [.linebr]#/# +
and broke the trees of their borders.

34 He spoke, and the swarming-locusts [.linebr]#/# +
and licking-locusts came—and that without number—

35 And ate up all the herbs in their land [.linebr]#/# +
and devoured the fruit of their ground.

36 He also smote all the first-born in their land, [.linebr]#/# +
the chief of all their strength.

37 He also brought them forth with silver and gold. [.linebr]#/# +
And there was not one feeble person among their tribes.

38 Egypt was glad when they departed, [.linebr]#/# +
for the fear of them fell upon them.

39 He spread a cloud for a covering [.linebr]#/# +
and fire to give light in the night.

40 The people asked, and he brought quails [.linebr]#/# +
and satisfied them with the bread of heaven.

41 He opened the rock, and the waters gushed out. [.linebr]#/# +
They ran in the dry places like a river.

42 For he remembered his holy promise [.linebr]#/# +
and Abraham his servant.

43 And he brought forth his people with joy [.linebr]#/# +
and his chosen with gladness.

44 He gave them the lands of the heathen, [.linebr]#/# +
and they inherited the labor of the people,

45 So that they might observe his statutes [.linebr]#/# +
and keep his laws. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD.

[#psa106%breakable]
=== Psalm 106

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist exhorts to praise God, 1-3. He prays for pardon of sin, as God pardoned the fathers, 4-6. The story of the people's rebellion and God's mercy, 7-46. He concludes with prayer and praise, 47, 48._

1 Praise the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
O give thanks to the LORD, for he is good. [.linebr]#/# +
For his mercy endures forever.

2 Who can utter the mighty acts of the LORD? [.linebr]#/# +
Who can show forth all his praise?

3 Blessed are those who keep judgment [.linebr]#/# +
and he who does righteousness at all times.

4 Remember me, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
with the favor that you bear to your people. [.linebr]#/# +
O visit me with your salvation

5 So that I may see the good of your chosen, [.linebr]#/# +
so that I may rejoice in the gladness of your nation, [.linebr]#/# +
so that I may glory with your inheritance.

6 We have sinned with our fathers. [.linebr]#/# +
We have committed iniquity. We have done wickedly.

7 Our fathers did not understand your wonders in Egypt. [.linebr]#/# +
They did not remember the multitude of your mercies, [.linebr]#/# +
but provoked him at the sea, even at the Red Sea.

8 Nevertheless, he saved them for his name's sake [.linebr]#/# +
so that he might make his mighty power to be known.

9 He rebuked the Red Sea also, and it was dried up. [.linebr]#/# +
Thus he led them through the depths, as through the wilderness.

[[psa106-010]]10 And he saved them from the hand of him who hated them [.linebr]#/# +
and redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.

11 And the waters covered their enemies. [.linebr]#/# +
There was not one of them left.

12 Then they believed his words. [.linebr]#/# +
They sang his praise.

13 They soon forgot his works. [.linebr]#/# +
They did not wait for his counsel,

14 But lusted exceedingly in the wilderness [.linebr]#/# +
and tested God in the desert.

15 And he gave them their request, [.linebr]#/# +
but sent leanness into their soul.

16 In the camp they also envied Moses [.linebr]#/# +
and Aaron, the saint of the LORD.

17 The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan [.linebr]#/# +
and covered the company of Abiram.

18 And a fire was kindled in their company. [.linebr]#/# +
The flame burned up the wicked.

19 They made a calf in Horeb [.linebr]#/# +
and worshiped the molten image.

20 Thus they changed their glory [.linebr]#/# +
into the similitude of an ox that eats grass.

21 They forgot God their Savior [.linebr]#/# +
who had done great things in Egypt,

22 Wondrous works in the land of Ham [.linebr]#/# +
and awesome things by the Red Sea;

23 Therefore, he said that he would destroy them, [.linebr]#/# +
had Moses his chosen not stood before him in the breach [.linebr]#/# +
to turn away his wrath, lest he should destroy them.

24 They even despised the pleasant land [.linebr]#/# +
and did not believe his word,

25 But murmured in their tents [.linebr]#/# +
and did not listen to the voice of the LORD;

26 Therefore, he lifted up his hand against them [.linebr]#/# +
to overthrow them in the wilderness,

27 To overthrow their offspring also among the nations, [.linebr]#/# +
and to scatter them in the lands.

28 They joined themselves also to Baal-peor [.linebr]#/# +
and ate the sacrifices of the dead.

29 Thus they provoked him to anger with their inventions, [.linebr]#/# +
and the plague broke in upon them.

30 Then Phinehas stood up and executed judgment. [.linebr]#/# +
And so the plague was stayed.

31 And that was counted to him for righteousness [.linebr]#/# +
to all generations forever.

32 They also angered him at the waters of strife [.linebr]#/# +
so that it went ill with Moses for their sakes,

33 For they provoked his spirit [.linebr]#/# +
and he spoke unadvisedly with his lips.

34 They did not destroy the nations, [.linebr]#/# +
concerning whom the LORD commanded them,

35 But were mingled among the heathen [.linebr]#/# +
and learned their works.

36 And they served their idols, [.linebr]#/# +
which were a snare to them.

37 They even sacrificed their sons and their daughters to demons,

38 And shed innocent blood, [.linebr]#/# +
even the blood of their sons and of their daughters, [.linebr]#/# +
whom they sacrificed to the idols of Canaan. [.linebr]#/# +
And the land was polluted with blood.

39 Thus they were defiled with their own works [.linebr]#/# +
and went astray with their own inventions.

40 Therefore, the wrath of the LORD was kindled against his people [.linebr]#/# +
because he abhorred his own inheritance.

41 And he gave them into the hand of the heathen, [.linebr]#/# +
and those who hated them ruled over them.

42 Their enemies also oppressed them, [.linebr]#/# +
and they were brought into subjection under their hand.

43 Many times he delivered them, [.linebr]#/# +
but they provoked him with their counsel [.linebr]#/# +
and were brought low for their iniquity.

44 Nevertheless, he regarded their affliction [.linebr]#/# +
when he heard their cry.

45 And he remembered for them his covenant [.linebr]#/# +
and repented according to the multitude of his mercies.

46 He also made them to be pitied [.linebr]#/# +
by all those who carried them captive.

47 Save us, O LORD our God, [.linebr]#/# +
and gather us from among the heathen [.linebr]#/# +
so that we may give thanks to your holy name [.linebr]#/# +
and triumph in your praise.

48 Blessed be the LORD God of Israel [.linebr]#/# +
from everlasting to everlasting. [.linebr]#/# +
And let all the people say, "Amen." [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.10]*: Quoted in xref:#luk001-071[Luke 1:71].

[#psalms-book-5%breakable]
=== BOOK V

[#psa107%breakable]
=== Psalm 107

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist exhorts the redeemed to praise God and to observe his manifold providence, 1-3, over travelers, 4-9; over captives, 10-16; over sick men, 17-22; over sailors, 23-32; and in many varieties of life, 33-43._

1 O give thanks to the LORD, for he is good. [.linebr]#/# +
For his mercy endures forever.

2 Let the redeemed of the LORD say so, [.linebr]#/# +
whom he has redeemed from the hand of the enemy

3 And gathered out of the lands [.linebr]#/# +
from the east, from the west, [.linebr]#/# +
from the north, and from the south.

4 They wandered in the wilderness in a solitary way. [.linebr]#/# +
They found no city to dwell in.

5 Hungry and thirsty, [.linebr]#/# +
their soul fainted in them.

6 Then they cried to the LORD in their trouble, [.linebr]#/# +
and he delivered them out of their distresses.

7 And he led them forth by the right way [.linebr]#/# +
so that they might go to a city of habitation.

8 Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness [.linebr]#/# +
and for his wonderful works to the children of men!

[[psa107-009]]9 For he satisfies the longing soul [.linebr]#/# +
and fills the hungry soul with goodness.

10 There are those who sit in darkness and in the shadow of death, [.linebr]#/# +
being bound in affliction and iron,

11 Because they rebelled against the words of God [.linebr]#/# +
and despised the counsel of the Most High.

12 Therefore, he brought down their heart with labor. [.linebr]#/# +
They fell down, and there was no one to help.

13 Then they cried to the LORD in their trouble, [.linebr]#/# +
and he saved them out of their distresses.
