14 He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of death [.linebr]#/# +
and broke their bonds apart.

15 Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness [.linebr]#/# +
and for his wonderful works to the children of men!

16 For he has broken the gates of brass [.linebr]#/# +
and cut the bars of iron apart.

17 Fools, because of their transgression [.linebr]#/# +
and because of their iniquities, are afflicted.

18 Their soul abhors all manner of food, [.linebr]#/# +
and they draw near to the gates of death.

19 Then they cry to the LORD in their trouble, [.linebr]#/# +
and he saves them out of their distresses.

20 He sent his word and healed them [.linebr]#/# +
and delivered them from their destructions.

21 Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness [.linebr]#/# +
and for his wonderful works to the children of men!

22 And let them sacrifice the sacrifices of thanksgiving [.linebr]#/# +
and declare his works with rejoicing.

23 Those who go down to the sea in ships, [.linebr]#/# +
who do business on great waters,

24 These see the works of the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
and his wonders in the deep.

25 For he commands and raises the stormy wind, [.linebr]#/# +
which lifts up its waves.

26 They mount up to the heaven. [.linebr]#/# +
They go down again to the depths. [.linebr]#/# +
Their soul is melted because of trouble.

27 They reel to and fro and stagger like a drunken man. [.linebr]#/# +
They are at their wit's end.

28 Then they cry to the LORD in their trouble, [.linebr]#/# +
and he brings them out of their distresses.

29 He calms the storm to a gentle breeze [.linebr]#/# +
so that the waves of the sea are still.

30 Then they are glad because they are quiet. [.linebr]#/# +
Thus he brings them to their desired haven.

31 Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness [.linebr]#/# +
and for his wonderful works to the children of men!

32 Let them exalt him also in the congregation of the people [.linebr]#/# +
and praise him in the assembly of the elders.

33 He turns rivers into a wilderness, [.linebr]#/# +
the water-springs into dry ground,

34 And a fruitful land into barrenness [.linebr]#/# +
because of the wickedness of those who dwell in it.

35 He turns the wilderness into a standing water [.linebr]#/# +
and dry ground into water-springs.

36 And there he makes the hungry to dwell [.linebr]#/# +
so that they may prepare a city for habitation.

37 They sow the fields and plant vineyards, [.linebr]#/# +
which yield fruits of increase.

38 He also blesses them so that they are multiplied greatly. [.linebr]#/# +
He does not allow their livestock to decrease.

39 Again, they are diminished and brought low [.linebr]#/# +
through oppression, affliction, and sorrow.

40 He pours contempt upon princes [.linebr]#/# +
and causes them to wander in the wilderness where there is no way.

41 Yet he sets the poor on high from affliction [.linebr]#/# +
and increases their families like a flock.

42 The righteous shall see it and rejoice, [.linebr]#/# +
and all iniquity shall stop her mouth.

43 Whoever is wise and will observe these things, [.linebr]#/# +
even they shall understand the loving-kindness of the LORD.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.9]*: Quoted in xref:#luk001-053[Luke 1:53].

[#psa108%breakable]
=== Psalm 108

[.outline.text-center]
_David encourages himself to praise God, 1-4. He prays for God's assistance according to his promise, 5-10. His confidence in God's help, 11-13._

1 [_A Song or Psalm of David._]

O God, my heart is fixed. [.linebr]#/# +
I will sing and give praise, even with my glory.

2 Awake, psaltery and harp. [.linebr]#/# +
I myself will awake early.

3 I will praise you, O LORD, among the people, [.linebr]#/# +
and I will sing praises to you among the nations.

4 For your mercy is great above the heavens, [.linebr]#/# +
and your truth reaches to the clouds.

5 Be exalted, O God, above the heavens, [.linebr]#/# +
and your glory above all the earth,

6 So that your beloved may be delivered. [.linebr]#/# +
Save with your right hand, and answer me.

7 God has spoken in his holiness: "I will rejoice. [.linebr]#/# +
I will divide Shechem [.linebr]#/# +
and measure out the valley of Succoth.

8 Gilead is mine. [.linebr]#/# +
Manasseh is mine. [.linebr]#/# +
Ephraim also is the strength of my head. [.linebr]#/# +
Judah is my lawgiver.

9 Moab is my wash-pot. [.linebr]#/# +
Over Edom I will cast out my shoe. [.linebr]#/# +
Over Philistia I will triumph."

10 Who will bring me into the strong city? [.linebr]#/# +
Who will lead me into Edom?

11 Will you not, O God, who have cast us off? [.linebr]#/# +
And will you not, O God, go forth with our armies?

12 Give us help from trouble, [.linebr]#/# +
for vain is the help of man.

13 Through God we shall do valiantly, [.linebr]#/# +
for he will tread down our enemies.

[#psa109%breakable]
=== Psalm 109

[.outline.text-center]
_David speaks against his slanderous enemies, 1-5. He prays against them and declares God's judgment, 6-15. He shows their sin, 16-20. Bemoaning his own misery, he prays for help, 21-28. He promises thankfulness, 29-31._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

Do not hold your peace, O God of my praise,

2 For the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of the deceitful [.linebr]#/# +
are opened against me. [.linebr]#/# +
They have spoken against me [.linebr]#/# +
with a lying tongue.

3 They encompassed me also with words of hatred [.linebr]#/# +
and fought against me without a cause.

4 For my love they are my adversaries, [.linebr]#/# +
but I give myself to prayer.

5 And they have rewarded me evil for good [.linebr]#/# +
and hatred for my love.

6 Set a wicked man over him, [.linebr]#/# +
and let Satan stand at his right hand.

7 When he is judged, let him be condemned [.linebr]#/# +
and let his prayer become sin.

[[psa109-008]]8 Let his days be few [.linebr]#/# +
and let another take his office.

9 Let his children be fatherless [.linebr]#/# +
and his wife a widow.

10 Let his children continually wander around and beg. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them also seek their bread out of their desolate places.

11 Let the extortioner catch all that he has, [.linebr]#/# +
and let strangers plunder his labor.

12 Let there be no one to extend mercy to him, [.linebr]#/# +
neither let there be any to favor his fatherless children.

13 Let his posterity be cut off, [.linebr]#/# +
and in the generation following let their name be blotted out.

14 Let the iniquity of his fathers be remembered with the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and do not let the sin of his mother be blotted out.

15 Let them be before the LORD continually [.linebr]#/# +
so that he may cut off their memory from the earth.

16 For he did not remember to show mercy, [.linebr]#/# +
but persecuted the poor and needy man [.linebr]#/# +
so that he might even slay the broken in heart.

17 As he loved cursing, so let it come to him. [.linebr]#/# +
As he did not delight in blessing, so let it be far from him.

18 As he clothed himself with cursing as with his garment, [.linebr]#/# +
so let it come into his body like water [.linebr]#/# +
and like oil into his bones.

19 Let it be to him as the garment which covers him [.linebr]#/# +
and for a girdle with which he is girded continually.

20 Let this be the reward of my adversaries from the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
and of those who speak evil against my soul.

21 But deal with me, O Yahweh the Lord, for your name's sake. [.linebr]#/# +
Because your mercy is good, deliver me.

22 For I am poor and needy, [.linebr]#/# +
and my heart is wounded within me.

23 I am gone like the shadow when it declines. [.linebr]#/# +
I am tossed up and down like the locust.

24 My knees are weak through fasting, [.linebr]#/# +
and my flesh fails of fatness.

25 I also became a reproach to them. [.linebr]#/# +
When they looked upon me, they shook their heads.

26 Help me, O LORD my God. [.linebr]#/# +
O save me according to your mercy,

27 So that they may know that this is your hand, [.linebr]#/# +
that you, LORD, have done it.

28 They may curse, but you bless. [.linebr]#/# +
When they arise, let them be ashamed, [.linebr]#/# +
but let your servant rejoice.

29 Let my adversaries be clothed with shame, [.linebr]#/# +
and let them cover themselves with their own shame [.linebr]#/# +
as with a mantle.

30 I will greatly praise the LORD with my mouth. [.linebr]#/# +
I will even praise him among the multitude.

31 For he will stand at the right hand of the poor [.linebr]#/# +
to save him from those who condemn his soul.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.8]*: Quoted in xref:#act001-020[Acts 1:20].

[#psa110%breakable]
=== Psalm 110

[.outline.text-center]
_The kingdom, 1-3; the priesthood, 4; the conquest, 5, 6; and the passion of Christ, 7._

[[psa110-001]]1 [_A Psalm of David._]

The LORD said to my Lord, "Sit at my right hand [.linebr]#/# +
until I make your enemies your footstool."

2 The LORD will send the rod of your strength out of Zion. [.linebr]#/# +
Rule in the midst of your enemies.

3 Your people shall be willing [.linebr]#/# +
in the day of your power, in the beauties of holiness. [.linebr]#/# +
From the womb of the morning, [.linebr]#/# +
you have the dew of your youth.

[[psa110-004]]4 The LORD has sworn and will not repent, [.linebr]#/# +
"You are a priest forever [.linebr]#/# +
after the order of Melchizedek."

5 The Lord at your right hand [.linebr]#/# +
will strike through kings in the day of his wrath.

6 He will judge among the heathen. [.linebr]#/# +
He will fill the places with the dead bodies. [.linebr]#/# +
He will wound the heads over many countries.

7 He will drink from the brook in the way. [.linebr]#/# +
Therefore, he will lift up the head.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.1]*: Quoted in xref:#mth022-044[Matthew 22:44], xref:#mth026-064[26:64]; xref:#mrk012-036[Mark 12:36], xref:#mrk014-062[14:62]; xref:#luk020-042[Luke 20:42-43]; xref:#act002-034[Acts 2:34-35]; xref:#heb001-013[Hebrews 1:13], xref:#heb010-012[10:12-13]. *[v.4]*: Quoted in xref:#heb005-006[Hebrews 5:6], xref:#heb006-020[6:20], xref:#heb007-017[7:17], xref:#heb007-021[7:21].

[#psa111%breakable]
=== Psalm 111

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist, by his example, incites others to praise God for his glorious, 1-4, and gracious works, 5-9. The fear of God is the beginning of true wisdom, 10._

1 Praise the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
I will praise the LORD with my whole heart [.linebr]#/# +
in the assembly of the upright and in the congregation.

2 The works of the LORD are great, [.linebr]#/# +
sought out by all those who have pleasure in them.

3 His work is honorable and glorious, [.linebr]#/# +
and his righteousness endures forever.

4 He has made his wonderful works to be remembered. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD is gracious and full of compassion.

5 He has given food to those who fear him. [.linebr]#/# +
He will always be mindful of his covenant.

6 He has shown his people the power of his works [.linebr]#/# +
so that he may give them the heritage of the heathen.

7 The works of his hands are verity and judgment. [.linebr]#/# +
All his commandments are sure.

8 They stand fast forever and ever [.linebr]#/# +
and are done in truth and uprightness.

9 He sent redemption to his people. [.linebr]#/# +
He has commanded his covenant forever. [.linebr]#/# +
Holy and awesome is his name.

10 The fear of the LORD is the beginning of wisdom. [.linebr]#/# +
All those who do his commandments have a good understanding. [.linebr]#/# +
His praise endures forever.

[#psa112%breakable]
=== Psalm 112

[.outline.text-center]
_Godliness has the promises of this life, 1-3, and of the life to come, 4-9. The prosperity of the godly shall be an eyesore to the wicked, 10._

1 Praise the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Blessed is the man who fears the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
who delights greatly in his commandments.

2 His offspring shall be mighty upon earth. [.linebr]#/# +
The generation of the upright shall be blessed.

3 Wealth and riches shall be in his house, [.linebr]#/# +
and his righteousness endures forever.

4 To the upright there arises light in darkness. [.linebr]#/# +
He is gracious, full of compassion, and righteous.

5 A good man shows favor and lends. [.linebr]#/# +
He will guide his affairs with discretion.

6 Surely he shall not be moved forever. [.linebr]#/# +
The righteous shall be in everlasting remembrance.

7 He shall not be afraid of evil tidings. [.linebr]#/# +
His heart is fixed, trusting in the LORD.

8 His heart is established. He shall not be afraid [.linebr]#/# +
until he sees his desire upon his enemies.

[[psa112-009]]9 He has dispersed. He has given to the poor. [.linebr]#/# +
His righteousness endures forever. [.linebr]#/# +
His horn shall be exalted with honor.

10 The wicked shall see it and be grieved. [.linebr]#/# +
He shall gnash with his teeth and melt away. [.linebr]#/# +
The desire of the wicked shall perish.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.9]*: Quoted in xref:#sco009-009[2nd Corinthians 9:9].

[#psa113%breakable]
=== Psalm 113

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to praise God for his excellency, 1-5; for his mercy, 6-9._

1 Praise the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise, O servants of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
praise the name of the LORD.

2 Blessed be the name of the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
from this time forth and forevermore.

3 From the rising of the sun to the going down of the same, [.linebr]#/# +
the LORD'S name is to be praised.

4 The LORD is high above all nations, [.linebr]#/# +
and his glory above the heavens.

5 Who is like the LORD our God [.linebr]#/# +
who dwells on high,

6 Who humbles himself to behold [.linebr]#/# +
the things that are in heaven and in the earth?

7 He raises the poor out of the dust [.linebr]#/# +
and lifts the needy out of the dunghill

8 So that he may set him with princes, [.linebr]#/# +
even with the princes of his people.

9 He makes the barren woman to keep house [.linebr]#/# +
and to be a joyful mother of children. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD.

[#psa114%breakable]
=== Psalm 114

[.outline.text-center]
_The miracles wrought by God when he brought his people out of Egypt are a just ground for fearing him, 1-8._

1 When Israel went out of Egypt, [.linebr]#/# +
the house of Jacob from a people of a foreign language,

2 Judah was his sanctuary, [.linebr]#/# +
and Israel his dominion.

3 The sea saw it and fled. [.linebr]#/# +
The Jordan was driven back.

4 The mountains skipped like rams, [.linebr]#/# +
and the little hills like lambs.

5 What ailed you, O sea, that you fled; [.linebr]#/# +
O Jordan, that you were driven back;

6 O mountains, that you skipped like rams; [.linebr]#/# +
O little hills, like lambs?

7 Tremble, you earth, at the presence of the Lord, [.linebr]#/# +
at the presence of the God of Jacob,

8 Who turned the rock into a standing water, [.linebr]#/# +
the flint into a fountain of waters.

[#psa115%breakable]
=== Psalm 115

[.outline.text-center]
_Because God is truly glorious, 1-3, and idols are vanity, 4-8, the psalmist exhorts to confidence in God, 9-11. God is to be blessed for his blessings, 12-18._

1 Not to us, O LORD, not to us, [.linebr]#/# +
but to your name give glory [.linebr]#/# +
for your mercy and for your truth's sake.

2 Why should the heathen say, [.linebr]#/# +
"Where now is their God?"

3 But our God is in the heavens. [.linebr]#/# +
He has done whatever he pleased.

4 Their idols are silver and gold, [.linebr]#/# +
the work of men's hands.

5 They have mouths, but they do not speak. [.linebr]#/# +
They have eyes, but they do not see.

6 They have ears, but they do not hear. [.linebr]#/# +
They have noses, but they do not smell.

7 They have hands, but they do not handle. [.linebr]#/# +
They have feet, but they do not walk. [.linebr]#/# +
They do not speak through their throat.

8 Those who make them are like them, [.linebr]#/# +
and so is everyone who trusts in them.

9 O Israel, trust in the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
He is their help and their shield.

10 O house of Aaron, trust in the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
He is their help and their shield.

11 You who fear the LORD, trust in the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
He is their help and their shield.

12 The LORD has been mindful of us. [.linebr]#/# +
He will bless us. [.linebr]#/# +
He will bless the house of Israel. [.linebr]#/# +
He will bless the house of Aaron.

13 He will bless those who fear the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
both small and great.

14 The LORD will increase you more and more— [.linebr]#/# +
you and your children.

15 You are blessed of the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
who made heaven and earth.

16 The heaven, even the heavens, are the LORD'S, [.linebr]#/# +
but the earth he has given to the children of men.

17 The dead do not praise the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
neither any who go down into silence.

18 But we will bless the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
from this time forth and forever. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD.

[#psa116%breakable]
=== Psalm 116

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist professes his love and duty to God for his deliverance, 1-11. He gives diligence to be thankful, 12-19._

1 I love the LORD because he has heard [.linebr]#/# +
my voice and my supplications.

2 Because he has inclined his ear to me, [.linebr]#/# +
therefore I will call upon him as long as I live.

3 The sorrows of death encompassed me, [.linebr]#/# +
and the pains of hell came upon me. [.linebr]#/# +
I found trouble and sorrow.

4 Then I called upon the name of the LORD: [.linebr]#/# +
"O LORD, I implore you, deliver my soul."

5 Gracious is the LORD, and righteous. [.linebr]#/# +
Indeed, our God is merciful.

6 The LORD preserves the simple. [.linebr]#/# +
I was brought low, and he helped me.

7 Return to your rest, O my soul, [.linebr]#/# +
for the LORD has dealt bountifully with you.

8 For you have delivered my soul from death, [.linebr]#/# +
my eyes from tears, [.linebr]#/# +
and my feet from falling.

9 I will walk before the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
in the land of the living.

[[psa116-010]]10 I believed; therefore, I said, [.linebr]#/# +
"I was greatly afflicted."

11 I said in my haste, [.linebr]#/# +
"All men are liars."

12 What shall I render to the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
for all his benefits toward me?

13 I will take the cup of salvation [.linebr]#/# +
and call upon the name of the LORD.

14 I will pay my vows to the LORD now [.linebr]#/# +
in the presence of all his people.

15 Precious in the sight of the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
is the death of his saints.

16 O LORD, truly I am your servant. [.linebr]#/# +
I am your servant, the son of your woman-servant. [.linebr]#/# +
You have loosened my bonds.

17 I will offer to you the sacrifice of thanksgiving [.linebr]#/# +
and will call upon the name of the LORD.

18 I will pay my vows to the LORD now [.linebr]#/# +
in the presence of all his people,

19 In the courts of the LORD'S house, [.linebr]#/# +
in the midst of you, O Jerusalem. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD.

*[v.10]*: Quoted in xref:#sco004-013[2nd Corinthians 4:13].

[#psa117%breakable]

And the truth of the LORD endures forever. [.linebr]#/# +

[#psa118%breakable]
=== Psalm 118

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to praise God for his mercy, 1-4. The psalmist, by his experience, shows how good it is to trust in God, 5-18. Under the type of the psalmist the coming of Christ in his kingdom is expressed, 19-29._

1 O give thanks to the LORD, for he is good. [.linebr]#/# +
For his mercy endures forever.

2 Let Israel now say [.linebr]#/# +
that his mercy endures forever.

3 Let the house of Aaron now say [.linebr]#/# +
that his mercy endures forever.

4 Let those who fear the LORD now say [.linebr]#/# +
that his mercy endures forever.

5 I called upon the LORD in distress. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD answered me and set me in a large place.

[[psa118-006]]6 The LORD is on my side. [.linebr]#/# +
I will not fear. [.linebr]#/# +
What can man do to me?

7 The LORD takes my part with those who help me; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, I shall see my desire upon those who hate me.

8 It is better to trust in the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
than to put confidence in man.

9 It is better to trust in the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
than to put confidence in princes.

10 All nations encompassed me, [.linebr]#/# +
but in the name of the LORD I will destroy them.

11 They encompassed me. Yes, they encompassed me, [.linebr]#/# +
but in the name of the LORD I will destroy them.

12 They encompassed me like bees. [.linebr]#/# +
They are quenched like the fire of thorns, [.linebr]#/# +
for in the name of the LORD I will destroy them.

13 You have violently thrust at me so that I might fall, [.linebr]#/# +
but the LORD helped me.

14 The LORD is my strength and song [.linebr]#/# +
and has become my salvation.

15 The voice of rejoicing and salvation [.linebr]#/# +
is in the tabernacles of the righteous. [.linebr]#/# +
The right hand of the LORD does valiantly.

16 The right hand of the LORD is exalted. [.linebr]#/# +
The right hand of the LORD does valiantly.

17 I shall not die, but live [.linebr]#/# +
and declare the works of the LORD.

18 The LORD has chastened me severely, [.linebr]#/# +
but he has not given me over to death.

19 Open to me the gates of righteousness. [.linebr]#/# +
I will enter them, and I will praise the LORD.

20 This is the gate of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
into which the righteous shall enter.

21 I will praise you, for you have heard me [.linebr]#/# +
and have become my salvation.

[[psa118-022]]22 The stone which the builders refused [.linebr]#/# +
has become the head stone of the corner.

[[psa118-023]]23 This is the LORD'S doing. [.linebr]#/# +
It is wonderful in our eyes.

24 This is the day which the LORD has made. [.linebr]#/# +
We will rejoice and be glad in it.

[[psa118-025]]25 Save now, I implore you, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
O LORD, I implore you, send prosperity now.

[[psa118-026]]26 Blessed is he who comes in the name of the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
We have blessed you out of the house of the LORD.

27 God is the LORD, who has shown us light. [.linebr]#/# +
Bind the sacrifice with cords, [.linebr]#/# +
even to the horns of the altar.

28 You are my God, and I will praise you. [.linebr]#/# +
My God, I will exalt you.

29 O give thanks to the LORD, for he is good. [.linebr]#/# +
For his mercy endures forever.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.6]*: Quoted in xref:#heb013-006[Hebrews 13:6]. *[v.22]*: Quoted in xref:#mth021-042[Matthew 21:42]; xref:#mrk012-010[Mark 12:10]; xref:#luk020-017[Luke 20:17]; xref:#act004-011[Acts 4:11]; xref:#fpe002-007[1st Peter 2:7]. *[v.23]*: Quoted in xref:#mth021-042[Matthew 21:42]; xref:#mrk012-011[Mark 12:11]. *[v.26]*: Quoted in xref:#mrk011-009[Mark 11:9]; xref:#jhn012-013[John 12:13]. *[v.26]*: Quoted in xref:#mth021-009[Matthew 21:9], xref:#mth023-039[23:39]; xref:#mrk011-009[Mark 11:9]; xref:#luk013-035[Luke 13:35], xref:#luk019-038[19:38]; xref:#jhn012-013[John 12:13].

[#psa119%breakable]
=== Psalm 119

[.outline.text-center]
_This psalm contains various prayers, praises, and professions of obedience, 1-176._

+[+ _ALEPH_ - א +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|1 Blessed are the undefiled in the way, [.linebr]#/# +
who walk in the law of the LORD.

|
|2 Blessed are those who keep his testimonies, [.linebr]#/# +
who seek him with the whole heart.

|
|3 They also do no iniquity. [.linebr]#/# +
They walk in his ways.

|
|4 You have commanded us [.linebr]#/# +
to keep your precepts diligently.

|
|5 O that my ways were directed [.linebr]#/# +
to keep your statutes!

|
|6 Then I shall not be ashamed [.linebr]#/# +
when I have respect for all your commandments.

|
|7 I will praise you with uprightness of heart [.linebr]#/# +
when I have learned your righteous judgments.

|
|8 I will keep your statutes. [.linebr]#/# +
O do not forsake me utterly.
|===

+[+ _BET_ - ב +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|9 How shall a young man cleanse his way? [.linebr]#/# +
By taking heed to it, according to your word.

|
|10 With my whole heart I have sought you. [.linebr]#/# +
O do not let me wander from your commandments.

|
|11 I have hid your word in my heart [.linebr]#/# +
so that I might not sin against you.

|
|12 Blessed are you, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Teach me your statutes.

|
|13 With my lips I have declared [.linebr]#/# +
all the judgments of your mouth.

|
|14 I have rejoiced in the way of your testimonies [.linebr]#/# +
as much as in all riches.

|
|15 I will meditate in your precepts [.linebr]#/# +
and have respect for your ways.

|
|16 I will delight myself in your statutes. [.linebr]#/# +
I will not forget your word.
|===

+[+ _GIMEL_ - ג +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|17 Deal bountifully with your servant [.linebr]#/# +
so that I may live and keep your word.

|
|18 Open my eyes so that I may behold [.linebr]#/# +
wondrous things out of your law.

|
|19 I am a stranger in the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not hide your commandments from me.

|
|20 My soul breaks for the longing [.linebr]#/# +
that it has to your judgments at all times.

|
|21 You have rebuked the proud who are cursed, [.linebr]#/# +
who err from your commandments.

|
|22 Remove from me reproach and contempt, [.linebr]#/# +
for I have kept your testimonies.

|
|23 Princes also sat and spoke against me, [.linebr]#/# +
but your servant meditated in your statutes.

|
|24 Your testimonies are also my delight [.linebr]#/# +
and my counselors.
|===

+[+ _DALET_ - ד +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|25 My soul cleaves to the dust. [.linebr]#/# +
Revive me according to your word.

|
|26 I have declared my ways, and you heard me. [.linebr]#/# +
Teach me your statutes.

|
|27 Make me to understand the way of your precepts, [.linebr]#/# +
and I shall talk of your wondrous works.

|
|28 My soul melts for heaviness. [.linebr]#/# +
Strengthen me according to your word.

|
|29 Remove from me the way of lying [.linebr]#/# +
and grant me your law graciously.

|
|30 I have chosen the way of truth. [.linebr]#/# +
Your judgments I have laid before me.

|
|31 I have adhered to your testimonies. [.linebr]#/# +
O LORD, do not put me to shame.

|
|32 I will run the way of your commandments [.linebr]#/# +
when you enlarge my heart.
|===

+[+ _HE_ - ה +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|33 Teach me, O LORD, the way of your statutes, [.linebr]#/# +
and I shall keep it to the end.

|
|34 Give me understanding, and I shall keep your law. [.linebr]#/# +
I shall even observe it with my whole heart.

|
|35 Make me to go in the path of your commandments, [.linebr]#/# +
for in that I delight.

|
|36 Incline my heart to your testimonies [.linebr]#/# +
and not to covetousness.

|
|37 Turn away my eyes from beholding vanity [.linebr]#/# +
and revive me in your way.

|
|38 Establish your word to your servant [.linebr]#/# +
who is devoted to your fear.

|
|39 Turn away my reproach which I fear, [.linebr]#/# +
for your judgments are good.

|
|40 Behold, I have longed after your precepts. [.linebr]#/# +
Revive me in your righteousness.
|===

+[+ _VAV_ - ו +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|41 Let your mercies come also to me, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
even your salvation, according to your word.

|
|42 And I shall have an answer for him who reproaches me, [.linebr]#/# +
for I trust in your word.

|
|43 And do not take the word of truth utterly out of my mouth, [.linebr]#/# +
for I have hoped in your judgments.

|
|44 And I shall keep your law continually [.linebr]#/# +
forever and ever.

|
|45 And I will walk at liberty, [.linebr]#/# +
for I seek your precepts.

|
|46 I will also speak of your testimonies before kings [.linebr]#/# +
and will not be ashamed.

|
|47 And I will delight myself in your commandments, [.linebr]#/# +
which I have loved.

|
|48 I will also lift my hands to your commandments, which I have loved. [.linebr]#/# +
And I will meditate in your statutes.
|===

+[+ _ZAYIN_ - ז +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|49 Remember the word to your servant, [.linebr]#/# +
upon which you have caused me to hope.

|
|50 This is my comfort in my affliction, [.linebr]#/# +
for your word has revived me.

|
|51 The proud have had me greatly in derision, [.linebr]#/# +
yet I have not declined from your law.

|
|52 I remembered your judgments of old, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and have comforted myself.

|
|53 Horror has taken hold upon me [.linebr]#/# +
because of the wicked who forsake your law.

|
|54 Your statutes have been my songs [.linebr]#/# +
in the house of my pilgrimage.

|
|55 I have remembered your name, O LORD, in the night [.linebr]#/# +
and have kept your law.

|
|56 This I had [.linebr]#/# +
because I kept your precepts.
|===

+[+ _HET_ - ח +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|57 You are my portion, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
I have said that I would keep your words.

|
|58 I entreated your favor with my whole heart. [.linebr]#/# +
Be merciful to me according to your word.

|
|59 I considered my ways [.linebr]#/# +
and turned my feet to your testimonies.

|
|60 I made haste and did not delay [.linebr]#/# +
to keep your commandments.

|
|61 The ropes of the wicked have surrounded me, [.linebr]#/# +
but I have not forgotten your law.

|
|62 At midnight I will rise to give thanks to you [.linebr]#/# +
because of your righteous judgments.

|
|63 I am a companion of all those who fear [.linebr]#/# +
you and of those who keep your precepts.

|
|64 The earth, O LORD, is full of your mercy. [.linebr]#/# +
Teach me your statutes.
|===

+[+ _TET_ - ט +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|65 You have dealt well with your servant, [.linebr]#/# +
O LORD, according to your word.

|
|66 Teach me good judgment and knowledge, [.linebr]#/# +
for I have believed your commandments.

|
|67 Before I was afflicted I went astray, [.linebr]#/# +
but now I have kept your word.

|
|68 You are good and do good. [.linebr]#/# +
Teach me your statutes.

|
|69 The proud have forged a lie against me, [.linebr]#/# +
but I will keep your precepts with my whole heart.

|
|70 Their heart is as gross as fat, [.linebr]#/# +
but I delight in your law.

|
|71 It is good for me that I have been afflicted [.linebr]#/# +
so that I might learn your statutes.

|
|72 The law of your mouth is better to me [.linebr]#/# +
than thousands of gold and silver.
|===

+[+ _YOD_ - י +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|73 Your hands have made me and fashioned me. [.linebr]#/# +
Give me understanding so that I may learn your commandments.

|
|74 Those who fear you will be glad when they see me [.linebr]#/# +
because I have hoped in your word.

|
|75 I know, O LORD, that your judgments are right [.linebr]#/# +
and that you in faithfulness have afflicted me.

|
|76 Let, I pray you, your merciful kindness be for my comfort, [.linebr]#/# +
according to your word to your servant.

|
|77 Let your tender mercies come to me so that I may live, [.linebr]#/# +
for your law is my delight.

|
|78 Let the proud be ashamed, for they dealt perversely with me without a cause. [.linebr]#/# +
But I will meditate in your precepts.

|
|79 Let those who fear you turn to me, [.linebr]#/# +
and those who have known your testimonies.

|
|80 Let my heart be sound in your statutes [.linebr]#/# +
so that I may not be ashamed.
|===

+[+ _KAF_ - כ +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|81 My soul faints for your salvation, [.linebr]#/# +
but I hope in your word.

|
|82 My eyes fail for your word, [.linebr]#/# +
saying, "When will you comfort me?"

|
|83 For I have become like a bottle in the smoke, [.linebr]#/# +
yet I do not forget your statutes.

|
|84 How many are the days of your servant? [.linebr]#/# +
When will you execute judgment on those who persecute me?

|
|85 The proud have dug pits for me, [.linebr]#/# +
which are not according to your law.

|
|86 All your commandments are faithful. [.linebr]#/# +
They persecute me wrongfully. Help me.

|
|87 They had almost consumed me upon earth, [.linebr]#/# +
but I did not forsake your precepts.

|
|88 Revive me after your loving-kindness, [.linebr]#/# +
and I shall keep the testimony of your mouth.
|===

+[+ _LAMED_ - ל +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|89 Forever, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
your word is settled in heaven.

|
|90 Your faithfulness is to all generations. [.linebr]#/# +
You have established the earth, and it abides.

|
|91 They continue this day according to your ordinances, [.linebr]#/# +
for all are your servants.

|
|92 Unless your law had been my delight, [.linebr]#/# +
I would have perished in my affliction.

|
|93 I will never forget your precepts, [.linebr]#/# +
for with them you have revived me.

|
|94 I am yours. Save me, [.linebr]#/# +
for I have sought your precepts.

|
|95 The wicked have waited for me to destroy me, [.linebr]#/# +
but I will consider your testimonies.

|
|96 I have seen an end of all perfection, [.linebr]#/# +
but your commandment is exceedingly broad.
|===

+[+ _MEM_ - מ +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|97 O how I love your law! [.linebr]#/# +
It is my meditation all the day.

|
|98 You, through your commandments, have made me wiser than my enemies, [.linebr]#/# +
for they are always with me.

|
|99 I have more understanding than all my teachers, [.linebr]#/# +
for your testimonies are my meditation.

|
|100 I understand more than the ancients [.linebr]#/# +
because I keep your precepts.

|
|101 I have refrained my feet from every evil way [.linebr]#/# +
so that I might keep your word.

|
|102 I have not departed from your judgments, [.linebr]#/# +
for you have taught me.

|
|103 How sweet your words are to my taste! [.linebr]#/# +
They are even sweeter than honey to my mouth!

|
|104 Through your precepts I get understanding; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, I hate every false way.
|===

+[+ _NUN_ - נ +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|105 Your word is a lamp to my feet [.linebr]#/# +
and a light to my path.

|
|106 I have sworn, and I will perform it, [.linebr]#/# +
that I will keep your righteous judgments.

|
|107 I am afflicted very much. [.linebr]#/# +
Revive me, O LORD, according to your word.

|
|108 Accept, I implore you, the voluntary-offerings of my mouth, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and teach me your judgments.

|
|109 My soul is continually in my hand, [.linebr]#/# +
yet I do not forget your law.

|
|110 The wicked have laid a snare for me, [.linebr]#/# +
yet I did not err from your precepts.

|
|111 I have taken your testimonies as a heritage forever, [.linebr]#/# +
for they are the rejoicing of my heart.

|
|112 I have inclined my heart to perform your statutes [.linebr]#/# +
always, even to the end.
|===

+[+ _SAMEKH_ - ס +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|113 I hate vain thoughts, [.linebr]#/# +
but I love your law.

|
|114 You are my hiding place and my shield. [.linebr]#/# +
I hope in your word.

|
|[[psa119-115]]115 Depart from me, you evil-doers, [.linebr]#/# +
for I will keep the commandments of my God.

|
|116 Uphold me according to your word so that I may live, [.linebr]#/# +
and do not let me be ashamed of my hope.

|
|117 Support me, and I shall be safe [.linebr]#/# +
and will have respect to your statutes continually.

|
|118 You have trodden down all those who err from your statutes, [.linebr]#/# +
for their deceit is falsehood.

|
|119 You put away all the wicked of the earth like dross; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, I love your testimonies.

|
|120 My flesh trembles for fear of you, [.linebr]#/# +
and I am afraid of your judgments.
|===

+[+ _AYIN_ - ע +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|121 I have done judgment and justice. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not leave me to my oppressors.

|
|122 Be surety for your servant for good. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not let the proud oppress me.

|
|123 My eyes fail for your salvation [.linebr]#/# +
and for the word of your righteousness.

|
|124 Deal with your servant according to your mercy [.linebr]#/# +
and teach me your statutes.

|
|125 I am your servant. Give me understanding [.linebr]#/# +
so that I may know your testimonies.

|
|126 It is time for you, LORD, to work, [.linebr]#/# +
for they have made your law void.

|
|127 Therefore, I love your commandments [.linebr]#/# +
above gold, even above fine gold.

|
|128 Therefore, I esteem all your precepts concerning all things to be right, [.linebr]#/# +
and I hate every false way.
|===

+[+ _PE_ - פ +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|129 Your testimonies are wonderful; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, my soul keeps them.

|
|130 The entrance of your words gives light. [.linebr]#/# +
It gives understanding to the simple.

|
|131 I opened my mouth and panted, [.linebr]#/# +
for I longed for your commandments.

|
|132 Look upon me and be merciful to me, [.linebr]#/# +
as you always do to those who love your name.

|
|133 Order my steps in your word [.linebr]#/# +
and do not let any iniquity have dominion over me.

|
|134 Deliver me from the oppression of man, [.linebr]#/# +
and I will keep your precepts.

|
|135 Make your face to shine upon your servant [.linebr]#/# +
and teach me your statutes.

|
|136 Rivers of waters run down my eyes [.linebr]#/# +
because they do not keep your law.
|===

+[+ _TSADI_ - צ +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|137 You are righteous, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and your judgments are upright.

|
|138 Your testimonies that you have commanded are righteous [.linebr]#/# +
and very faithful.

|
|139 My zeal has consumed me [.linebr]#/# +
because my enemies have forgotten your words.

|
|140 Your word is very pure; [.linebr]#/# +
therefore, your servant loves it.

|
|141 I am small and despised, [.linebr]#/# +
yet I do not forget your precepts.

|
|142 Your righteousness is an everlasting righteousness, [.linebr]#/# +
and your law is the truth.

|
|143 Trouble and anguish have taken hold of me, [.linebr]#/# +
yet your commandments are my delights.

|
|144 The righteousness of your testimonies is everlasting. [.linebr]#/# +
Give me understanding, and I shall live.
|===

+[+ _QOF_ - ק +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|145 I cried with my whole heart. Hear me, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
I will keep your statutes.

|
|146 I cried to you. Save me, [.linebr]#/# +
and I shall keep your testimonies.

|
|147 I came before the dawning of the morning and cried. [.linebr]#/# +
I hoped in your word.

|
|148 My eyes anticipated the night watches [.linebr]#/# +
so that I might meditate in your word.

|
|149 Hear my voice according to your loving-kindness. [.linebr]#/# +
O LORD, revive me according to your judgment.

|
|150 They draw near who follow after mischief. [.linebr]#/# +
They are far from your law.

|
|151 You are near, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and all your commandments are truth.

|
|152 Concerning your testimonies, I have known of old [.linebr]#/# +
that you have founded them forever.
|===

+[+ _RESH_ - ר +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|154 Consider my affliction and deliver me, [.linebr]#/# +
for I do not forget your law.

|
|154 Plead my cause and deliver me. [.linebr]#/# +
Revive me according to your word.

|
|155 Salvation is far from the wicked, [.linebr]#/# +
for they do not seek your statutes.

|
|156 Your tender mercies are great, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Revive me according to your judgments.

|
|157 Many are my persecutors and my enemies, [.linebr]#/# +
yet I do not decline from your testimonies.

|
|158 I beheld the transgressors and was grieved [.linebr]#/# +
because they did not keep your word.

|
|159 Consider how I love your precepts. [.linebr]#/# +
Revive me, O LORD, according to your loving-kindness.

|
|160 Your word is true from the beginning. [.linebr]#/# +
Every one of your righteous judgments endures forever.
|===

+[+ _SHIN_ - ש +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|161 Princes have persecuted me without a cause, [.linebr]#/# +
but my heart stands in awe of your word.

|
|162 I rejoice at your word [.linebr]#/# +
as one who finds great plunder.

|
|163 I hate and abhor lying, [.linebr]#/# +
but I love your law.

|
|164 Seven times a day I praise you [.linebr]#/# +
because of your righteous judgments.

|
|165 Those who love your law have great peace, [.linebr]#/# +
and nothing shall cause them to stumble.

|
|166 LORD, I have hoped for your salvation [.linebr]#/# +
and performed your commandments.

|
|167 My soul has kept your testimonies, [.linebr]#/# +
and I love them exceedingly.

|
|168 I have kept your precepts and your testimonies, [.linebr]#/# +
for all my ways are before you.
|===

+[+ _TAV_ - ת +]+

[cols="7%,93%",grid=none,frame=none]
|===
|
|169 Let my cry come near before you, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Give me understanding according to your word.

|
|170 Let my supplication come before you. [.linebr]#/# +
Deliver me according to your word.

|
|171 My lips shall utter praise [.linebr]#/# +
when you have taught me your statutes.

|
|172 My tongue shall speak of your word, [.linebr]#/# +
for all your commandments are righteousness.

|
|173 Let your hand help me, [.linebr]#/# +
for I have chosen your precepts.

|
|174 I have longed for your salvation, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and your law is my delight.

|
|175 Let my soul live, and it shall praise you. [.linebr]#/# +
Let your judgments help me.

|
|176 I have gone astray like a lost sheep. Seek your servant, [.linebr]#/# +
for I do not forget your commandments.
|===
