[#psa120%breakable]
=== Psalm 120

[.outline.text-center]
_David prays against Doeg, 1, 2; reproves his tongue, 3, 4; deplores the necessity of his residence with the ungodly, 5-7._

1 [_A Song of Degrees._]

In my distress I cried to the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and he heard me.

2 Deliver my soul, O LORD, from lying lips [.linebr]#/# +
and from a deceitful tongue.

3 What shall be given to you? [.linebr]#/# +
Or what shall be done to you, [.linebr]#/# +
you false tongue?

4 Sharp arrows of the mighty [.linebr]#/# +
with coals of juniper.

5 Woe is me that I sojourn in Mesech, [.linebr]#/# +
that I dwell in the tents of Kedar!

6 My soul has long dwelt [.linebr]#/# +
with him who hates peace.

7 I am for peace, [.linebr]#/# +
but when I speak, they are for war.

[#psa121%breakable]
=== Psalm 121

[.outline.text-center]
_The great safety of the godly who put their trust in God's protection, 1-8._

1 [_A Song of Degrees._]

I will lift up my eyes to the hills. [.linebr]#/# +
From where does my help come?

2 My help comes from the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
who made heaven and earth.

3 He will not allow your foot to be moved. [.linebr]#/# +
He who keeps you will not slumber.

4 Behold, he who keeps Israel [.linebr]#/# +
shall neither slumber nor sleep.

5 The LORD is your keeper. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD is your shade upon your right hand.

6 The sun shall not smite you by day, [.linebr]#/# +
nor the moon by night.

7 The LORD will preserve you from all evil. [.linebr]#/# +
He will preserve your soul.

8 The LORD will preserve your going out and your coming in [.linebr]#/# +
from this time forth and even forever.

[#psa122%breakable]
=== Psalm 122

[.outline.text-center]
_David professes his joy for the church, 1-5; and prays for the peace thereof, 6-9._

1 [_A Song of Degrees of David._]

I was glad when they said to me, [.linebr]#/# +
"Let us go into the house of the LORD."

2 Our feet shall stand [.linebr]#/# +
within your gates, O Jerusalem.

3 Jerusalem is built as a city [.linebr]#/# +
that is compact together,

4 Where the tribes go up, the tribes of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
to the testimony of Israel [.linebr]#/# +
to give thanks to the name of the LORD.

5 For there thrones for judgment are set, [.linebr]#/# +
the thrones of the house of David.

6 Pray for the peace of Jerusalem. [.linebr]#/# +
They shall prosper who love you.

7 May peace be within your walls [.linebr]#/# +
and prosperity within your palaces.

8 For the sake of my brothers and my companions, [.linebr]#/# +
I will now say, "May peace be within you."

9 Because of the house of the LORD our God, [.linebr]#/# +
I will seek your good.

[#psa123%breakable]
=== Psalm 123

[.outline.text-center]
_The godly profess their confidence in God, 1, 2; and pray to be delivered from contempt, 3, 4._

1 [_A Song of Degrees._]

I raise my eyes to you, [.linebr]#/# +
O you who dwell in the heavens.

2 Behold, as the eyes of servants [.linebr]#/# +
look to the hand of their masters, [.linebr]#/# +
and as the eyes of a woman-servant [.linebr]#/# +
to the hand of her mistress, [.linebr]#/# +
so our eyes wait upon the LORD our God [.linebr]#/# +
until he has mercy upon us.

3 Have mercy upon us, O LORD, have mercy upon us, [.linebr]#/# +
for we are exceedingly filled with contempt.

4 Our soul is exceedingly filled [.linebr]#/# +
with the scorning of those who are at ease [.linebr]#/# +
and with the contempt of the proud.

[#psa124%breakable]
=== Psalm 124

[.outline.text-center]
_The church blesses God for a miraculous deliverance, 1-8._

1 [_A Song of Degrees of David._]

If it had not been the LORD who was on our side— [.linebr]#/# +
now may Israel say—

2 If it had not been the LORD who was on our side [.linebr]#/# +
when men rose up against us,

3 Then they would have swallowed us up alive [.linebr]#/# +
when their wrath was kindled against us;

4 Then the waters would have overwhelmed us, [.linebr]#/# +
the stream would have gone over our soul;

5 Then the proud waters would have gone over our soul.

6 Blessed be the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
who has not given us as a prey to their teeth.

7 Our soul has escaped like a bird out of the snare of the fowlers. [.linebr]#/# +
The snare is broken, and we have escaped.

8 Our help is in the name of the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
who made heaven and earth.

[#psa125%breakable]
=== Psalm 125

[.outline.text-center]
_The safety of those who trust in God, 1-3. A prayer for the godly and against the wicked, 4, 5._

1 [_A Song of Degrees._]

Those who trust in the LORD shall be like mount Zion, [.linebr]#/# +
which cannot be moved, but abides forever.

2 As the mountains are around Jerusalem, [.linebr]#/# +
so the LORD is around his people [.linebr]#/# +
from now on even forever.

3 For the rod of the wicked shall not rest [.linebr]#/# +
upon the lot of the righteous, [.linebr]#/# +
lest the righteous put forth their hands to iniquity.

4 Do good, O LORD, to those who are good [.linebr]#/# +
and to those who are upright in their hearts.

5 As for those who turn aside to their crooked ways, [.linebr]#/# +
the LORD shall lead them forth with the workers of iniquity, [.linebr]#/# +
but peace shall be upon Israel.

[#psa126%breakable]
=== Psalm 126

[.outline.text-center]
_The church, celebrating her incredible return out of captivity, 1-3, prays for and prophesies the good success thereof, 4-6._

1 [_A Song of Degrees._]

When the LORD turned back the captivity of Zion, [.linebr]#/# +
we were like those who dream.

2 Then our mouth was filled with laughter [.linebr]#/# +
and our tongue with singing. [.linebr]#/# +
Then they said among the heathen, [.linebr]#/# +
"The LORD has done great things for them."

3 The LORD has done great things for us, [.linebr]#/# +
of which we are glad.

4 Turn back our captivity, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
like the streams in the south.

5 Those who sow in tears shall reap in joy.

6 He who goes forth and weeps, [.linebr]#/# +
bearing precious seed, [.linebr]#/# +
shall doubtless return with rejoicing, [.linebr]#/# +
bringing his sheaves with him.

[#psa127%breakable]
=== Psalm 127

[.outline.text-center]
_The virtue of God's blessing, 1, 2. Good children are his gift, 3-5._

1 [_A Song of Degrees for Solomon._]

Unless the LORD builds the house, [.linebr]#/# +
they labor in vain who build it. [.linebr]#/# +
Unless the LORD keeps the city, [.linebr]#/# +
the watchman wakes in vain.

2 It is vain for you to rise early, [.linebr]#/# +
to sit up late, [.linebr]#/# +
to eat the bread of sorrows, [.linebr]#/# +
for he gives his beloved sleep.

3 Behold, children are a heritage of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and the fruit of the womb is his reward.

4 As arrows are in the hand of a mighty man, [.linebr]#/# +
so are children of the youth.

5 Happy is the man who has his quiver full of them. [.linebr]#/# +
They shall not be ashamed, [.linebr]#/# +
but they shall speak with the enemies in the gate.

[#psa128%breakable]
=== Psalm 128

[.outline.text-center]
_The various blessings which follow those who fear God, 1-6._

1 [_A Song of Degrees._]

Blessed is everyone who fears the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
who walks in his ways.

2 For you shall eat the labor of your hands. [.linebr]#/# +
You shall be happy, and it shall be well with you.

3 Your wife shall be as a fruitful vine [.linebr]#/# +
by the sides of your house, [.linebr]#/# +
your children like olive plants [.linebr]#/# +
around your table.

4 Behold, thus the man who fears the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
shall be blessed.

5 The LORD shall bless you out of Zion, [.linebr]#/# +
and you shall see the good of Jerusalem [.linebr]#/# +
all the days of your life.

6 Indeed, you shall see your children's children [.linebr]#/# +
and peace upon Israel.

[#psa129%breakable]
=== Psalm 129

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to praise God for saving Israel in their great afflictions, 1-4. The haters of the church are cursed, 5-8._

1 [_A Song of Degrees._]

Many a time they have afflicted me from my youth— [.linebr]#/# +
may Israel now say—

2 Many a time they have afflicted me from my youth, [.linebr]#/# +
yet they have not prevailed against me.

3 The plowers plowed upon my back. [.linebr]#/# +
They made their furrows long.

4 The LORD is righteous. [.linebr]#/# +
He has cut apart the cords of the wicked.

5 Let them all be confounded and turned back [.linebr]#/# +
who hate Zion.

6 Let them be like the grass upon the house-tops, [.linebr]#/# +
which withers before it grows up,

7 With which the reaper does not fill his hand, [.linebr]#/# +
nor he who binds sheaves, his bosom;

8 Neither do those who go by, say, [.linebr]#/# +
"May the blessing of the LORD be upon you. [.linebr]#/# +
We bless you in the name of the LORD."

[#psa130%breakable]
=== Psalm 130

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist professes his hope in prayer, 1-4; and his patience in hope, 5, 6. He exhorts Israel to trust in God, 7, 8._

1 [_A Song of Degrees._]

Out of the depths I have cried to you, O LORD.

2 Lord, hear my voice. [.linebr]#/# +
Let your ears be attentive [.linebr]#/# +
to the voice of my supplications.

3 If you, LORD, should mark iniquities, [.linebr]#/# +
O Lord, who shall stand?

4 But there is forgiveness with you [.linebr]#/# +
so that you may be feared.

5 I wait for the LORD. My soul waits, [.linebr]#/# +
and I hope in his word.

6 My soul waits for the Lord [.linebr]#/# +
more than those who watch for the morning, [.linebr]#/# +
even more than those who watch for the morning.

7 Let Israel hope in the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
for with the LORD there is mercy [.linebr]#/# +
and with him is plenteous redemption.

8 And he shall redeem Israel [.linebr]#/# +
from all his iniquities.

[#psa131%breakable]
=== Psalm 131

[.outline.text-center]
_David, professing his humility, 1, 2, exhorts Israel to trust in God, 3._

1 [_A Song of Degrees of David._]

LORD, my heart is not haughty, and my eyes are not lofty, [.linebr]#/# +
neither do I exercise myself in great matters [.linebr]#/# +
or in things too high for me.

2 Surely I have behaved and quieted myself [.linebr]#/# +
like a child who is weaned by his mother. [.linebr]#/# +
My soul is even like a weaned child.

3 Let Israel hope in the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
from now on and forever.

[#psa132%breakable]
=== Psalm 132

[.outline.text-center]
_In his prayer, David commends to God the religious care he had for the ark. 1-7. His prayer at the moving of the ark, 8-10; with a repetition of God's promises, 11-18._

1 [_A Song of Degrees._]

LORD, remember David [.linebr]#/# +
and all his afflictions,

2 How he swore to the LORD [.linebr]#/# +
and vowed to the mighty God of Jacob:

3 "Surely I will not come into the tabernacle of my house [.linebr]#/# +
or go up into my bed,

4 I will not give sleep to my eyes [.linebr]#/# +
or slumber to my eyelids,

5 Until I find a place for the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
a habitation for the mighty God of Jacob."

6 Behold, we heard of it at Ephratah. [.linebr]#/# +
We found it in the fields of Jaar.

7 We will go into his tabernacles. [.linebr]#/# +
We will worship at his footstool.

8 Arise, O LORD, into your rest— [.linebr]#/# +
you and the ark of your strength.

9 Let your priests be clothed with righteousness, [.linebr]#/# +
and let your saints shout for joy.

10 For your servant David's sake, [.linebr]#/# +
do not turn away the face of your anointed.

11 The LORD has sworn in truth to David [.linebr]#/# +
and he will not turn from it: [.linebr]#/# +
"The fruit of your body I will set upon your throne.

12 If your children will keep my covenant [.linebr]#/# +
and my testimony that I shall teach them, [.linebr]#/# +
their children shall also sit upon your throne forever."

13 For the LORD has chosen Zion. [.linebr]#/# +
He has desired it for his habitation.

14 "This is my rest forever. [.linebr]#/# +
Here I will dwell, for I have desired it.

15 I will abundantly bless her provision. [.linebr]#/# +
I will satisfy her poor with bread.

16 I will also clothe her priests with salvation, [.linebr]#/# +
and her saints shall shout aloud for joy.

17 There I will make the horn of David to bud. [.linebr]#/# +
I have ordained a lamp for my anointed.

18 His enemies I will clothe with shame, [.linebr]#/# +
but upon himself his crown shall flourish."

[#psa133%breakable]
=== Psalm 133

[.outline.text-center]
_The blessedness of unity among brothers, 1-3._

1 [_A Song of Degrees of David._]

Behold, how good and how pleasant it is [.linebr]#/# +
for brothers to dwell together in unity!

2 It is like the precious ointment upon the head [.linebr]#/# +
that ran down upon the beard, [.linebr]#/# +
even Aaron's beard, [.linebr]#/# +
that went down to the skirts of his garment.

3 It is like the dew of Hermon [.linebr]#/# +
and like the dew that descended upon the mountains of Zion. [.linebr]#/# +
For there the LORD commanded the blessing, [.linebr]#/# +
even life forever.

[#psa134%breakable]
=== Psalm 134

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to bless God, 1-3._

1 [_A Song of Degrees._]

Behold, bless the LORD, all servants of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
who by night stand in the house of the LORD.

2 Lift up your hands in the sanctuary [.linebr]#/# +
and bless the LORD.

3 May the LORD who made heaven and earth [.linebr]#/# +
bless you out of Zion.

[#psa135%breakable]
=== Psalm 135

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to praise God for his mercy, 1-4; for his power, 5-7; for his judgments, 8-14. The vanity of idols, 15-18. An exhortation to bless God, 19-21._

1 Praise the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the name of the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise him, O servants of the LORD.

2 You who stand in the house of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
in the courts of the house of our God,

3 Praise the LORD, for the LORD is good. [.linebr]#/# +
Sing praises to his name, for it is pleasant.

4 For the LORD has chosen Jacob for himself, [.linebr]#/# +
Israel for his peculiar treasure.

5 For I know that the LORD is great [.linebr]#/# +
and that our Lord is above all gods.

6 Whatever the LORD pleased, he did [.linebr]#/# +
in heaven and in earth, [.linebr]#/# +
in the seas and all deep places.

7 He causes the vapors to ascend [.linebr]#/# +
from the ends of the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
He makes lightnings for the rain. [.linebr]#/# +
He brings the wind out of his treasuries.

8 He smote the first-born of Egypt, [.linebr]#/# +
both of man and beast.

9 He sent tokens and wonders [.linebr]#/# +
into the midst of you, O Egypt, [.linebr]#/# +
upon Pharaoh and upon all his servants.

10 He smote great nations [.linebr]#/# +
and slew mighty kings:

11 Sihon king of the Amorites, [.linebr]#/# +
Og king of Bashan, [.linebr]#/# +
and all the kingdoms of Canaan.

12 He gave their land for a heritage, [.linebr]#/# +
a heritage to Israel his people.

13 Your name, O LORD, endures forever, [.linebr]#/# +
and your memorial, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
throughout all generations.

14 For the LORD will judge his people [.linebr]#/# +
and have compassion on his servants.

15 The idols of the heathen are silver and gold, [.linebr]#/# +
the work of men's hands.

16 They have mouths, but they do not speak. [.linebr]#/# +
They have eyes, but they do not see.

17 They have ears, but they do not hear, [.linebr]#/# +
neither is there any breath in their mouths.

18 Those who make them are like them, [.linebr]#/# +
and so is everyone who trusts in them.

19 Bless the LORD, O house of Israel. [.linebr]#/# +
Bless the LORD, O house of Aaron.

20 Bless the LORD, O house of Levi. [.linebr]#/# +
You who fear the LORD, bless the LORD.

21 Blessed be the LORD out of Zion, [.linebr]#/# +
who dwells at Jerusalem. Praise the LORD.

[#psa136%breakable]
=== Psalm 136

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to give thanks to God for particular mercies, 1-26._

1 O give thanks to the LORD, for he is good— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

2 O give thanks to the God of gods—
[.silver]#/# +for his mercy endures forever—

3 O give thanks to the Lord of lords— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

4 To him who alone does great wonders— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

5 To him who by wisdom made the heavens— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

6 To him who stretched out the earth above the waters— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

7 To him who made great lights— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

8 The sun to rule by day— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

9 The moon and stars to rule by night— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

10 To him who smote Egypt in their first-born— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

11 And brought out Israel from among them— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

12 With a strong hand and with an out-stretched arm— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

13 To him who divided the Red Sea into parts— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

14 And made Israel to pass through its midst— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

15 But overthrew Pharaoh and his army in the Red Sea— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

16 To him who led his people through the wilderness— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

17 To him who smote great kings— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

18 And slew famous kings— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

19 Sihon king of the Amorites— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

20 And Og king of Bashan— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

21 And gave their land for a heritage— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

22 Even a heritage to Israel his servant— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

23 Who remembered us in our low estate— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

24 And has redeemed us from our enemies— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

25 Who gives food to all flesh— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever—

26 O give thanks to the God of heaven— [.linebr]#/# +
for his mercy endures forever.

[#psa137%breakable]
=== Psalm 137

[.outline.text-center]
_The constancy of the Jews in captivity, 1-6. The prophet curses Edom and Babel, 7-9._

1 By the rivers of Babylon [.linebr]#/# +
we sat down. We even wept [.linebr]#/# +
when we remembered Zion.

2 We hung our harps [.linebr]#/# +
upon the willows in its midst.

3 For there those who carried us away captive [.linebr]#/# +
required of us a song, [.linebr]#/# +
and those who wasted us [.linebr]#/# +
required of us mirth, saying, [.linebr]#/# +
"Sing us one of the songs of Zion."

4 How shall we sing the LORD'S song [.linebr]#/# +
in a foreign land?

5 If I forget you, O Jerusalem, [.linebr]#/# +
let my right hand forget her skill.

6 If I do not remember you, [.linebr]#/# +
let my tongue cleave to the roof of my mouth, [.linebr]#/# +
if I do not prefer Jerusalem above my chief joy.

7 Remember, O LORD, the children of Edom [.linebr]#/# +
in the day of Jerusalem, [.linebr]#/# +
who said, "Raze it, raze it, [.linebr]#/# +
even to its foundation."

8 O daughter of Babylon, who is to be destroyed, [.linebr]#/# +
happy shall he be who rewards you [.linebr]#/# +
as you have served us.

9 Happy shall he be who takes and dashes your little ones [.linebr]#/# +
against the stones.

[#psa138%breakable]
=== Psalm 138

[.outline.text-center]
_David praises God for the truth of his word, 1-3. He prophesies that the kings of the earth shall praise God, 4-6. He professes his confidence in God, 7, 8._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

I will praise you with my whole heart. [.linebr]#/# +
Before the gods I will sing praise to you.

2 I will worship toward your holy temple [.linebr]#/# +
and praise your name [.linebr]#/# +
for your loving-kindness and for your truth, [.linebr]#/# +
for you have magnified your word [.linebr]#/# +
above all your name.

3 In the day when I cried you answered me [.linebr]#/# +
and strengthened me with strength in my soul.

4 All the kings of the earth shall praise you, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
when they hear the words of your mouth.

5 Indeed, they shall sing in the ways of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
for the glory of the LORD is great.

6 Though the LORD is high, [.linebr]#/# +
yet he has respect to the lowly. [.linebr]#/# +
But the proud he knows afar off.

7 Though I walk in the midst of trouble, [.linebr]#/# +
you will revive me. [.linebr]#/# +
You will stretch forth your hand [.linebr]#/# +
against the wrath of my enemies, [.linebr]#/# +
and your right hand will save me.

8 The LORD will perfect that which concerns me. [.linebr]#/# +
Your mercy, O LORD, endures forever. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not forsake the works of your own hands.

[#psa139%breakable]
=== Psalm 139

[.outline.text-center]
_David praises God for his all-seeing providence, 1-16; and for his infinite mercies, 17, 18. He defies the wicked, 19-22. He prays for sincerity, 23, 24._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

O LORD, you have searched me and known me.

2 You know my sitting down and my rising up. [.linebr]#/# +
You understand my thought afar off.

3 You compass my path and my lying down [.linebr]#/# +
and are acquainted with all my ways.

4 For there is not a word on my tongue, [.linebr]#/# +
but behold, O LORD, you know it altogether.

5 You have beset me behind and before [.linebr]#/# +
and laid your hand upon me.

6 Such knowledge is too wonderful for me. [.linebr]#/# +
It is high. I cannot attain to it.

7 Where shall I go from your Spirit? [.linebr]#/# +
Or where shall I flee from your presence?

8 If I ascend into heaven, you are there. [.linebr]#/# +
If I make my bed in hell, behold, you are there.

9 If I take the wings of the morning [.linebr]#/# +
and dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea,

10 Even there your hand shall lead me [.linebr]#/# +
and your right hand shall hold me.

11 If I say, "Surely the darkness shall cover me, [.linebr]#/# +
even the night shall be light around me,"

12 Even the darkness does not hide from you, [.linebr]#/# +
but the night shines like the day. [.linebr]#/# +
The darkness and the light are both alike to you.

13 For you have possessed my inmost being. [.linebr]#/# +
You have covered me in my mother's womb.

14 I will praise you, for I am fearfully and wonderfully made. [.linebr]#/# +
Your works are wonderful, [.linebr]#/# +
and that my soul knows well.

15 My substance was not hid from you [.linebr]#/# +
when I was made in secret [.linebr]#/# +
and skillfully formed in the lowest parts of the earth.

16 Your eyes saw my substance, being without form. [.linebr]#/# +
And in your book they were all written, [.linebr]#/# +
even the days that were ordained for me, [.linebr]#/# +
when as yet there were none of them.

17 How precious your thoughts are to me, O God! [.linebr]#/# +
How great the sum of them is!

18 If I should count them, [.linebr]#/# +
they are more in number than the sand. [.linebr]#/# +
When I awake, I am still with you.

19 Surely you will slay the wicked, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
Depart from me therefore, you bloody men.

20 For they speak against you wickedly, [.linebr]#/# +
and your enemies take your name in vain.

21 Do I, O LORD, not hate those who hate you? [.linebr]#/# +
And am I not grieved with those who rise up against you?

22 I hate them with perfect hatred. [.linebr]#/# +
I count them my enemies.

23 Search me, O God, and know my heart. [.linebr]#/# +
Try me and know my thoughts.

24 See if there is any wicked way in me [.linebr]#/# +
and lead me in the everlasting way.

[#psa140%breakable]
=== Psalm 140

[.outline.text-center]
_David prays to be delivered from Saul and Doeg, 1-7. He prays against them, 8-11. He comforts himself by confidence in God, 12, 13._

1 [_To the Chief Musician. A Psalm of David._]

Deliver me, O LORD, from the evil men. [.linebr]#/# +
Preserve me from the violent men

2 Who devise mischiefs in their heart. [.linebr]#/# +
Continually they are assembled for war.

[[psa140-003]]3 They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent. [.linebr]#/# +
Adder's poison is under their lips. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

4 Keep me, O LORD, from the hands of the wicked. [.linebr]#/# +
Preserve me from the violent men [.linebr]#/# +
who have purposed to overthrow my goings.

5 The proud have hid a snare for me, and also cords. [.linebr]#/# +
They have spread a net by the wayside. [.linebr]#/# +
They have set traps for me. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

6 I said to the LORD, "You are my God." [.linebr]#/# +
Hear the voice of my supplications, O LORD.

7 O GOD the Lord, the strength of my salvation, [.linebr]#/# +
you have covered my head in the day of battle.

8 Do not grant, O LORD, the desires of the wicked. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not further his wicked device, [.linebr]#/# +
lest they exalt themselves. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

9 As for the head of those who encompass me, [.linebr]#/# +
let the mischief of their own lips cover them.

10 Let burning coals fall upon them. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them be cast into the fire, [.linebr]#/# +
into deep pits, so that they do not rise again.

11 Do not let an evil speaker be established on the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
Evil shall hunt the violent man to overthrow him.

12 I know that the LORD will maintain [.linebr]#/# +
the cause of the afflicted [.linebr]#/# +
and the right of the poor.

13 Surely the righteous shall give thanks to your name. [.linebr]#/# +
The upright shall dwell in your presence.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.3]*: Quoted in xref:#rom003-013[Romans 3:13].

[#psa141%breakable]
=== Psalm 141

[.outline.text-center]
_David prays that his appeal may be acceptable, 1, 2; his conscience sincere, 3-6; and his life free from snares, 7-10._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

LORD, I cry to you. Make haste to me. [.linebr]#/# +
Give ear to my voice when I cry to you.

2 Let my prayer be set forth before you as incense, [.linebr]#/# +
and the lifting up of my hands as the evening sacrifice.

3 Set a watch, O LORD, before my mouth. [.linebr]#/# +
Keep the door of my lips.

4 Do not incline my heart to any evil thing [.linebr]#/# +
or to practice wicked works [.linebr]#/# +
with men who work iniquity. [.linebr]#/# +
And do not let me eat their dainties.

5 Let the righteous smite me—it shall be a kindness. [.linebr]#/# +
And let him reprove me—it shall be an excellent oil, [.linebr]#/# +
which shall not break my head. [.linebr]#/# +
For still my prayer shall also be against their wickedness.

6 When their judges are overthrown in stony places, [.linebr]#/# +
they shall hear my words, for they are sweet.

7 As when one plows and cleaves the earth, [.linebr]#/# +
so our bones are scattered at the grave's mouth

8 But my eyes are to you, O GOD the Lord. [.linebr]#/# +
My trust is in you. Do not leave my soul destitute.

9 Keep me from the snare which they have laid for me [.linebr]#/# +
and the traps of the workers of iniquity.

10 Let the wicked fall into their own nets [.linebr]#/# +
while I escape.

[#psa142%breakable]
=== Psalm 142

[.outline.text-center]
_David shows that in his trouble all his comfort was in prayer to God, 1-7._

1 [_Maschil of David: a prayer when he was in the cave._]

I cried to the LORD with my voice. [.linebr]#/# +
With my voice to the LORD I made my supplication.

2 I poured out my complaint before him. [.linebr]#/# +
I uttered before him my trouble.

3 When my spirit was overwhelmed within me, [.linebr]#/# +
you knew my path. [.linebr]#/# +
In the way in which I walked [.linebr]#/# +
they have secretly laid a snare for me.

4 I looked on my right hand and beheld, [.linebr]#/# +
but there was no man who would know me. [.linebr]#/# +
Refuge failed me. [.linebr]#/# +
No man cared for my soul.

5 I cried to you, O LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
I said, "You are my refuge [.linebr]#/# +
and my portion in the land of the living."

6 Attend to my cry, [.linebr]#/# +
for I am brought very low. [.linebr]#/# +
Deliver me from my persecutors, [.linebr]#/# +
for they are stronger than I am.

7 Bring my soul out of prison [.linebr]#/# +
so that I may praise your name. [.linebr]#/# +
The righteous shall encompass me, [.linebr]#/# +
for you will deal bountifully with me.

[#psa143%breakable]
=== Psalm 143

[.outline.text-center]
_David prays for favor in judgment, 1, 2. He bemoans his griefs, 3, 4. He strengthens his faith by meditation and prayer, 5, 6. He prays for grace, 7, 8; for deliverance, 9; for sanctification, 10, 11; for destruction of his enemies, 12._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

Hear my prayer, O LORD. Give ear to my supplications. [.linebr]#/# +
Answer me in your faithfulness and in your righteousness.

2 And do not enter into judgment with your servant, [.linebr]#/# +
for in your sight no living man is righteous.

3 For the enemy has persecuted my soul. [.linebr]#/# +
He has smitten my life down to the ground. [.linebr]#/# +
He has made me to dwell in darkness [.linebr]#/# +
like those who have been long dead.

4 Therefore, my spirit is overwhelmed within me. [.linebr]#/# +
My heart within me is desolate.

5 I remember the days of old. [.linebr]#/# +
I meditate on all your works. [.linebr]#/# +
I muse on the work of your hands.

6 I stretch forth my hands to you. [.linebr]#/# +
My soul thirsts after you like a thirsty land. [.linebr]#/# +
+[+ _Selah._ +]+

7 Hear me speedily, O LORD. My spirit fails. [.linebr]#/# +
Do not hide your face from me, [.linebr]#/# +
lest I be like those who go down into the pit.

8 Cause me to hear your loving-kindness in the morning, [.linebr]#/# +
for I trust in you. [.linebr]#/# +
Cause me to know the way in which I should walk, [.linebr]#/# +
for I lift up my soul to you.

9 Deliver me, O LORD, from my enemies. [.linebr]#/# +
I flee to you to hide me.

10 Teach me to do your will, [.linebr]#/# +
for you are my God. [.linebr]#/# +
Your Spirit is good. [.linebr]#/# +
Lead me into the land of uprightness.

11 Revive me, O LORD, for your name's sake. [.linebr]#/# +
For your righteousness' sake bring my soul out of trouble.

12 And in your mercy cut off my enemies [.linebr]#/# +
and destroy all those who afflict my soul, [.linebr]#/# +
for I am your servant.

[#psa144%breakable]
=== Psalm 144

[.outline.text-center]
_David blesses God for his mercy, both to him and to man, 1-4. He prays that God would powerfully deliver him from his enemies, 5-8. He promises to praise God, 9, 10. He prays for the happy state of the kingdom, 11-15._

1 [_A Psalm of David._]

Blessed be the LORD my strength [.linebr]#/# +
who teaches my hands to war [.linebr]#/# +
and my fingers to fight;

2 My goodness, my fortress, [.linebr]#/# +
my high tower, and my deliverer; [.linebr]#/# +
my shield, and he in whom I trust, [.linebr]#/# +
who subdues my people under me.

3 LORD, what is man that you take knowledge of him, [.linebr]#/# +
or the son of man that you make account of him?

4 Man is like vanity. [.linebr]#/# +
His days are like a shadow that passes away.

5 Bow your heavens, O LORD, and come down. [.linebr]#/# +
Touch the mountains, and they shall smoke.

6 Cast forth lightning and scatter them. [.linebr]#/# +
Shoot your arrows and destroy them.

7 Send your hand from above. [.linebr]#/# +
Rid me and deliver me from the great waters, [.linebr]#/# +
from the hand of strange children,

8 Whose mouth speaks vanity [.linebr]#/# +
and their right hand is a right hand of falsehood.

9 I will sing a new song to you, O God. [.linebr]#/# +
Upon a psaltery and an instrument of ten strings [.linebr]#/# +
I will sing praises to you.

10 It is he who gives salvation to kings, [.linebr]#/# +
who delivers David his servant [.linebr]#/# +
from the hurtful sword.

11 Rid me and deliver me [.linebr]#/# +
from the hand of strange children, [.linebr]#/# +
whose mouth speaks vanity [.linebr]#/# +
and their right hand is a right hand of falsehood,

12 So that our sons may be like plants [.linebr]#/# +
grown up in their youth; [.linebr]#/# +
so that our daughters may be like corner stones, [.linebr]#/# +
polished after the similitude of a palace;

13 So that our granaries may be full, [.linebr]#/# +
affording all manner of store; [.linebr]#/# +
so that our sheep may bring forth thousands [.linebr]#/# +
and ten thousands in our streets;

14 So that our oxen may be strong to labor; [.linebr]#/# +
so that there is no breaking in nor going out; [.linebr]#/# +
and so that there is no complaining in our streets.

15 Happy are the people who are in such a case. [.linebr]#/# +
Indeed, happy are the people whose God is the LORD.

[#psa145%breakable]
=== Psalm 145

[.outline.text-center]
_David praises God for his fame, 1-7; for his goodness, 8-10; for his kingdom, 11-13; for his providence, 14-16; for his justice, holiness, and saving mercy, 17-21._

1 [_David's Psalm of Praise._]

I will extol you, my God, O king, [.linebr]#/# +
and I will bless your name forever and ever.

2 Every day I will bless you [.linebr]#/# +
and will praise your name forever and ever.

3 The LORD is great and greatly to be praised, [.linebr]#/# +
and his greatness is unsearchable.

4 One generation shall praise your works to another [.linebr]#/# +
and declare your mighty acts.

5 I will speak of the glorious honor of your majesty [.linebr]#/# +
and of your wondrous works.

6 And men shall speak of the might of your awesome acts. [.linebr]#/# +
And I will declare your greatness.

7 They shall abundantly utter the memory of your great goodness [.linebr]#/# +
and sing of your righteousness.

8 The LORD is gracious and full of compassion, [.linebr]#/# +
slow to anger and of great mercy.

9 The LORD is good to all, [.linebr]#/# +
and his tender mercies are over all his works.

10 All your works shall praise you, O LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
and your saints shall bless you.

11 They shall speak of the glory of your kingdom [.linebr]#/# +
and talk of your power,

12 To make known to the sons of men his mighty acts [.linebr]#/# +
and the glorious majesty of his kingdom.

13 Your kingdom is an everlasting kingdom, [.linebr]#/# +
and your dominion endures throughout all generations.

14 The LORD upholds all who fall [.linebr]#/# +
and raises up all those who are bowed down.

15 The eyes of all wait upon you, [.linebr]#/# +
and you give them their food in due season.

16 You open your hand [.linebr]#/# +
and satisfy the desire of every living creature.

17 The LORD is righteous in all his ways [.linebr]#/# +
and holy in all his works.

18 The LORD is near to all those who call upon him, [.linebr]#/# +
to all who call upon him in truth.

19 He will fulfill the desire of those who fear him. [.linebr]#/# +
He also will hear their cry and save them.

20 The LORD preserves all those who love him, [.linebr]#/# +
but all the wicked he will destroy.

21 My mouth shall speak the praise of the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
And let all flesh bless his holy name forever and ever.

[#psa146%breakable]
=== Psalm 146

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist vows perpetual praises to God, 1, 2. He exhorts not to trust in man, 3, 4. God, for his power, justice, mercy, and kingdom, is only worthy to be trusted, 5-10._

1 Praise the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD, O my soul.

2 While I live I will praise the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
I will sing praises to my God while I have any being.

3 Do not put your trust in princes, [.linebr]#/# +
nor in a son of man, in whom there is no help.

4 His breath goes forth and he returns to the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
In that very day his thoughts perish.

5 Happy is he who has the God of Jacob for his help, [.linebr]#/# +
whose hope is in the LORD his God,

[[psa146-006]]6 Who made heaven, earth, [.linebr]#/# +
the sea, and all that is in them, [.linebr]#/# +
who keeps truth forever,

7 Who executes judgment for the oppressed, [.linebr]#/# +
who gives food to the hungry. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD sets the prisoners free.

8 The LORD opens the eyes of the blind. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD raises those who are bowed down. [.linebr]#/# +
The LORD loves the righteous.

9 The LORD preserves the strangers. [.linebr]#/# +
He relieves the fatherless and widow, [.linebr]#/# +
but the way of the wicked he turns upside down.

10 The LORD will reign forever, [.linebr]#/# +
even your God, O Zion, to all generations. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD.

[%breakable]
References::
*[v.6]*: Quoted in xref:#act004-024[Acts 4:24].

[#psa147%breakable]
=== Psalm 147

[.outline.text-center]
_The prophet exhorts to praise God for his care of the church, 1-3; his power and wisdom, 4, 5; his mercy, 6; his providence, 7-11; to praise him for his blessings upon the kingdom, 12-14; for his power over the elements, 15-18; and for his ordinances in the church, 19, 20._

1 Praise the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
for it is good to sing praises to our God. [.linebr]#/# +
For it is pleasant, and praise is fitting.

2 The LORD builds up Jerusalem. [.linebr]#/# +
He gathers together the outcasts of Israel.

3 He heals the broken in heart [.linebr]#/# +
and binds up their wounds.

4 He tells the number of the stars. [.linebr]#/# +
He calls them all by their names.

5 Our Lord is great and of great power. [.linebr]#/# +
His understanding is infinite.

6 The LORD lifts up the meek. [.linebr]#/# +
He casts the wicked down to the ground.

7 Sing to the LORD with thanksgiving. [.linebr]#/# +
Sing praise upon the harp to our God,

8 Who covers the heaven with clouds, [.linebr]#/# +
who prepares rain for the earth, [.linebr]#/# +
who makes grass to grow upon the mountains.

9 He gives to the beast his food, [.linebr]#/# +
and to the young ravens which cry.

10 He does not delight in the strength of the horse. [.linebr]#/# +
He does not take pleasure in the legs of a man.

11 The LORD takes pleasure in those who fear him, [.linebr]#/# +
in those who hope in his mercy.

12 Praise the LORD, O Jerusalem. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise your God, O Zion.

13 For he has strengthened the bars of your gates. [.linebr]#/# +
He has blessed your children within you.

14 He makes peace in your borders [.linebr]#/# +
and fills you with the finest of the wheat.

15 He sends forth his commandment upon the earth. [.linebr]#/# +
His word runs very swiftly.

16 He gives snow like wool. [.linebr]#/# +
He scatters the hoar-frost like ashes.

17 He casts forth his ice like morsels. [.linebr]#/# +
Who can stand before his cold?

18 He sends out his word and melts them. [.linebr]#/# +
He causes his wind to blow, and the waters flow.

19 He shows his word to Jacob, [.linebr]#/# +
his statutes and his judgments to Israel.

20 He has not dealt so with any nation. [.linebr]#/# +
And as for his judgments, they have not known them. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD.

[#psa148%breakable]
=== Psalm 148

[.outline.text-center]
_The psalmist exhorts the celestial, 1-6, the terrestrial, 7-10, and the rational creatures to praise God, 11-14._

1 Praise the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD from the heavens. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise him in the heights.

2 Praise him, all his angels. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise him, all his hosts.

3 Praise him, sun and moon. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise him, all you stars of light.

4 Praise him, you heavens of heavens [.linebr]#/# +
and you waters that are above the heavens.

5 Let them praise the name of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
for he commanded and they were created.

6 He has also established them forever and ever. [.linebr]#/# +
He has made a decree which shall not pass away.

7 Praise the LORD from the earth, [.linebr]#/# +
you sea-creatures and all deeps,

8 Fire and hail, snow and vapors, [.linebr]#/# +
stormy wind fulfilling his word,

9 Mountains and all hills, [.linebr]#/# +
fruitful trees and all cedars,

10 Beasts and all livestock, [.linebr]#/# +
creeping animals and flying birds,

11 Kings of the earth and all people, [.linebr]#/# +
princes and all judges of the earth,

12 Both young men and virgins, [.linebr]#/# +
old men and children.

13 Let them praise the name of the LORD, [.linebr]#/# +
for his name alone is excellent. [.linebr]#/# +
His glory is above the earth and heaven.

14 He also exalts the horn of his people, [.linebr]#/# +
the praise of all his saints, [.linebr]#/# +
even of the children of Israel, a people near to him. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD.

[#psa149%breakable]
=== Psalm 149

[.outline.text-center]
_The prophet exhorts to praise God for his love to the church, 1-4; and for that power which he has given to the church, 3-9._

1 Praise the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Sing to the LORD a new song, [.linebr]#/# +
and his praise in the congregation of saints.

2 Let Israel rejoice in him who made them. [.linebr]#/# +
Let the children of Zion be joyful in their King.

3 Let them praise his name in the dance. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them sing praises to him with the tambourine and harp.

4 For the LORD takes pleasure in his people. [.linebr]#/# +
He will beautify the meek with salvation.

5 Let the saints be joyful in glory. [.linebr]#/# +
Let them sing aloud upon their beds.

6 Let the high praises of God be in their mouth [.linebr]#/# +
and a two-edged sword in their hand,

7 To execute vengeance upon the heathen [.linebr]#/# +
and punishments upon the people,

8 To bind their kings with chains [.linebr]#/# +
and their nobles with fetters of iron,

9 To execute upon them the judgment written. [.linebr]#/# +
All his saints have this honor. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD.

[#psa150%breakable]
=== Psalm 150

[.outline.text-center]
_An exhortation to praise God, 1, 2; with all kinds of instruments, 3-6._

1 Praise the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise God in his sanctuary. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise him in the firmament of his power.

2 Praise him for his mighty acts. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise him according to his excellent greatness.

3 Praise him with the sound of the trumpet. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise him with the psaltery and harp.

4 Praise him with the timbrel and dance. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise him with stringed instruments and pipes.

5 Praise him upon the loud cymbals. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise him upon the high sounding cymbals.

6 Let everything that has breath [.linebr]#/# +
praise the LORD. [.linebr]#/# +
Praise the LORD.
